 2. nirālambanavāda (NAV)

 4. anumānapariccheda (AMP)

 6. upamānapariccheda (UMP)

 8. abhāvapariccheda (ABH)
 9. citrākṣepavāda (CAV)

 13. apohavāda (APV)

VII. vākyādhikaraṇa (VAA)
VIII.vedapauruṣeyatādhikaraṇa (VPA)

* pratijñāsūtra (PJS)
||
PJS1ab viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe
PJS1cd śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||
PJS2ab abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn
PJS2cd tatprasādāt kariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||
PJS3ab tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ
PJS3cd santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hy anasūyavaḥ ||
PJS4ab na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ
PJS4cd doṣo hy avidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||
PJS5ab kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu
PJS5cd neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||
PJS6ab nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate
PJS6cd sāpavādā yataḥ ke cin mokṣasvargāv api prati ||
PJS7ab āgamapravaṇaś cāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣv apy apodyate
PJS7cd na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣv apy apodyate ||
PJS8ab yathā kathañ cid ārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī
PJS8cd vāgvṛttir alpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||
PJS9ab mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhir viśeṣeṇoj jvalīkṛte
PJS9cd vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||
PJS10ab prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā
PJS10cd tāmāstikapathe kartum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||
PJS11ab athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtram ādyam idaṃ kṛtam
PJS11cd dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||
PJS12ab sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit
PJS12cd yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate ||
PJS13ab mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā
PJS13cd na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||
PJS14ab vidyāntareṣu nāpy etad yady abhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam
PJS14cd anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvat tebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||
PJS15ab mīmāṃsāyāṃ tv ihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ
PJS15cd nyāyamārge mahān doṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||
PJS16ab tasmāt prayojanaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam
PJS16cd yat svenoktaṃ vadeyus tad bhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||
PJS17ab siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate
PJS17cd śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||
PJS18ab śāstrṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāv ubhau
PJS18cd taduktyantargatas tasmād bhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||
PJS19ab siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanād yataḥ
PJS19cd tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate ||
PJS20ab yāvat prayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate
PJS20cd asambaddhapralāpitvād bhavet tāvad asaṃgatiḥ ||
PJS21ab iha tv ākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate
PJS21cd dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmān nānyo 'bhidhīyate ||
PJS22ab na cāpy atrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate
PJS22cd sambandhaṃ kriyayor hy eṣa brūte śāstrāc ca te pṛthak ||
PJS23ab yo 'py ayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiś cid āditaḥ
PJS23cd kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||
PJS24ab sadasadbhāvayos tasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate
PJS24cd śrotuvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||
PJS25ab tasmād vyākhyāṅgam icchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ
PJS25cd śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyas tu niṣphalaḥ ||
PJS26ab loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate
PJS26cd bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||
PJS27ab sarvavyākhyām upālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare
PJS27cd parisaṃkhyās tutī kecithaśabdasya dūṣaṇam || 
PJS28ab sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā
PJS28cd viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tv iyam ucyate ||
PJS29ab pravṛttis tu padeṣv eva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā
PJS29cd vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||
PJS30ab adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt
PJS30cd tenaiṣām iti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye saty api grahaḥ ||
PJS31ab evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam
PJS31cd prasiddhatvād avācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam ||
PJS32ab vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate
PJS32cd svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||
PJS33ab vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñ cil laukikārthavyatikramaḥ
PJS33cd śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣam upālambho 'yam ucyate ||
PJS34ab athāta ity ayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate
PJS34cd tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣādibhir bhavet ||
PJS35ab prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā
PJS35cd na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||
PJS36ab sūtrārthe kliśyataś caivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ
PJS36cd tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||
PJS37ab na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ
PJS37cd yat tasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||
PJS38ab prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣv anena kim
PJS38cd phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||
PJS39ab codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt
PJS39cd padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
PJS40ab evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate
PJS40cd padacchedadādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatis tv iyam ||
PJS41ab brabīty eva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate
PJS41cd nanv aśaktam idaṃ sūtraṃ samyak sūtritam ity api ||
PJS42ab sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate
PJS42cd na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||
PJS43ab nānyato vedavidbhyaś ca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate
PJS43cd pratyākhyānasya hetuś ca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||
PJS44ab yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvān nivārayet
PJS44cd vākyārthe tatra sandehād vyākhyānaṃ cet pravartate ||
PJS45ab sūtreṣv api samānatvāt pratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate
PJS45cd na vyākhyātavyam ityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||
PJS46ab duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate
PJS46cd asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvāt phalgutvāc cāpi parvayoḥ ||
PJS47ab madhyame cātidaurjanyāt parisaṃkhyaiva yujyate
PJS47cd vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||
PJS48ab yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredam upadiśyate
PJS48cd adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||
PJS49ab neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te
PJS49cd yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||
PJS50ab tadarthanirṇaye hetur jaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ
PJS50cd vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāt tathā padatadarthayoḥ ||
PJS51ab adhyāhārādibhir muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate
PJS51cd asambhavād avaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||
PJS52ab anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate
PJS52cd prāthamyenāvaruddhatvād upāyavaśato 'tha vā ||
PJS53ab yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām
PJS53cd tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ity ayam ||
PJS54ab vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptam anūdyate
PJS54cd śeṣabhājāṃ bhavel lopa ity adhyāhārakalpanā ||
PJS55ab viprakarṣāt paśoś ceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate
PJS55cd padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamād iti ||
PJS56ab sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam
PJS56cd paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtram evānyathā kṛtam || 
PJS57ab agnayaś ca svakālatvād deyadharmāpayātanam
PJS57cd vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpās tv amī kṛtāḥ ||
PJS58ab autpattikas tu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhor iti
PJS58cd darśanāc ca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ity api ||
PJS59ab sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate
PJS59cd prasiddhair abhidhānād dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||
PJS60ab bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmād ekavākyatā
PJS60cd vedādhyayanavākyād vā tenāthety asya dūṣaṇam ||
PJS61ab prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrair vedārthanirṇayaḥ
PJS61cd na ca so 'sty athaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||
PJS62ab prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tac ca nāstīti dūṣaṇam
PJS62cd prasiddho 'py athaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||
PJS63ab pradarśanārtham ity eke, ke cin nānārthavācinaḥ
PJS63cd samudāyād avacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||
PJS64ab śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat
PJS64cd na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||
PJS65ab yad vākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvād asambhavāt
PJS65cd yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||
PJS66ab sa nāsty atrāthaśabdasyety adhyāhārādikalpanam
PJS66cd vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||
PJS67ab nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate
PJS67cd anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhir bādhyate dhruvam ||
PJS68ab tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kim api gamyate
PJS68cd viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānād viśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||
PJS69ab sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitad ity abravīt paraḥ
PJS69cd ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||
PJS70ab vedādhyayanam ākṣiptaṃ kim asūtritacodanā
PJS70cd yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||
PJS71ab tadānantaryam uktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārtham avakalpate
PJS71cd kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamād yasya kasya cit ||
PJS72ab kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam
PJS72cd saṅkalpādibhir apy eṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||
PJS73ab sādhāraṇyāt tu te 'py atra nopadeśyāḥ kathañ cana
PJS73cd tasmād dharmabubhutsāyām asādhāraṇakāraṇam ||
PJS74ab nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tac ca nākhyayanād ṛte
PJS74cd anyasyāpīty anenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||
PJS75ab prāg apīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpy anyasya sambhavāt
PJS75cd pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tv ity anena kim ||
PJS76ab vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā
PJS76cd na tāvat sādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||
PJS77ab iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ
PJS77cd dharmamātrābhidhānād dhi buddhādivacanāny api ||
PJS78ab paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsety anyasyāpīti codanā
PJS78cd yad vā bhavatu nāmedṛk sūtraṃ vedam adhītya tu ||
PJS79ab jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryety atrāpi dvayam īpsitam
PJS79cd nānadhītya na cāpy anyat kṛtvety etan na labhyate ||
PJS80ab vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyor vākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ
PJS80cd adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāder apy anantarā ||
PJS81ab bhaved dharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhis tadā
PJS81cd ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||
PJS82ab ity evam anuvādatvāt prāg apy eṣā prasajyate
PJS82cd buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tv ity apākriyā ||
PJS83ab prāg apīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyād vedalābhataḥ
PJS83cd naivaitayor vacobhaṅgyor eko 'py artho vidhīyate ||
PJS84ab api cetyādikenoktam, kin tv ityetad vidhīyate
PJS84cd ānantaryaṃ parastāc ca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||
PJS85ab ke cid adhyāharanti, asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ
PJS85cd na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate || 
PJS86ab sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā
PJS86cd ānantaryavacovyaktir āśritaivātra lakṣyate ||
PJS87ab śrutārthaṃ tv aparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate
PJS87cd pratītā dharmajijñāsā vedādhyāyād anantarā ||
PJS88ab tatkālasyāvaruddhatvāt snānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet
PJS88cd virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||
PJS89ab snānasya tena bādhaḥ syād dharmajijñāsayā balāt
PJS89cd dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tv iti ||
PJS90ab punaruktyā gatārthatvāt tyaktaṃ kaiś cit, tad ucyate
PJS90cd yady apy asya bhaved vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam ||
PJS91ab tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayed avirodhataḥ
PJS91cd granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||
PJS92ab adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tv avirodhitā
PJS92cd yas tv evamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||
PJS93ab adṣṭāyātha vāpy anyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram
PJS93cd ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||
PJS94ab avidhitvam anāśritya so 'vasānam apekṣate
PJS94cd tato 'pekṣāvaśāt snānam asnānādinivartanam ||
PJS95ab virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet
PJS95cd tasmād adhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||
PJS96ab dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānām evaṃ vyākhyeyam āśritā
PJS96cd snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||
PJS97ab tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram
PJS97cd yathaivādhyayanāt snānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||
PJS98ab tathā tataḥ paro 'py anyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ paras tataḥ
PJS98cd tataś cāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||
PJS99ab yogyatvād āgate kāle prāthamyāt snānabādhanam
PJS99cd so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthād bādha ity avagamyate ||
PJS100ab guṇapradhānayor vāpi virodhād guṇabādhanam
PJS100cd snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttir guruveśmanaḥ ||
PJS101ab virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam
PJS101cd tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||
PJS102ab jijñāsetāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate
PJS102cd gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvac ca na samāpyate ||
PJS103ab tāvat sakalavācitvān na snānaṃ paryavasyati
PJS103cd gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||
PJS104ab tatparatvavidhānāc ca na tāvad dārasaṅgrahaḥ
PJS104cd vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyād iti punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||
PJS105ab smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛter yady apy anantaram
PJS105cd viparītārtham ity asmāt tadvākyād apanīyate ||
PJS106ab athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastād upavarṇitaḥ
PJS106cd tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvāt pradarśitaḥ ||
PJS107ab smṛtiprāptam idānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam
PJS107cd pratiṣedhann adṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||
PJS108ab nivṛttya gurugehāc ca jijñāsārthaḥ punar bhavet
PJS108cd praveśaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||
PJS109ab nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ
PJS109cd smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syād akṛtārthasya nirgame ||
PJS110ab athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā
PJS110cd ānantaryopadeśitvād ataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||
PJS111ab yogyatvam athaśabdena yady api pratipāditam
PJS111cd tad eva hetur atreti nātaḥśabdād vinā bhavet ||
PJS112ab lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā tad dhi prasajyate
PJS112cd jijñāsāyāś ca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||
PJS113ab ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanam āśritam
PJS113cd hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādy apy asau vadet ||
PJS114ab snānabādhasya vā hetur ata ity ucyate punaḥ
PJS114cd yogyasyādhītavedatvān nāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate || 
PJS115ab sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā
PJS115cd jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||
PJS116ab iṣes tu karma bāhyaḥ syād dharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam
PJS116cd samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||
PJS117ab evaṃ viṣayanānātvān na kā cit punaruktatā
PJS117cd sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||
PJS118ab prakṛtyā vikṛtir yasmāc caturthyantā samasyate
PJS118cd tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminn asamāsatā ||
PJS119ab sa hi tasyety anenokto dharmasyety eṣa vigrahaḥ
PJS119cd dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||
PJS120ab prāpnoty atra caturthy eva viśeṣaś ced vivakṣitaḥ
PJS120cd sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||
PJS121ab sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu
PJS121cd viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
PJS122ab sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā
PJS122cd anyasādhanam anyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||
PJS123ab kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca krator iti
PJS123cd śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaś ca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||
PJS124ab prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāt tu neṣyate
PJS124cd aprasiddhas tv aśakyatvānnatarām ity ato 'bravīt ||
PJS125ab jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayād dharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca
PJS125cd asandigdho hy ajijñāsyo yo vā syān niṣprayojanaḥ ||
PJS126ab svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate
PJS126cd pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||
PJS127ab sthite vedapramāṇatve punar vākyārthanirṇaye
PJS127cd matir bahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayān nopajāyate ||
PJS128ab ke cid āhur asāv arthaḥ, ke cin nāsāv ayaṃ tv iti
PJS128cd tannirṇayārtham apy etat paraṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

* codanāsūtra (CDS)

CDS1ab dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate
CDS1cd svarūpādes tataḥ siddhaḥ, svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||
CDS2ab dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate
CDS2cd svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||
CDS3ab kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau
CDS3cd tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||
CDS4ab codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam
CDS4cd sākāṅkṣam iti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||
CDS5ab sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣv api
CDS5cd indriyāder asāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||
CDS6ab atyantāsaty api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi
CDS6cd tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvāt pramāṇatā ||
CDS7ab codanety abravīc cātra śabdamātravivakṣayā
CDS7cd na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaś cid asti vidhāyakaḥ ||
CDS8ab indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvan na sādhyate
CDS8cd tāvac ca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||
CDS9ab nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam
CDS9cd pramāṇaṃ tv api śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate ||
CDS10ab padārthas tanmatir vā syād vākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā
CDS10cd pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||
CDS11ab jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate
CDS11cd codanoktis tadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||
CDS12ab nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ
CDS12cd sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāc codanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||
CDS13ab dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate
CDS13cd teṣām aindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||
CDS14ab śreyaḥsādhanatā hy eṣāṃ nityaṃ vedāt pratīyate 
CDS14cd tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmān nendriyagocaraḥ ||
CDS15ab pradarśanārtham atroktam indriyaṃ sūtrakāravat
CDS15cd nānyat kiñ ceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||
CDS16ab tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punar indriyakīrtanam
CDS16cd kiñ ceti madhyam acchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||
CDS17ab yady api tv anumānasyāpy evamādau samarthatā
CDS17cd vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit ||
CDS18ab na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam
CDS18cd liṅgasya kasya cit siddhaṃ yena syād anumānatā ||
CDS19ab nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate
CDS19cd padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||
CDS20ab vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, padārthānāṃ ca hetutā
CDS20cd sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||
CDS21ab nityatvāder asiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā
CDS21cd sutarām apramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||
CDS22ab pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayet sadā
CDS22cd smṛtivac ca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||
CDS23ab nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā
CDS23cd buddhiḥ sākṣād adṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||
CDS24ab nātmīyād anyadīyād vā pratyakṣāder vinā kva cit
CDS24cd vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāc codanāsv api ||
CDS25ab tena saty api vijñāne pratijñāder yathaiva hi
CDS25cd svātantryān na pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||
CDS26ab svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā
CDS26cd pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||
CDS27ab yad vāptenāpraṇītatvād bālonmattādivākyavat
CDS27cd vyomādivac ca nityatvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||
CDS28ab yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ
CDS28cd svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syur vākyatvāt puruṣoktivat ||
CDS29ab prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām
CDS29cd śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvād apramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi ||
CDS30ab na syād vaktṛguṇānāṃ ced vacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā
CDS30cd taddoṣair apramāṇatvaṃ kim ity asya bhaviṣyati ||
CDS31ab evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare
CDS31cd prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanv ity etadacūcudat ||
CDS32ab tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate
CDS32cd tato 'pi pratyayotpattes tasmāj jātyuttaraṃ tv idam ||
CDS33ab sarvavijñānaviṣayam idaṃ tāvat parīkṣyatām
CDS33cd pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||
CDS34ab svato 'satām asādhyatvāt ke cid āhur dvayaṃ svataḥ
CDS34cd apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||
CDS35ab svatas tāvad dvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca
CDS35cd niḥsvabhāvatvam evaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate ||
CDS36ab kathaṃ hy anyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ
CDS36cd kimātmakaṃ bhavet tac ca svabhāvadvayavarjitam ||
CDS37ab vijñānavyaktibhedena bhavec ced aviruddhatā
CDS37cd tathāpy anyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||
CDS38ab tasmāt svābhāvikaṃ teṣām apramāṇatvam iṣyatām
CDS38cd prāmāṇyañ ca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||
CDS39ab aprāmāṇyam avastutvān na syāt kāraṇadoṣataḥ
CDS39cd vastutvāt tu guṇais teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam upajanyate ||
CDS40ab prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāt tadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ
CDS40cd tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||
CDS41ab matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvāt prāmāṇyaṃ nopajāyate
CDS41cd hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyaty avastunaḥ ||
CDS42ab indriyādiguṇāś cāsya kāraṇam, tadasad dvidhā
CDS42cd duṣṭatvād indriyādīnām abhāve 'nyatamasya vā ||
CDS43ab ata eva ca vo bhrāntir doṣair mithyātvadhīr iti 
CDS43cd tadvyāptes tu guṇābhāvas tatkṛtā hy apramāṇatā ||
CDS44ab tasmāt kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam
CDS44cd svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate ||
CDS45ab anvayavyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ
CDS45cd nājñāne dṛśyate hy etatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||
CDS46ab tataś ca puruṣābhāvāt sati vā śuddhyasambhavāt
CDS46cd nirmūlatvāt pramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||
CDS47ab svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām
CDS47cd na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ||
CDS48ab ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet
CDS48cd labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu ||
CDS49ab jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvan nārtho 'vadhāryate
CDS49cd yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarād bhavet ||
CDS50ab tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt
CDS50cd yāvad dhi na paricchinnā śuddhis tāvad asatsamā ||
CDS51ab tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syāt pramāṇatā
CDS51cd tasyāpy evam itīcchaś ca na kva cid vyavatiṣṭhate ||
CDS52ab yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyan naiva gṛhyate
CDS52cd nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānād ayatnataḥ ||
CDS53ab tasmād bodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā

CDS54ab aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ
CDS54cd vastutvād dvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||
CDS55ab avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate
CDS55cd kāraṇābhāvatas tv eva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||
CDS56ab doṣataś cāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām
CDS56cd guṇajñānānavasthāvan na doṣeṣu prasajyate ||

CDS57cd pūrvābādhena notpattir uttarasya hi sidhyati ||
CDS58ab duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare
CDS58cd arthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||
CDS59ab tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīr vā parā na cet
CDS59cd tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvād ādyamānatā ||
CDS60ab svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānāt pramāṇatā

CDS62cd tadabhāvaḥ kva cit tāvad guṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ ||
CDS63ab tadguṇair apakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt
CDS63cd yadā vaktur abhāvena na syur doṣā nirāśrayāḥ ||
CDS64ab pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇās tathā
CDS64cd prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syād ity udāhṛtam ||
CDS65ab tasmād guṇebhyo doṣāṇām abhāvas tadabhāvataḥ
CDS65cd aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||

CDS66cd doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaś cen nanu saivāsthitir bhavet ||
CDS67ab tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ
CDS67cd doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||
CDS68ab tatrāpavādanirmuktir vaktrabhāvāl laghīyasī
CDS68cd vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkām api gacchati ||
CDS69ab ato vaktranadhīnatvāt prāmāṇye tadupāsanam
CDS69cd na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||
CDS70ab tataś cāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate
CDS70cd prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||
CDS71ab pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā
CDS71cd tadabhāve hi tad duṣyeditaran na kadā cana ||
CDS72ab tenetaraiḥ pramāṇair yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ 
CDS72cd tayaiva syāt pramāṇatvam anuvādatvam anyathā ||
CDS73ab anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatir naiva kāraṇam
CDS73cd tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvād ekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||
CDS74ab yatrāpi syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇair uttaraiḥ punaḥ
CDS74cd nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtas tathā ||

CDS76ab kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā
CDS76cd prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||

CDS238ab vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ aduḥkhātmakatā tathā
CDS238cd na ca yā sampradānasya prītis tādṛk phalaṃ śrutam ||
CDS239ab dātus tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate
CDS239cd sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||
CDS240ab vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tv etadviruddhatā
CDS240cd prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||
CDS241ab dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, tasya kīdṛk phalaṃ bhavet
CDS241cd japahomādidṛṣṭāntāt parapīḍādivarjanāt ||
CDS242ab coditatvasya hetutvād viruddhāvyabhicāritā
CDS242cd vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyan na ca kāraṇam ||
CDS243ab dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ
CDS243cd anugrahāc ca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatām ||
CDS244ab vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet
CDS244cd krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||
CDS245ab bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hy upakāritā
CDS245cd anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||
CDS246ab hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmād dṛṣṭāṃ pīḍām apaśyataḥ 
CDS246cd pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ ||
CDS247ab anyonyāśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan
CDS247cd evamādāv aśāstrajño mleccho nodvijate kva cit ||
CDS248ab tasya nādharmayogaḥ syāt pūrvoktā yadi kalpanā
CDS248cd tasmād anugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvam apāsya ca ||
CDS249ab dharmādharmārthibhir nityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau
CDS249cd kva cid asyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||
CDS250ab pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati
CDS250cd śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
CDS251ab vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām
CDS251cd tad eva cedaṃ karmeti śāstram evānudhāvatā ||
CDS252ab hiṃsādīnām adharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ
CDS252cd evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhus tair apy etat parīkṣyatām ||
CDS253ab surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ
CDS253cd vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syād viprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||
CDS254ab pañcamyām iṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ
CDS254cd tasmād yady ādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||
CDS255ab śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tat phalam
CDS255cd hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||
CDS256ab pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate
CDS256cd jñānam eva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
CDS257ab jñāyante śāstratas tāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ
CDS257cd vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣv api karmasu ||
CDS258ab abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātur eṣv api
CDS258cd rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāder bhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||
CDS259ab tathāpy ekaphalatvaṃ cet kriyātvāt sarvasaṅkaraḥ
CDS259cd yajitvādyaviśeṣāc ca citrādiphalatulyatā ||
CDS260ab bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced ihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati
CDS260cd vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
CDS261ab puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate
CDS261cd na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhān na ca kalpyate ||
CDS262ab na ca prakaraṇasthatvāt puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet
CDS262cd karmopakāraḥ kalpyas tu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||
CDS263ab kalpanāvasaras tatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt
CDS263cd kratvarthaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ paśor nārādupakriyā ||
CDS264ab dṛṣṭaiva tv avadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā
CDS264cd abhicāre 'py upāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate ||
CDS265ab tasmād anaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyām etad ucyate
CDS265cd uddeśāc ca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||
CDS266ab bhāvanāvidhir apy eva phalāṃśād vinivartate
CDS266cd ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenāder nāpy adharmatā ||
CDS267ab phalānarthānubandhitvāt taddvāreṇopacaryate
CDS267cd nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||
CDS268ab tasmāt kriyāntarād eva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate
CDS268cd phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||
CDS269ab kevalaprītihetutvāt taddharmatvena hīṣyate
CDS269cd nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāder dharmatā bhavet ||
CDS270ab phalaṃ tāvad adharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate
CDS270cd yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syād anuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||
CDS271ab tasya dharmatvam ucyeta tatḥ śyenādivarjanam
CDS271cd yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||
CDS272ab dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāt tadā śyene 'pi dharmatā
CDS272cd yadi tv aprītihetur yaḥ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
CDS273ab so 'dharmaś codanārthaḥ syāt tadā śyene 'py adharmatā
CDS273cd yas tu hiṃsātvasādharmyād bāhyavaccodanāsv api ||
CDS274ab vaded anarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpy āgamabādhanam
CDS274cd tam anādṛtya yo brūyād yāgāder apy asau vadet ||
CDS275ab svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvād bhojanādivat 
CDS275cd gītāmantrārthavādair yā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||
CDS276ab pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvāt sānyārthatvena nīyate
CDS276cd śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt sūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||
CDS277ab aśakteś cobhayoḥ sāmyān na sūtreṣv ity anuttaram
CDS277cd prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate ||
CDS278ab sūtreṣu hy anayā yuktyā gatir eṣāpi yujyate
CDS278cd tasmād āvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||
CDS279ab ekadeśānumānād vā dve sūtre parikalpite
CDS279cd itaretarasāmīpyād etāv eva parasparam ||
CDS280ab kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā
CDS280cd viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvād atha vety api bhāṣite ||
CDS281ab vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvam uttaram
CDS281cd arthaṃ vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
CDS282ab tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ
CDS282cd dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||
CDS283ab vṛttam eva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate
CDS283cd codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||
CDS284ab labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hy anyathā bhavet
CDS284cd tathā ca ye 'py anarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||
CDS285ab niṣedhais te 'pi dharmāḥ syuś codanālakṣaṇatvataḥ
CDS285cd tasmād arthāparityāgād ekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||
CDS286ab labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syād arthānuvādataḥ
CDS286cd viśeṣaṇād vinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||
CDS287ab kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam

* nimittasūtra

NMS1ab pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yady api
NMS1cd vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||
NMS2ab pratijñāmātram ityetajjaiminer matam ucyate
NMS2cd vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāram abravīt ||

* pratyakṣasūtra

PAS1ab varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam
PAS1cd tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||
PAS2ab lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate
PAS2cd kimarthaṃ cānumānāder lakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||
PAS3ab na tāvad apramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpy akṣabuddhiṣu
PAS3cd śakyate 'ntargatir vaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||
PAS4ab na cāpi siddhir eṣāṃ syād arthāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇāt
PAS4cd na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇam iti niścitam ||
PAS5ab pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiś ca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt
PAS5cd vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||
PAS6ab tadetatpūrvakatve dhīr na ca tallakṣaṇād bhavet
PAS6cd tadukter vānumānādi kiṃ na syāt tadapūrvakam ||
PAS7ab na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yat tayor api
PAS7cd pratyakṣalakṣaṇād eṣāṃ kathañ cid avadhāraṇā ||
PAS8ab prasiddhatvād avācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate
PAS8cd tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||
PAS9ab na tv ekaṃ lakṣayed eṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañ cana
PAS9cd sambhavaty ekavākyatve vākyabhedaś ca neṣyate ||
PAS10ab na cāpy etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam
PAS10cd tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||
PAS11ab taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet
PAS11cd kena cit samprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syān niyogataḥ ||
PAS12ab grāhyeṇānyena vety etat kṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam 
PAS12cd samprayogasya yena syād viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||
PAS13ab asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe
PAS13cd tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||
PAS14ab tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāder yadutthitam
PAS14cd viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||
PAS15ab satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaś ced, etad eva hi
PAS15cd pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhir eva ca ||
PAS16ab svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttir vā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati
PAS16cd tasmād vidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||
PAS17ab tena naiṣā vacovyaktir yatsatīndriyasaṅgame
PAS17cd vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||
PAS18ab pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ
PAS18cd vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||
PAS19ab evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā
PAS19cd evaṃliṅgakam ityetad bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
PAS20ab yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam
PAS20cd tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animittatā ||
PAS21ab pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye
PAS21cd asmād ādau prasiddhatvād yogyartham abhidhīyate ||
PAS22ab prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt
PAS22cd tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiś ca sambandhāder anīkṣaṇāt ||
PAS23ab śakyam anyāpramāṇatvam iti sūtrair na paṭhyate
PAS23cd na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||
PAS24ab na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati
PAS24cd sarvathā lokasiddhatvād dharmo 'yaṃ tāvad iṣyate ||
PAS25ab tataś ca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate
PAS25cd animittaprasaṅgas tu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||
PAS26ab atītānāgate 'py arthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca
PAS26cd pratyakṣaṃ yoginām iṣṭaṃ kaiś cin muktātmanām api ||
PAS27ab vidyamānopalambhatvam asiddhaṃ tatra tān prati
PAS27cd bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyair vyabhicāritā ||
PAS28ab mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sad ity ayam
PAS28cd na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yoginām api ||
PAS29ab pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam
PAS29cd satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpy asmatpratyakṣavad bhavet ||
PAS30ab teṣām avartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ
PAS30cd pratyakṣaṃ sā tatas tv eva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||
PAS31ab loke cāpy aprasiddhatvāt pratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ
PAS31cd pratibhāvad dvayāsattvaṃ sad ity etena kathyate ||
PAS32ab laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī
PAS32cd na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syād yoginām api ||
PAS33ab avidyamānasaṃyogāt syāc cet pratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit
PAS33cd bhaviṣyaty api dharme syāc chaktety āha sad ity ayam ||
PAS34ab pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānān na dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā
PAS34cd phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāsty asau ||
PAS35ab asmatpratyakṣavac cāpi vidyamānopalambhanam
PAS35cd pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvāc ca neṣyate ||
PAS36ab avidyamānasaṃyogāt pratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ
PAS36cd yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||
PAS37ab saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ
PAS37cd pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||
PAS38ab samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ
PAS38cd prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||
PAS39ab duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt
PAS39cd evaṃ saty anuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||
PAS40ab tataś cāprāpyakāritvād yad bauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ
PAS40cd lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||
PAS41ab prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila 
PAS41cd adhiṣṭānādhikaś cārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||
PAS42ab vyāpāramātravācitvād aviruddhaṃ tad atra naḥ
PAS42cd yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||
PAS43ab yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ
PAS43cd sāṃkhyādīn vā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||
PAS44ab tayoś ca prāpyakāritvam indriyatvāt tvagādivat
PAS44cd ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāc ca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||
PAS45ab cikitsādiprayogaś ca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate
PAS45cd so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||
PAS46ab taddeśaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate
PAS46cd cakṣurādyupakāraś ca pādādāv api dṛśyate ||
PAS47ab tasmān naikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāt tatra vartanam
PAS47cd bahirvṛttis tayoś ceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||
PAS48ab adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam
PAS48cd pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||
PAS49ab dīpaprabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati
PAS49cd tathā bahirgatāpy eṣā mūlacchedād vinaśyati ||
PAS50ab adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu saty apy ucchinnayatnayā
PAS50cd tayārtho 'nupanītatvād ātmanā nānubhūyate ||
PAS51ab vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syād adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca
PAS51cd śabde tv ādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāv asambhavāt ||
PAS52ab puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau
PAS52cd puruṣo laukiko vā syād yo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||
PAS53ab vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate
PAS53cd buddhijanmeti cāpy āha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||
PAS54ab vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ
PAS54cd pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūd iti janma vivakṣyate ||
PAS55ab na hi tat kṣaṇam apy āste, jāyate vāpramātmakam
PAS55cd yenārthagrahaṇe paścād vyāpriyetendriyādivat ||
PAS56ab tena janmaiva viṣaye buddher vyāpāra iṣyate
PAS56cd tad eva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||
PAS57ab janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam
PAS57cd tac ca bhūtabhaviṣyattvāt kṛtaṃ buddher viśeṣaṇam ||
PAS58ab yadāpy aulūkyasiddhāntāt samavāyasya janmatā
PAS58cd buddhis tatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||
PAS59ab pramāṇaphalabhāvaś ca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām
PAS59cd sarvathāpy animittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||
PAS60ab yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt tasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ
PAS60cd manaso vendriyair yoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||
PAS61ab tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārāc ca pramāṇatā
PAS61cd vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||
PAS62ab na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate
PAS62cd yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāt tatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||
PAS63ab prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate
PAS63cd mā bhūt kāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||
PAS64ab yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvād indriyārthayoḥ
PAS64cd niyatā saṅgatir hetuḥ phale 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
PAS65ab yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ
PAS65cd vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpy akṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||
PAS66ab saṃyoge tv ātmamanasoḥ syāc ced viṣayabhinnatā
PAS66cd pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||
PAS67ab athāpy āśraya iṣṭas te na yogād viṣayāntaram
PAS67cd ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||
PAS68ab prakṛṣṭasādhanatvāc ca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ
PAS68cd karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā ||
PAS69ab pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate
PAS69cd pramāṇaṃ tv indriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
PAS70ab pramāṇaphalate buddhyor viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ 
PAS70cd yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||
PAS71ab viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam
PAS71cd prasūte niścayaṃ paścāt tasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||
PAS72ab niścayas tu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāv ālocite tadā
PAS72cd tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syād arthānavadhāraṇāt ||
PAS73ab hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ ced viśeṣyadhīḥ
PAS73cd upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaś cet, iyaṃ phalam ||

PAS74cd sādhyasādhanayor bhedo laukikas tena bādhitaḥ ||

PAS75cd tathaiva paraśor loke cchidayā saha naikatā ||

PAS76cd tattyāgena parebhyas tu bhedo rucim upāgataḥ ||

PAS78cd pramāṇatvaṃ bhavej jñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||
PAS79ab svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhān na yujyate
PAS79cd pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvān na yujyate ||

PAS81cd tasyāpy evaṃ tathā ca syān nākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||
PAS82ab na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate

PAS83ab manasas tv indriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu

PAS84cd sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||

PAS196cd bhaved gavādiśabdānāṃ sarvair vastu hi gamyate ||
PAS197ab na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam itīṣyate
PAS197cd na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syād anyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||
PAS198ab na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate
PAS198cd śabdārthayor yato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||
PAS199ab śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣv api dṛśyate
PAS199cd ekādhikaraṇās tena syus te nīlotpalādivat ||
PAS200ab na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padam arthe prayujyate
PAS200cd tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
PAS201ab tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ
PAS201cd na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||
PAS202ab tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā
PAS202cd śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||
PAS203ab mama vācyānabhijñatvān na bhavet smaraṇaṃ tataḥ
PAS203cd bhavatas tv artharūpasya vācakeṣv api darśanāt ||
PAS204ab yathā tv ajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīr na jāyate
PAS204cd tathaivājñātavācyānām upalabdhe 'pi vācake ||
PAS205ab tasmān nātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet
PAS205cd smārakatvāc ca teṣv eva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||
PAS206ab tena sambandhavelāyām arthātmā yo 'vasīyate
PAS206cd śabdād api sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
PAS207ab pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim
PAS207cd tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañ cit pratīyate ||
PAS208ab karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ
PAS208cd bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||
PAS209ab ātmādhyāsas tu sādṛśyād uparāgāc ca dṛśyate
PAS209cd na tāvad arthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||
PAS210ab na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate
PAS210cd dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||
PAS211ab śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptir ucyate
PAS211cd sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvair evānurañjanam ||
PAS212ab na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñ cid asty anurāgakṛt
PAS212cd na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīs tvagādibhiḥ ||
PAS213ab anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane
PAS213cd nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
PAS214ab tathās tv iti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati
PAS214cd katham evaṃ vaded artho nānṛtād dhi pratīyate ||
PAS215ab śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ 
PAS215cd pravṛttir na tu tat tantram artharūpaṃ kadā cana ||
PAS216ab tasmāt prāg api ye śabdād bhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ
PAS216cd gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||
PAS217ab śabdābhyupāyake 'py arthe tadabhāve ca yady api
PAS217cd arthabuddhir na jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
PAS218ab cakṣurāder abhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate
PAS218cd svarūpanāśo rūpādes tāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||
PAS219ab sambandhasya ca nityatvān nārethasya syād arūpatā
PAS219cd yugapanna hi sarveṣām anyākārārthavedanam ||
PAS220ab tadākāre 'pi tadvac ced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām
PAS220cd kiṃ nv arthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nv aśaktatā ||
PAS221ab sadasadbhāvayor arthe virodhitvād asambhavaḥ
PAS221cd grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvam aśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||
PAS222ab yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyety abhidhāsyate
PAS222cd tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||
PAS223ab devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt
PAS223cd arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpy anityatā ||
PAS224ab tatrāpy autpattikī śaktis tadrūpapratyayaṃ prati
PAS224cd grāhyagrāhakayor iṣṭā niyogasya tv anityatā ||
PAS225ab tatra sarvair atādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogāt pratīyate
PAS225cd teneṣṭam eva mithyātvaṃ kaiś cid adhyāsakalpane ||
PAS226ab yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdāt pratīyate
PAS226cd tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdas tatra yathārthatā ||
PAS227ab niyogāt parato vāpi śabdena vyajyatām iyam
PAS227cd tadgrāhyaśaktir arthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||
PAS228ab sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā
PAS228cd sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
PAS229ab tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā
PAS229cd buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānād upajāyate ||
PAS230ab cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣam asau bhavet
PAS230cd viviktā eva te 'py arthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||
PAS231ab smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣatā tayoḥ
PAS231cd tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tv arthasyāpi vāryate ||
PAS232ab gṛhītam api gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yady api
PAS232cd tathāpi vyatirekeṇ apūrvabodhāt pratīyate ||
PAS233ab vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāsty avasaro miteḥ
PAS233cd yaḥ pūrvāvagatoṃ 'śo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||
PAS234ab idānīn tanam astitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam
PAS234cd na hi smaraṇato yatprāk tat pratyakṣam itīdṛśam ||
PAS235ab vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate
PAS235cd na cāpi smaraṇāt paścād indriyasya pravartanam ||
PAS236ab vāryate kena cin nātastat tadānīṃ praduṣyati
PAS236cd tenendriyārthasambandhāt prāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||
PAS237ab vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iti gamyatām
PAS237cd vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api cendriyaiḥ ||
PAS238ab na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ
PAS238cd tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣv api ||
PAS239ab sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirnaṃ tāvatā
PAS239cd yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||
PAS240ab vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ
PAS240cd gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtās tu ye ||
PAS241ab tadajñānān na mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām
PAS241cd te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpy eṣaṃ viviktatām ||
PAS242ab yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvad gotvādivas tv api
PAS242cd saṅkīrṇam arthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsarvajitāḥ ||
PAS243ab vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ
PAS243cd yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||
PAS244ab sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyan na gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ 
PAS244cd tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||
PAS245ab tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt
PAS245cd tena yāvat pramātṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||
PAS246ab na syāt tāvad bhavet teṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam
PAS246cd tasmād yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||
PAS247ab pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane
PAS247cd pratyakṣatvam ataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||
PAS248ab sambandhasyeti tat pūrvam anumānādi jāyate
PAS248cd sarvaṃ cāpy anumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||
PAS249ab na pravartata ity etadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate
PAS249cd nanv evaṃ sati yāpy agner dūrād apy auṣṇyakalpanā ||
PAS250ab sāpi pratyakṣam eva syād yathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ
PAS250cd pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||
PAS251ab vijñānaṃ nānyad astīti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ
PAS251cd tatrāpy akṣair asambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||
PAS252ab yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate
PAS252cd sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||
PAS253ab tasmād yadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam
PAS253cd tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||
PAS254ab evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ
PAS254cd pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

* autpattikasūtra -- vṛttikāragrantha (VKG)

VKG1ab pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ
VKG1cd dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||
VKG2ab dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau
VKG2cd prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||
VKG3ab idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye
VKG3cd ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||
VKG4ab nirmūlāsambhavād atra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate
VKG4cd kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||
VKG5ab na caitāni parityajya pṛthag loke pramāṇatā
VKG5cd saṃsāramocakādeś ca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||
VKG6ab na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cid evaṃ vigānataḥ
VKG6cd mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||
VKG7ab na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstram anāśritam
VKG7cd tanmūlārthaprasiddhis tu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||
VKG8ab tasmād abhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śknuyāt
VKG8cd codanā cet samuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||
VKG9ab upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate
VKG9cd jñāyate yena tajjñānam ekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||
VKG10ab autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate
VKG10cd abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatas tena pramāṇatā ||
VKG11ab sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtir anyathā
VKG11cd codanā copadeśaś ca vidhiś caikārthavācinaḥ ||
VKG12ab vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhir āśritaḥ
VKG12cd sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||
VKG13ab sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt
VKG13cd pravṛttisiddhir icchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam ||
VKG14ab vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate
VKG14cd śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||
VKG15ab vidhau tu tam atikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate
VKG15cd tatsādhanasya dharmatvam evaṃ sati ca labhyate ||
VKG16ab svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syād anāptanaroktiṣu
VKG16cd āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||
VKG17ab ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ 
VKG17cd nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarāt paricodanā ||
VKG18ab pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānād vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam
VKG18cd naitat pratyakṣam ityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||
VKG19ab tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā
VKG19cd yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tad iṣyate ||
VKG20ab sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hy etat, tatsator vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ
VKG20cd śobhanārthas tu sacchabdaḥ, yad vākhyāhārakalpanā ||
VKG21ab arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam
VKG21cd bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||
VKG22ab sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam
VKG22cd na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||
VKG23ab nimittadoṣabodhena paścād yatrāpy abādhanam
VKG23cd bhavaty eva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||
VKG24ab sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam
VKG24cd na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhis tatra balīyasī ||
VKG25ab jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścād asambhavāt
VKG25cd nāśyate yuktibhis tatra vyaktam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
VKG26ab svataḥ prāmāṇyataś cātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt
VKG26cd tadrūpapratyayotpattes tadasadvādinām api ||

* autpattikasūtra nirālambanavāda (NAV)

NAV1ab pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam
NAV1cd vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||
NAV2ab sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣv evaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ
NAV2cd vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||
NAV3ab karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike
NAV3cd sarvam ityādy ayuktaṃ syād arthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||
NAV4ab tasmād dharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇair lokasammataiḥ
NAV4cd arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||
NAV5ab yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvam etat prakalpyate
NAV5cd jñānamātre 'pi kasmād vo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||
NAV6ab saṃvṛter na tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam
NAV6cd satyā cet saṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cet satyatā katham ||
NAV7ab satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ
NAV7cd virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||
NAV8ab tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ
NAV8cd vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||
NAV9ab nāstikyaparihārāṛthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ kalpaneti ca
NAV9cd kalpanāpi tv abhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||
NAV10ab tasmād yan nāsti nāsty eva, yat tv asti paramārthataḥ
NAV10cd tat satyam anyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||
NAV11ab svapnādibhogavac cāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā
NAV11cd tannivṛttyartham eveha paramārthe kaś cit pravartate ||
NAV12ab na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaś cit pravartate
NAV12cd yādṛcchikatvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||
NAV13ab paramāṛthaphalāvāptim icchadbhis tena yatnataḥ
NAV13cd pratipattir vidhātavyā yuktibhir bāhyavastuṣu ||
NAV14ab tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ
NAV14cd tasyāpy abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||
NAV15ab tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvad dvayor api
NAV15cd nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvat saṃvṛtikalpanā ||
NAV16ab tasmāt sādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpy ayam
NAV16cd bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||
NAV17ab bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitam ekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt
NAV17cd pramāṇam āśritaś caikas tatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||
NAV18ab pramāṇasthas tu mūlatvād ihedānīṃ parīkṣyate 
NAV18cd prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tv anumānataḥ ||
NAV19ab pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāt tacchaktyavekṣaṇāt
NAV19cd tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanv iti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||
NAV20ab tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam
NAV20cd tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||
NAV21ab kalpitaḥ samprayogas tu svapnādāv api vidyate
NAV21cd tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgas tena durlabhaḥ ||
NAV22ab mithyātvaṃ yad dvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathety atra cocyate
NAV22cd sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||
NAV23ab stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāt tathā hi yaḥ
NAV23cd pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||
NAV24ab siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca
NAV24cd mā bhūtām evaśabdaś ca vyārtho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||
NAV25ab sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ
NAV25cd svāṃśābhyupagamāc cāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||
NAV26ab pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam
NAV26cd hetuś copanyenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||
NAV27ab vipakṣābhāvataś cātra vyatireko na kathyate
NAV27cd sāmānyasya ca hetutvāt kasmāt pakṣaikadeśatā ||
NAV28ab jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ
NAV28cd bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||
NAV29ab tasmād yad bhāṣyakāreṇa dattam uttam atra tu
NAV29cd vikalpasamatā vā syād vaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||
NAV30ab dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣasya jātyukti kaiś cid āśritā
NAV30cd pratijñādoṣam evāhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣabādhanam ||
NAV31ab śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam
NAV31cd tadā te śuddha eva syāt pakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||
NAV32ab pratyakṣādeś ca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate
NAV32cd tanniṣedhakṛtas tasya tair bhavet pakṣabādhanam ||
NAV33ab suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayād ṛte
NAV33cd pramāṇābhāsatā nāstīty etasmāt katyate balam ||
NAV34ab duṣṭajñānagṛhītāpratiṣedho hi yujyate
NAV34cd gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||
NAV35ab agrāhyatvāc ca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ
NAV35cd aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyam anyatarasya vā ||
NAV36ab vaktṛśrotroś ca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇviśeṣyayoḥ
NAV36cd tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvyor api ||
NAV37ab sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ
NAV37cd tasmān nirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||
NAV38ab nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cid vastu gamyate
NAV38cd tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||
NAV39ab yady avastu kathaṃ tv asmāṃs tvaṃ bodhayitum icchasi
NAV39cd budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tv atha sādhyate ||
NAV40ab asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, k.lptau vastu prasajyate
NAV40cd katham iṣṭam abhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||
NAV41ab tathā pratyaya ity eṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet
NAV41cd bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma cet siddhasādhanam ||

* autpattikasūtra śunyavāda (SNV)

SNV1ab evam ukte 'numānasya jñānam ācritya dūṣaṇe
SNV1cd jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||
SNV2ab yat tāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate
SNV2cd dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||
SNV3ab pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite
SNV3cd atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||
SNV4ab tad yady etena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ
SNV4cd tvaduktaṃ sarvam ātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||
SNV5ab tatra tāvad idaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api
SNV5cd grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||
SNV6ab na cāpy ākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā
SNV6cd na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||
SNV7ab gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam
SNV7cd tasmād ākāravad vastu grāhyatvād vidyate dhruvam ||
SNV8ab ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānam ākāravad yadi
SNV8cd tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāsty arthakalpanā ||
SNV9ab yadi vākāravattā syād bāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ
SNV9cd tad asti gṛhyamāṇatvāt tatsiddhaivāsti dhīr api ||

SNV10cd ekam ākāravad vastu grāhyam ity adhyagīṣmahi ||
SNV11ab tad yady ākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyate tasya ca
SNV11cd grāhyatvam anyathā na syād iti grāhakakalpanā ||

SNV215cd vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||
SNV216ab svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu
SNV216cd nirdhāraṇe bhaved dhetur nāpūrvākārakalpane ||
SNV217ab tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā
SNV217cd ākārabhedasampattir aviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||
SNV218ab nānekākārasaṃvitter nirākāratvakalpanā
SNV218cd yuktā, pratītibhedāt tu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||
SNV219ab saṃvitteś ca viruddhānām ekasminn api sambhavaḥ
SNV219cd ekākāraṃ bhaved ekam iti neśvarabhāṣitam ||
SNV220ab tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yad yathaivopalabhyate
SNV220cd na cāpy aikāntikaṃ tasya syād ekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ || 
SNV221ab tasmād deśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak
SNV221cd vastvākārāḥ pratīyerann udbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||
SNV222ab yugapadgrāhāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam
SNV222cd śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāv ākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
SNV223ab nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak
SNV223cd cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
SNV224ab evam eva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavaty api
SNV224cd vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
SNV225ab tasmād bahiḥ sthito 'py ātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ
SNV225cd prāpya vāprāpya vā buddher viṣayatvena kalpyate ||
SNV226ab vadanti laukikā yac ca yādṛg jñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ
SNV226cd te punar jñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||
SNV227ab grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet
SNV227cd tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||
SNV228ab laiṅgikāsattvam aprāptair etair bāhyārthavādibhiḥ
SNV228cd jñānānubhavam utkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||
SNV229ab yathā loke ca tadbuddhir vācyam evaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ
SNV229cd na yādṛgantarākāras tādṛg bāhyo 'vakalpate ||
SNV230ab utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi
SNV230cd pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||
SNV231ab bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivam icchati
SNV231cd pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||
SNV232ab uttaraṃ grahakābhāvāl liṅgābhāvāc ca nāsti naḥ
SNV232cd tadā grahaṇam ity etat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||
SNV233ab teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam arthakāle 'vagamyate
SNV233cd tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syād ity etadupadiśyate ||
SNV234ab nanv ity etadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt
SNV234cd paurvāpryavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||
SNV235ab kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syāj jñātatvam atha cet tadā
SNV235cd bhūtakālāśrayād brūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||
SNV236ab atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājāt parasya tu
SNV236cd bhrāntatvād anyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||
SNV237ab sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ
SNV237cd prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitter yugapad veti cintyate ||
SNV238ab evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāj jñānāvabodhanam
SNV238cd bravītu nūnam etasya paścād utpadyate 'pi tat ||
SNV239ab na caitac chaktyate tasmād utpatter apakarṣaṇam
SNV239cd karomi tāvat tatkālā saṃvittir api setsyati ||
SNV240ab prāk ca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayor dhruvam
SNV240cd vivekādarśanam, tasmād idam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||
SNV241ab yugapad gṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate
SNV241cd tasmād arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||
SNV242ab yas tv etasyottaro granthaḥ prāg evāsau nirūpitaḥ
SNV242cd na tv etat sādhanaṃ sākṣāt pūrvaṃ buddher abodhane ||
SNV243ab na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'py ajñātavad yataḥ
SNV243cd tasān na grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||
SNV244ab ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ
SNV244cd tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvād granthavarṇanā ||
SNV245ab kāmaṃ buddher iti tv etadarthādhīnatvam ucyate
SNV245cd na cārtharūpād bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam ||
SNV246ab pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat
SNV246cd asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||
SNV247ab svacchatvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām
SNV247cd vāsanopaplavāt tena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||
SNV248ab nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānam ubhayor api
SNV248cd nijaśaktyanusāritvāj jñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||
SNV249ab tantvarthair api kasmād vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ
SNV249cd nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tair mṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ || 
SNV250ab tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hy anuyojye mate yadi
SNV250cd arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvad eva prasajyate ||
SNV251ab arthārambhavyavasthā cet sāmarthyaniyamāśrayā
SNV251cd jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||
SNV252ab tasmād yatrobhayor doṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ
SNV252cd naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyas tādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||
SNV253ab deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ
SNV253cd śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||
SNV254ab śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattilpitāḥ
SNV254cd prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavsthitāḥ ||
SNV255ab bhavatas tu na vijñānād bhinnābhinnā nirūpyate
SNV255cd śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||
SNV256ab vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate
SNV256cd nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yad ucyate ||
SNV257ab tasyāś cāsambhavenaitad apārārthyāc ca durlabham
SNV257cd deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||
SNV258ab matvaitad api cety āha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati
SNV258cd tasmād aparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyas te yathā paṭaḥ ||
SNV259ab tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhir itīdṛśaḥ
SNV259cd evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvad bāhyaśūnyatā ||
SNV260ab āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ ato 'nyathāpi vā
SNV260cd nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattir viparyayāt ||
SNV261ab tasmād abhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ
SNV261cd evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||
SNV262cd bāhyasyāṇusamūhāder grāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||
SNV263ab tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktād jñeyatvam anyasya balād upeyam
SNV263cd grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||
SNV264ab iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ
SNV264cd ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamam idaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

* auttpattikasūtra anumānapariccheda (AMP)

AMP1ab pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvād evaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat
AMP1cd prasiddham anumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tad apy ataḥ ||
AMP2ab pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ ekadeśyatha vocyate
AMP2cd karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||
AMP3ab dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandham upalabdhaṃ parasparam
AMP3cd tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau ||
AMP4ab sambandho vyāptir iṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā
AMP4cd vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyam iṣyate ||
AMP5ab yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet
AMP5cd sa vyāpyo vyāpakas tasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||
AMP6ab tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakas tasya gṛhyate
AMP6cd na hy anyathā bhavaty eṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||
AMP7ab vyāpakatvagṛhītas tu vyāpyo yady api vastutaḥ
AMP7cd ādhikye 'py aviruddhatvād vyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||
AMP8ab vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭam etc ca goviṣāṇitvayor mitau
AMP8cd vyāpyatvād gamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||
AMP9ab tena yatrāpy ubhau dhrmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau
AMP9cd tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syād aṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||
AMP10ab tena dharmyantareṣv eṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī
AMP10cd deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||
AMP11ab tasya tāvati tādṛk sa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ
AMP11cd vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādkaḥ ||
AMP12ab bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ
AMP12cd jñāyate bhedahānena, kva cic cāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||
AMP13ab kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattik.lptivat
AMP13cd vyāpteś ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaś cid dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ || 
AMP14ab asmin saty amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate
AMP14cd anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ ||
AMP15ab tair dṛṣṭair api naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā
AMP15cd ye tu tān api visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||
AMP16ab sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣair bhrāmyanti te ciram
AMP16cd teṣv āgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||
AMP17ab alaukikavivādāś ca varṇyas te haitukais tataḥ
AMP17cd niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānām adharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||
AMP18ab tadabhāve na tatsiddhir hiṃsātvād aprayojakāt
AMP18cd hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||
AMP19ab jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ
AMP19cd traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||
AMP20ab na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate
AMP20cd kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca niāśitā ||
AMP21ab prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśair na prayujyate
AMP21cd jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||
AMP22ab śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ
AMP22cd tasmād ya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||
AMP23ab sa eva gamakas tasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ
AMP23cd upāttaś caikadeśābhyāṃ dharmy apy atraikadeśatā ||
AMP24ab apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpair naikadeśatā
AMP24cd sa eva cobhayātamāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||
AMP25ab asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ
AMP25cd ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||
AMP26ab anityaḥ kṛtako yasmād dhūmavān agnimān iti
AMP26cd dharmyabhinnam upādānam, bhedo 'trāgnir itīdṛśe ||
AMP27ab ekadeśaviśiṣṭaś ca dharmyevātrānumīyate
AMP27cd na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavaty anumeyatā ||
AMP28ab na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam
AMP28cd vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||
AMP29ab ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca
AMP29cd dvayṃ ca na syād iṣṭaṃ sat pakṣeṣv eṣu yathākramam ||
AMP30ab anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi
AMP30cd dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||
AMP31ab sambandho 'py anupādānān nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau
AMP31cd na cāpy anugamas tena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||
AMP32ab na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāg bhavet
AMP32cd tasmad arthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||
AMP33ab na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ
AMP33cd viśīṣṭārthapratītau syāt sambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
AMP34ab viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam āpannau dvāv imāv ataḥ
AMP34cd gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvas tu kaiś cid iṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||
AMP35ab sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tv avagamyate
AMP35cd viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||
AMP36ab tatrotaraṃ vadanty anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam
AMP36cd hetudharmeṇa samandhas tasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
AMP37ab pradhānatvād dhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet
AMP37cd tatrāsambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||
AMP38ab dhvaner ity atha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane
AMP38cd bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||
AMP39ab agner deśaviśiṣṭatve na caitat pakṣalakṣaṇam
AMP39cd viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhaved evamprakārikā ||
AMP40ab yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva cid deśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā
AMP40cd agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||
AMP41ab yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā
AMP41cd yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy ayam ||
AMP42ab etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yam agnir iti, iha tu
AMP42cd pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syād viruddhatā || 
AMP43ab vyāptir etena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate
AMP43cd nāpi pūrvasya, nāpy eṣa vahniḥ sarvair viśiṣyate ||
AMP44ab deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy asya na deśena viśeṣyatā
AMP44cd etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yam ity etat kathyate katham ||
AMP45ab yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnir nāyam ity avadhāryate
AMP45cd agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||
AMP46ab tajjñānakālabuddhaś ca na deśaḥ syād viśeṣaṇam
AMP46cd deśasya parvatādes tu svarūpe pāvakād ṛte ||
AMP47ab gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati
AMP47cd tasmād dharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā ||
AMP48ab sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiś ca kalpitā
AMP48cd nanu śabdavad eva syāl liṅgamyaṃ viśiṣaṇam ||
AMP49ab naivam, na hy atra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā
AMP49cd na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaś cāvadhāritaḥ ||
AMP50ab viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāt tanmātrasyānumeyatā
AMP50cd nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||
AMP51ab naitad asti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā
AMP51cd dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||
AMP52ab phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārāt puroditam
AMP52cd prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakāras tu manyate ||
AMP53ab pratyakṣāniyamoktaś ca sarvatraivānuṣajyate
AMP53cd anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||
AMP54ab parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ
AMP54cd tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||
AMP55ab niyamas tadvipakṣāc ca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ
AMP55cd asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam ||
AMP56ab tādrūpyeṇa paricchittis tadviparyayato 'pi ca
AMP56cd pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||
AMP57ab tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param
AMP57cd vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||
AMP58ab mūle tasya hy anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ
AMP58cd pratyakṣādeś ca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||
AMP59ab tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāder asambhavāt
AMP59cd agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||
AMP60ab teṣām aśrāvaṇatvādi viruddham anumānataḥ
AMP60cd na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||
AMP61ab sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu
AMP61cd tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syāt pratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||
AMP62ab pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ
AMP62cd yāvajjīvam ahaṃ maunīty uktimātreṇa bādhyate ||
AMP63ab sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam
AMP63cd dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||
AMP64ab bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate
AMP64cd candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||
AMP65ab sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate
AMP65cd jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayed idam ||
AMP66ab na gor gavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ
AMP66cd gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃś caitro yadā bahiḥ ||
AMP67ab nāstīti sādhyate bādhas tatrārthāpattito bhavet
AMP67cd agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||
AMP68ab śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane
AMP68cd śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||
AMP69ab divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam
AMP69cd śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||
AMP70ab evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhas tāvad udāhṛtaḥ
AMP70cd dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||
AMP71ab śrutyarthākṣiptayor vākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ
AMP71cd tṛṇādivikriyāhetor agnimaddhimasādhane || 
AMP72ab pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāt tadviśeṣotthabādhanam
AMP72cd adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpam itīha tu ||
AMP73ab vihitatvād adharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam
AMP73cd tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣas tasya bādhyate ||
AMP74ab ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ity ukte dvayabādhanam
AMP74cd svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||
AMP75ab kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayor iha
AMP75cd darśanād ekadeśasyety anenaitad vyudasyate ||
AMP76ab yatraikasyobhayor vāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ
AMP76cd śaityān na dāhako bahniś cākṣuṣatvād anityatā ||
AMP77ab śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ
AMP77cd kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||
AMP78ab svokte caivamprakāre syād asiddho 'nyatarasya tu
AMP78cd bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayor anyatarasya vā ||
AMP79ab dhūmas tridhāpy asiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvat svarūpataḥ
AMP79cd eta eva prakārāḥ syur āśrayāsiddhikalpane ||
AMP80ab jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā
AMP80cd sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvād ātmā sarvagatas tv iti ||
AMP81ab bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādes tu saṃśayaḥ
AMP81cd bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||
AMP82ab dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātas tadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam
AMP82cd itarat sādhanaṃ tu syād vādinā yadi sādhyate ||
AMP83ab nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ
AMP83cd sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||
AMP84ab jñātasambandhavacanāt, trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ
AMP84cd san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||
AMP85ab dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāv ekatraikadeśini
AMP85cd prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||
AMP86ab nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ
AMP86cd nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syād asādhāraṇas tvayam ||
AMP87ab niścayaikāṅgavaikalyād eṣa saṃśayakāraṇam
AMP87cd sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||
AMP88ab viruddhaikānavāpteś ca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam
AMP88cd atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||
AMP89ab dvayāsattvavirodhāc ca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam
AMP89cd sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||
AMP90ab nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ
AMP90cd vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāv amūrtivat ||
AMP91ab kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā
AMP91cd yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyor arūpatvena sādhyate ||
AMP92ab sparśāt pratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā
AMP92cd ke cij jātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||
AMP93ab sādhāraṇatvam aṃśena samastaṃ vāpy ananvayam
AMP93cd pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktair yasya sādhanaiḥ ||
AMP94ab tat parājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt
AMP94cd kva cit saṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||
AMP95ab saṅghāte nirṇayas tābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat
AMP95cd pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||
AMP96ab tasmād bhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau
AMP96cd ṣoḍhā viruddhatām āhuś caturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||
AMP97ab śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā
AMP97cd nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhād viruddhatā ||
AMP98ab bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tv evaṃ prayujyate
AMP98cd arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syāt prāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||
AMP99ab vibhaktimattvāt paścādvat svarūpeṇeti cāśrite
AMP99cd asvarūpārthayogas tu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||
AMP100ab tena prāg api sambandhād asvarūpārthatā bhavet
AMP100cd ihapratyayahetutvād dravyāder vyatiricyate || 
AMP101ab samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ
AMP101cd atrāpy asamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||
AMP102ab tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyād viruddhatā
AMP102cd yac ca sattāvad ekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||
AMP103ab tatra saṃyogavadbhedāt syād viśeṣaviruddhatā
AMP103cd nityam ātmāstitā kaiś cid yadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||
AMP104ab sādhyate 'vayavābhāvād vyomavad dvayabādhanam
AMP104cd tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||
AMP105ab pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat
AMP105cd śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||
AMP106ab ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam
AMP106cd asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||
AMP107ab anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate
AMP107cd gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptir gamyeti bhāṣitum ||
AMP108ab sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate
AMP108cd tatra hetvartham uddiśya sādhyopādānam iṣyate ||
AMP109ab uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaś cetaro mataḥ
AMP109cd yadvṛttayoḥ prāthamyam ity ādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||
AMP110ab tadvṛttam eva kāraś ca syād upādeyalakṣaṇam
AMP110cd vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||
AMP111ab sādhyahetutvam arthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ
AMP111cd tatrājñānād yadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||
AMP112ab viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati
AMP112cd vivakṣann api vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vaded yadi ||
AMP113ab ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā
AMP113cd na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syād aniṣṭasya caiva tat ||
AMP114ab tasmād vyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ
AMP114cd yadā samyak prayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||
AMP115ab sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvāt paramārthataḥ
AMP115cd nityo dhvaniramūrttatvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ||
AMP116ab ghaṭavad vyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati
AMP116cd dharmyasiddhāv api hy evaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||
AMP117ab tat sadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite
AMP117cd karmādyālocanād vyāptir hetor nāstīti varjanam ||
AMP118ab vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate
AMP118cd sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||
AMP119ab paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt tac ca nāpekṣate yadā
AMP119cd vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vaded yadā ||
AMP120ab viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tat samādhitsayā tadā
AMP120cd pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||
AMP121ab sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetos tatropayujyate
AMP121cd vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayor yādṛg iṣyate ||
AMP122ab tayor abhāvayos tasmād viparītaḥ pratīyate
AMP122cd dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnis tataś cyutaḥ ||
AMP123ab adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute
AMP123cd tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmas tatacyutaḥ ||
AMP124ab anyatrānavakāśatvād vyāpyate dhruvam agninā
AMP124cd vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||
AMP125ab naiva vyāpyād vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet
AMP125cd tasmād dhūmena sādhyatvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā ||
AMP126ab tadānagnir adhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ na cānyathā
AMP126cd anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāpter vāpi viparyaye ||
AMP127ab na prastutopakāraḥ syād anyad vāpi prasādhyate
AMP127cd yatrāpy arthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet ||
AMP128ab yad anityaṃ tu tan mūrtam aṇuvad buddhivat khavat
AMP128cd sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||
AMP129ab yasyāyaṃ nāsty asau hetus tena sādhyena nāpyate
AMP129cd tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate || 
AMP130ab sahadṛṣṭir na sambandho vyāptir naiva ca tāvatā
AMP130cd mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmād aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||
AMP131ab karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvam iṣyate
AMP131cd aśeṣāpekṣitatvāc ca saukaryāc cāpy adarśanāt ||
AMP132ab sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati
AMP132cd tāvatā na hy anaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||
AMP133ab bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpter bhaviṣyati
AMP133cd astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||
AMP134ab ke cit sādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ
AMP134cd vaidharmyoktim apīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||
AMP135ab hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt sādhyenaivāvadhārite
AMP135cd vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||
AMP136ab tat tu mandaphalaṃ yasmāt pakṣe 'py evaṃ nirūpitam
AMP136cd vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyān nityaṃ nivartate ||
AMP137ab tasmād yathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām
AMP137cd nivṛttir na tu dairdhyādes tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
AMP138ab dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hy agnidhūmayoḥ
AMP138cd pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyos tathaiva hi ||
AMP139ab āditye 'nupalabdhiś cen na deśe 'py adhunātane
AMP139cd kva cit tatropalabdhiś ced devadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||
AMP140ab yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā
AMP140cd syād agnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmād evaṃ pracakṣate ||
AMP141ab pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayor eva viśeṣayoḥ
AMP141cd gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||
AMP142ab taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam
AMP142cd yadāgnir budhyate, tasya pūrvabodhāt punaḥ punaḥ ||
AMP143ab sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhāt pramāṇatā
AMP143cd viśeṣadṛṣṭam etac ca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||
AMP144ab ākṛtyor eva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit
AMP144cd hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||
AMP145ab agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau
AMP145cd sāmānyadṛṣṭam ekāntād atretyāditya ucyate ||
AMP146ab pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam
AMP146cd vastutvaṃ ca, atra hetur vā dvayasyāpy abhidhīyate ||
AMP147ab dhūmād agnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet
AMP147cd abhāvānyapramāṇatvāt svārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||
AMP148ab sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca
AMP148cd abhāvānyaprameyatvād asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
AMP149ab sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate
AMP149cd na ca liṅgavinirmuktam anumānaṃ pravartate ||
AMP150ab asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cid iṣyate
AMP150cd na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñ cid asti prakāśakam ||
AMP151ab tasya vāpy anumānena syād anyena gatiḥ punaḥ
AMP151cd tadutpattiś ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||
AMP152ab tasya cāpy anumānatvāt bhavel liṅgena codbhavaḥ
AMP152cd anumānāntarād eva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||
AMP153ab liṅgaliṅgyanumānānām ānantyād ekaliṅgini
AMP153cd gatir yugasahasreṣu bahuṣv api na vidyate ||
AMP154ab atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmād gatir bhavet
AMP154cd pramāṇād apramāṇād vā tathā liṅgigatir bhavet ||
AMP155ab evam apy anumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate
AMP155cd pramāṇāntaram eva syāt sāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||
AMP156ab apramāṇāvabuddhād vā liṅgāl liṅgini yā matiḥ
AMP156cd sāpi mithyā bhaven nityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||
AMP157ab nanv apramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtir iṣyate
AMP157cd yathā liṅgigatau hetus tathā liṅgagatir bhavet ||
AMP158ab tatra yat pūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate
AMP158cd tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāc caritārthatā || 
AMP159ab na tu liṅgagatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate
AMP159cd tadabhāvāsmṛtiś cātra na kathañ cit pravartate ||
AMP160ab smārtam etadabhedena vijñānam iti yo vadet
AMP160cd tasya vandhyāsute 'py asti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||
AMP161ab na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam
AMP161cd yasmān nāsyāvinābhāvas tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañ cana ||
AMP162ab syād vā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat
AMP162cd na hy asādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||
AMP163ab na cāpy avyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca
AMP163cd vinā pūrvānusandhānāl liṅgatvam upapadyate ||
AMP164ab kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'py aliṅgam ananvayāt
AMP164cd etasmād eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasyāpy aliṅgatā ||
AMP165ab sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam
AMP165cd kva cid vā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||
AMP166ab sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyam eṣitavyaś ca liṅganaḥ
AMP166cd anumānapravṛttes tu prāg jñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||
AMP167ab na cāpi vāsanāmātrāl liṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ
AMP167cd liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvat syāt trirūpāl liṅgato na tat ||
AMP168ab tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāv ānumānikaḥ
AMP168cd pramāṇāntaragamyatvāt tatra doṣo na jāyate ||
AMP169ab pratyakṣāvagatāl liṅgād yasya liṅgigatir bhavet
AMP169cd tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñ cit prārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||
AMP170ab yatrāpy anumitāl liṅgāl liṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet
AMP170cd tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣād eva gamyate ||
AMP171ab liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā
AMP171cd pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭam iti dūraṃ na gamyate ||
AMP172ab evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ
AMP172cd taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||
AMP173ab tasmāt pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate
AMP173cd pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatir bhavet ||
AMP174ab pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet
AMP174cd yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||
AMP175ab rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā
AMP175cd svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||
AMP176ab te cāpi tāvat sāmānyaṃ yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ
AMP176cd dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||
AMP177ab na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit
AMP177cd na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||
AMP178ab bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet
AMP178cd na ca bhinneṣv abhinnatvabuddher grāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||
AMP179ab samudāyo na vāpy asti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā
AMP179cd sarveṣām asatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||
AMP180ab na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā
AMP180cd samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣām apagacchati ||
AMP181ab sāmānyam ity adṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ
AMP181cd vyāsaṅginī bhavaty eṣā dhīrvināpy ekakalpanāt ||
AMP182ab vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ
AMP182cd grahaṇaṃ tadvad eva syāt prativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||
AMP183ab mīmāṃsakaiś ca nāvaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ
AMP183cd yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayed bhavān ||
AMP184ab samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ
AMP184cd yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||
AMP185ab samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā
AMP185cd yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||
AMP186ab tasmād yad gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā
AMP186cd tat tathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyam atha vetarat ||
AMP187ab sattādisāmānyam apekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatām upaiti
AMP187cd tasmād asādhāraṇam akṣagamyaṃ vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta || 
AMP188ab sāmānyarupeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhir atra
AMP188cd yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smin dvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

* autpattikasūtra śabdapariccheda (SBP)

SBP1ab pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam
SBP1cd adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrād abhidhīyate ||
SBP2ab sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam
SBP2cd na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ito 'py asya na vācyatā ||
SBP3ab yac coktaṃ śabdavijñānād arthe jñānam itīdṛśamū
SBP3cd aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||
SBP4ab pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā
SBP4cd puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstram abhidhīyate ||
SBP5ab svarūpakathanaṃ yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate
SBP5cd tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvam avagamyate ||
SBP6ab bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyād evopajāyate
SBP6cd pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tacchāstraṃ na padād yataḥ ||
SBP7ab aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam
SBP7cd na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||
SBP8ab tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam
SBP8cd vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||
SBP9ab pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ
