SBP9cd śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||
SBP10ab yat tu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam
SBP10cd tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||
SBP11ab veśeṣaś ca na sāmānyam antareṇāsti kaś cana
SBP11cd tasmāt tam apy udāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayet sukham ||
SBP12ab sāmānyarūpam apy etadadhikārād viśiṣyate
SBP12cd codanā copadeśaś ca śāstram evety udāhṛtam ||
SBP13ab yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyām eva vartate
SBP13cd śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||
SBP14ab pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam
SBP14cd śāstrasyāpy aparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||
SBP15ab tatrānumānam evedaṃ bauddhair vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam
SBP15cd bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhis tv iṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||
SBP16ab pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā
SBP16cd vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstīty etena bhinnatā ||
SBP17ab yair uktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā
SBP17cd dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣān na hi bhinnatā ||
SBP18ab tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvan na pratipādyate
SBP18cd tāvad viśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||
SBP19ab yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītir yāpi śabdataḥ
SBP19cd na dhūmāder itīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||
SBP20ab hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane
SBP20cd bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ ||
SBP21ab puruṣākṣiptatayāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā
SBP21cd padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||
SBP22ab sambandhātubhavaś cāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ
SBP22cd etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||
SBP23ab kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ uktā cānyair abhinnatā
SBP23cd āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyād anumānataḥ ||
SBP24ab na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedāt sarvatra bhinnatā
SBP24cd na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedas teṣāṃ pratīyate ||
SBP25ab na cāpy ajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñ cit prakāśakam
SBP25cd sambandhān anubhūtyāto na syād ananumānatā ||
SBP26ab tulyākāratayāpy atra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām
SBP26cd agnidhūmeṣv adṛṣṭatvān na bhedas tannivāraṇāt ||
SBP27ab pratibimbeṣv anaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe 
SBP27cd tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||
SBP28ab pratyakṣatā tadāpy atra tadānyair vyabhicāritā
SBP28cd yatra pādādi bambena gatānām anumīyate ||
SBP29ab ekavākyāt sakṛc coktān nāpy anekasya tatkṣaṇam
SBP29cd syād viruddhāviruddhasya bodhād etasya bhinnātā ||
SBP30ab liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ
SBP30cd virodhān nānumānaṃ cet, syād anāgamatāpi te ||
SBP31ab yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syād anumānatā
SBP31cd sakṛduccarite cāsmin vivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||
SBP32ab yas tv anirdhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam
SBP32cd sa liṅge 'py asphuṭe dṛṣṭas tasmān naitena bhidyate ||
SBP33ab dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam
SBP33cd prasiddhatvād dhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||
SBP34ab anabhyas te tv apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim
SBP34cd atra pratyukta ity evaṃ budhyante hi cirāt kva cit ||
SBP35ab paroktā hetavaś cātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ
SBP35cd śabdānumānayor aikyaṃ dhūmād agnyanumānavat ||
SBP36ab anvayavyatirekābhyām ekapratyakṣadarśanāt
SBP36cd sambandhapūrvakatvāc ca pratipattir ito yataḥ ||
SBP37ab pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāt tadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt
SBP37cd sāmānyaviṣayatvāc ca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||
SBP38ab kaiś cin mīmāṃsakair ukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt
SBP38cd pūrvābhyāṃ hy aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate ||
SBP39ab tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syāt puruṣokte, tathās tu cet
SBP39cd pratyayaḥ kin nimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nv asau ||
SBP40ab na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañ cana
SBP40cd viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||
SBP41ab tena vaktur abhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite
SBP41cd puruṣoktir api śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||
SBP42ab na cāpy ananumeyatvam āgamārthasya śakyate
SBP42cd liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gner iva kalpyate ||
SBP43ab na cāpy ananumeyavāt pramāṇāntaragamyatā
SBP43cd rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
SBP44ab evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cin nātiprapañcinaḥ
SBP44cd anumānaviśeṣo 'yam īdṛg dharmasya bodhakaḥ ||
SBP45ab bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam
SBP45cd saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||
SBP46ab lakṣaṇena tv abhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ
SBP46cd vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syād atallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||
SBP47ab āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyān nṛvacassu hi
SBP47cd lakṣaṇenānumānatvāt prāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||
SBP48ab vede tv āptanarābhāvāt sambandhānubhavād ṛte
SBP48cd lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyety aprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||
SBP49ab nanv ekadeśasatyatve tasya syād anumānatā
SBP49cd vedatvād agnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||
SBP50ab nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvad vā gauṇatā bhavet
SBP50cd nātaḥ pratyanumānānām evaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||
SBP51ab tasmāl lakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā
SBP51cd samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||
SBP52ab tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syād āgamalakṣaṇam
SBP52cd nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmāt pramāṇatā ||
SBP53ab purastād varṇitaṃ hy etat, tsmāc chabdena yā matiḥ
SBP53cd tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cet syād doṣadarśanam ||
SBP54ab anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam
SBP54cd pade tāvat kṛto yatnaḥ parair ity atra varṇyate ||
SBP55ab viṣayo 'nyādṛśas tāvad dṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ
SBP55cd sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||
SBP56ab dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaś ca liṅgīty etac ca sādhitam 
SBP56cd na tāvad anumānaṃ hi yāvat tadviṣayaṃ na tat ||
SBP57ab sāmānyād atiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ
SBP57cd sāmarthyād anumeyatvād aśrute 'pi padāntare ||
SBP58ab saṃkhyādimān padārthaś cet, na tāvat so 'vyayādiṣu
SBP58cd yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakter viśeṣaṇam ||
SBP59ab padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyāc ca kriyātmanaḥ
SBP59cd vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||
SBP60ab saty apy atra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvān naivā pakṣatā
SBP60cd tāvān eva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ ||
SBP61ab bhedabuddheś ca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ
SBP61cd viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||
SBP62ab viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiś cātra viparyayaḥ
SBP62cd atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmān na kalpyate ||
SBP63ab pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetus tatra prasajyate
SBP63cd pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ hetur iṣyate ||
SBP64ab śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate
SBP64cd vyaktir eva viśiṣyāto hetuś caikā prasajyate ||
SBP65ab bhaved vyañjakabhedāc cet, na tv evaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ
SBP65cd kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvad deśakālataḥ ||
SBP66ab tatpratītiviśiṣṭaś cet, paraṃ kim anumīyate
SBP66cd na pratyāyanaśaktiś ca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||
SBP67ab viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktir hi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat
SBP67cd sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetus tad eva ca ||
SBP68ab tasmād arthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā
SBP68cd kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||
SBP69ab na kriyākartṛsambandhād ṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit
SBP69cd rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||
SBP70ab vṛkṣas tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ
SBP70cd deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||
SBP71ab kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate
SBP71cd na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||
SBP72ab na cāsty asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā
SBP72cd tasmān na pakṣadharmo 'yam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||
SBP73ab nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā
SBP73cd vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||
SBP74ab tair apy etannirūpyaṃ tu śabdas tadviṣayaḥ katham
SBP74cd na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||
SBP75ab tasmād utpādayaty eṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim
SBP75cd tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||
SBP76ab tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā
SBP76cd na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchen na caivam anumānatā ||
SBP77ab gamakatāc ca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvād gamako yadi
SBP77cd syād anyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmān naiṣāpi kalpanā ||
SBP78ab na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ
SBP78cd śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatir bhavet ||
SBP79ab na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā
SBP79cd na cāpi pūrvasambandham apekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||
SBP80ab dhūmavān ayam ity evam apūrvasyāpi jāyate
SBP80cd pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||
SBP81ab na tv atra pūrvasambandhād adhikā pakṣadharmatā
SBP81cd na cārthapratyayāt pūrvam ity anaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
SBP82ab na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet
SBP82cd parvatādir yathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||
SBP83ab yaś cātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ
SBP83cd na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃs taddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||
SBP84ab prāk sa cet pakṣadharmatvād gṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param
SBP84cd paṣadharmādibhir jñātair yena syād anumānitā ||
SBP85ab anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate 
SBP85cd vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||
SBP86ab yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgner astitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ
SBP86cd na tv evaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||
SBP87ab na tāvat tatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate
SBP87cd bhaven nityavibhutvāc cet, sarvārtheṣu ca tat samam ||
SBP88ab tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvād vyatirekasya cāgateḥ
SBP88cd sarvaśabdair aśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||
SBP89ab athaivaṃ deśakālābhyām asatyatvaprakalpane
SBP89cd vācakapratyayaṃ kaś cid brūyād arthadhiyānvitam ||
SBP90ab naivam apy asti dṛṣṭo hi vināpy arthadhiyā kva cit
SBP90cd vācakapratyayo 'smābhir avyutpannanarān prati ||
SBP91ab dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhaved anvayakalpanā
SBP91cd śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||
SBP92ab nanu ye jñātasambandhās teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ
SBP92cd yady evam anvayāt pūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||
SBP93ab nāṅgam arthadhiyām eṣā bhaved anvayakalpanā
SBP93cd anvayādhīnajanmatvam anumānasya ca sthitam ||
SBP94ab jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśād eva jāyate
SBP94cd paścād anvaya ity eṣa kāraṇaṃ katham ucyate ||
SBP95ab tasmāt tannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate
SBP95cd na ca dhūmānvayāt pūrvaṃ śaktatvam avagamyate ||
SBP96ab vyatireko 'py avijñātād arthāc chabdadhiyau yadi
SBP96cd so 'pi paścāt sthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||
SBP97ab sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam
SBP97cd syād anvayo 'tirekaś ca na tv arthādhigamasya tau ||
SBP98ab tasmād ananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavad bhavet
SBP98cd trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||
SBP99ab sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā
SBP99cd yuktā na tu padajñānāt padārtho 'tra pramīyate ||
SBP100ab padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate
SBP100cd pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||
SBP101ab tatra yat pūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate
SBP101cd pramite ca prayuktatvād anuvādo 'dhikād vinā ||
SBP102ab adṛṣṭapūrve tv ajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā
SBP102cd sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tv anyagocaraḥ ||
SBP103ab parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matir bhavet
SBP103cd parokṣaś cānubhūtaś ca yas tatra smṛtir iṣyate ||
SBP104ab pramite ca pravṛttatvāt smṛter nāsti pramāṇatā
SBP104cd paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate ||
SBP105ab tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā
SBP105cd pratyabhijñānavat kasmāt smṛter api na kalpyate ||
SBP106ab yāvān pūrvaparicchinnas tāvān evāvadhāryate
SBP106cd smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||
SBP107ab padam abhyadhikābhāvāt smārakān na viśiṣyate
SBP107cd padādhikyaṃ bhavet kiñ cit tatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||
SBP108ab prāṇam anumānaṃ vā yady api syāt padānmitiḥ
SBP108cd vākyārthasyāgamārthatvād doṣo nāgamavādinām ||
SBP109ab vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavād ṛte
SBP109cd buddhir utpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||
SBP110ab vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati
SBP110cd sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||
SBP111ab vākyeṣv adṛṣṭeṣv api sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim
SBP111cd dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

* autpattikasūtra upamānapariccheda (UMP)

UMP1ab kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikair yadi
UMP1cd bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaur gavayas tathā || 
UMP2ab etasminn upamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ
UMP2cd tasyāgamābahirbhāvād anyathaivopavarṇitam ||
UMP3ab puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate
UMP3cd tadīyavacanatvena tasmād āgama eva saḥ ||
UMP4ab sadṛśād upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare
UMP4cd dhyānādismṛtitulyatvāt sā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
UMP5ab deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate
UMP5cd prameyaṃ naivam asty atra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||
UMP6ab śrutātideśavākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ
UMP6cd yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñ cid gosādṛśyānurañjitā ||
UMP7ab pratyakṣo gavayas tāvat sādṛśyasmṛtir atra tu
UMP7cd nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtir nendriyād gatiḥ ||
UMP8ab pūrvavākyārthavijñānān nādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi
UMP8cd smaraṇād aviśiṣṭatvāt saṅgater na pramāṇatā ||
UMP9ab atha tv adhikatā kā cit pratyakṣādivaśād bhavet
UMP9cd yāvaddhīndriyasambandhas tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam ||
UMP10ab syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā
UMP10cd śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||
UMP11ab ye 'pi hy aśrutatadvākyās teṣām api bhavaty ayam
UMP11cd pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||
UMP12ab atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate
UMP12cd na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||
UMP13ab na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate
UMP13cd sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyād avagato hy asau ||
UMP14ab na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane
UMP14cd śaktyor atīndriyatvena smṛtir eva hi seṣyate ||
UMP15ab śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣam upapāditam
UMP15cd tasmāt sādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||
UMP16ab vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate
UMP16cd jātyādivat tadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||
UMP17ab pratyakṣābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpakavādinām
UMP17cd prameyavastvabhāvāc ca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||
UMP18ab sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyam apabādhitum
UMP18cd bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||
UMP19ab sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat
UMP19cd tat svāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||
UMP20ab evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ
UMP20cd ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedād etasya citratā ||
UMP21ab na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā
UMP21cd bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||
UMP22ab yamayoḥ katham etac ced, dṛṣṭatvāt kim ihocyate
UMP22cd kva cid dhi bhūyasām etat kva cid alpīyasām api ||
UMP23ab naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate
UMP23cd sāmānyāny api caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||
UMP24ab anantāśrayayogāc ca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate
UMP24cd tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||
UMP25ab sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cid abhyupagamyate
UMP25cd sarvasya hy āśrayaḥ kaś cid asti deśāntarādiṣu ||
UMP26ab teṣāṃ bhūyas tayā cedaṃ sādṛśyam atiricyate
UMP26cd tāni vyastāni santy evaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva cit kva cit ||
UMP27ab sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate
UMP27cd tad apy avayavānāṃ syāt samānavayavāntaraiḥ ||
UMP28ab evaṃ tāvad yato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā
UMP28cd tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavet sādṛśyavarjitam ||
UMP29ab pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate
UMP29cd sa eveti bhavet tatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||
UMP30ab citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet
UMP30cd tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā || 
UMP31ab rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cit tulyatā kva cit
UMP31cd nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate ||
UMP32ab pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satām eva svabhāvataḥ
UMP32cd pariṇāmādibhir vyaktir yathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||
UMP33ab na hi śaktyātmanā kiñ cid asajjama prapadyate
UMP33cd dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntararasthitiḥ ||
UMP34ab vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā
UMP34cd dvayor ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||
UMP35ab sāmānyavac ca sādṛśyam ekaikatra samāpte
UMP35cd pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāt tadupapadyate ||
UMP36ab tatra yady api gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānam upajāyate
UMP36cd sannidhergavayasthatvād bhaved indriyagocaraḥ ||
UMP37ab tasmād yat smaryate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam
UMP37cd prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||
UMP38ab pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ
UMP38cd viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddher upamānanapramāṇatā ||
UMP39ab pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake
UMP39cd viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||
UMP40ab yatra tv asadṛśād eva kalpayitvopajāyate
UMP40cd sādṛśyapratyayas tatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||
UMP41ab bādhakapratyayāc caiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā
UMP41cd yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||
UMP42ab samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi
UMP42cd na bādhyate samīpādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat ||
UMP43ab na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt
UMP43cd prāk prameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||
UMP44ab gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavām anumāpakam
UMP44cd pratijñārthaikadeśatvād gogatasya na liṅgatā ||
UMP45ab gavayaś cāpy asambandhān na gor liṅgatvamṛcchati
UMP45cd sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||
UMP46ab ekasminn api dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane
UMP46cd sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃs tadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||
UMP47ab śṛṅgitvāder athocyeta sambandhāl liṅgatā gavi
UMP47cd na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||
UMP48ab yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syān niḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet
UMP48cd na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||
UMP49ab sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayāt param
UMP49cd gavayapratyayād eva gojñānam upajāyate ||
UMP50ab sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣām evopamā bhavet
UMP50cd na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gaur anumīyate ||
UMP51ab itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate
UMP51cd nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇān nātivartate ||
UMP52ab bhinnānumānād upameyam uktam, sauryādivākyair asahāyi dṛṣṭam
UMP52cd sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayed ity upayujyate naḥ ||
UMP53ab pratinidhir api caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogād bhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau
UMP53cd tad api phalam abhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtir api gauṇair bodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||
UMP54ab matir api ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminn
UMP54cd itaraviṣayabodhe 'saty apītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

* autpattikasūtra arthāpattipariccheda (AAP)
 {fehlt}

* autpattikasūtra abhāvapariccheda (ABH)

ABH1ab pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate
ABH1cd vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||
ABH2ab vastvasaṅkarasiddhiś ca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā
ABH2cd kṣīre dadhyādi yan nāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate || 
ABH3ab nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate
ABH3cd gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvas tu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||
ABH4ab śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ
ABH4cd śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||
ABH5ab kṣīre dadhi bhaved evaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ
ABH5cd śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtir ātmani ||
ABH6ab apsu gandho rasaś cāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha
ABH6cd vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na ced asya pramāṇatā ||
ABH7ab na ca syād vyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ
ABH7cd prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||
ABH8ab na cāvastuna ete syur bhedās tenāsya vastutā
ABH8cd kāryādīnām abhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||
ABH9ab yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatas tv ayam
ABH9cd tasmād gavādivad vastu, prameyatvāc ca gamyate ||
ABH10ab na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntir vāpi yadṛcchayā
ABH10cd bhavaty ato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||
ABH11ab pratyakṣāder anutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate
ABH11cd sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||
ABH12ab svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake
ABH12cd vastuni jñāyate kaiś cid rūpaṃ kiñ cit kadā cana ||
ABH13ab yasya yatra yadodbhūtir jighṛkṣā vopajāyate
ABH13cd cetyate 'nubhavas tasy tena ca vyapadiśyate ||
ABH14ab tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ
ABH14cd ubhayor api saṃvittāv ubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||
ABH15ab ayam eveti yo hy eṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ
ABH15cd naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamād ṛte ||
ABH16ab nāstīty api ca saṃvittir na vastvanugamād ṛte
ABH16cd jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñ cid upaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||
ABH17ab pratyakṣādyavatāras tu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā
ABH17cd vyāpāras tadanutpatter abhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||
ABH18ab na tāvad indriyair eṣā nāstīty utpadyate matiḥ
ABH18cd bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||
ABH19ab nanu bhāvād abhinnatvāt samprayogo 'sti tena ca
ABH19cd na hy atyantam abhedo 'sti rūpādivad ihāpi naḥ ||
ABH20ab dharmayor bheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite
ABH20cd udbhavābhibhavātmatvād grahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||
ABH21ab idam eva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate
ABH21cd bhāvābhāvadhiyor akṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||
ABH22ab rūpāder api bhedaṃ ca ke cid grāhakabhedataḥ
ABH22cd varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||
ABH23ab buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityam eva hi
ABH23cd na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalanā ||
ABH24ab sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāder ekateṣyate
ABH24cd svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||
ABH25ab yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syād bhedo 'tra naiva hi
ABH25cd sadsadrūpatā buddher bhaved anyataratra naḥ ||
ABH26ab tatsambandhe sad ityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate
ABH26cd nāsty atredam itīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||
ABH27ab gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam
ABH27cd mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||
ABH28ab svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścāt kiñ cit smarann api
ABH28cd tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭas tadaiva pratipadyate ||
ABH29ab na cāpy atrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvāt pratīyate
ABH29cd bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||
ABH30ab abhāvāvagater janma bhāvāṃśe hy ajighṛkṣite
ABH30cd tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||
ABH31ab na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavat pratipadyate
ABH31cd saha sarvair abhāvaiś ca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ || 
ABH32ab kva cid bhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana
ABH32cd tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cid avagamyate ||
ABH33ab yatrāpy adṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca
ABH33cd tadabhāvamatir dṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||
ABH34ab kasya cid yadi bhāvasya syād abhāvena kena cit
ABH34cd sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||
ABH35ab gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ
ABH35cd sarvatra matir ityevaṃ vyabhicārād aliṅgatā ||
ABH36ab sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam
ABH36cd tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇopajāyate ||
ABH37ab tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet
ABH37cd tatrāvaśyam abhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
ABH38ab pratyakṣāder anutpattir na tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati
ABH38cd na viśeṣaṇasambandhas tasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||
ABH39ab na cāpy abhāvasāmānye pramāṇam upajāyate
ABH39cd vyabhicārād viśeṣās tu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||
ABH40ab na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate ced asāv api
ABH40cd abhāvatvād abhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||
ABH41ab sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā
ABH41cd tadgṛhītir hi liṅgena syād anyenety anantatā ||
ABH42ab liṅgābhāve tathaiva syād anavastheyam ity ataḥ
ABH42cd kvāpy asya syāt pramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||
ABH43ab nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāder ajanmanaḥ
ABH43cd tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvam ānantaryāt pratīyate ||
ABH44ab trilakṣaṇena yā buddhir janyate sānumeṣyate
ABH44cd na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||
ABH45ab mānaṃ katham abhāvaś cet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam
ABH45cd meyo yadvadabhavo hi mānam apy evam iṣyatām ||
ABH46ab bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā
ABH46cd tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||
ABH47ab bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam
ABH47cd paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyaṃ syād dvayor api ||
ABH48ab yadi cāsya pramāṇatvam abhāvatvena neṣyate
ABH48cd vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭam ity abhimānitā ||
ABH49ab na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvad eva hi
ABH49cd tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||
ABH50ab pramāṇānām anutpatter nābhāvasyāpi dharmatā
ABH50cd yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||
ABH51ab yo na sannihitas tatra tasya dharmo bhaved iyam
ABH51cd na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||
ABH52ab abhāvena tu sambandho bhavet tadviṣayatvataḥ
ABH52cd tajjānād viṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||
ABH53ab saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate
ABH53cd nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||
ABH54ab abhāvaśabdavācyatvāt pratyakṣādeś ca bhidyate
ABH54cd pramāṇānām abhāvo hi prameyāṇām abhāvavat ||
ABH55ab abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate
ABH55cd prameyatvād yathā bhāvas tasmād bhāvātmakāt pṛthak ||
ABH56ab karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvair yathāvac ca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ
ABH56cd na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetat prabhavaṃ kratūnām ||
ABH57ab yuktyāgamābhyām iti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye
ABH57cd tato 'dhikaṃ yad dvayam iṣṭam anyair bhedo na tasyety api siddham etat ||
ABH58ab iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatir aviyutabhāvāt sānumānād abhinnā
ABH58cd jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityam aitihyam uktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamād bhidyate tat ||

* autpattikasūtra citrākṣepavāda (CAV)

CAV1ab paralokaphalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāś codanāḥ paraiḥ 
CAV1cd idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||
CAV2ab citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāś codaṇā mṛṣā
CAV2cd pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tair arthāsaṅgatir yataḥ ||
CAV3ab yadīdṛk tanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsor yathā vacaḥ
CAV3cd nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||
CAV4ab na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ
CAV4cd snānabhujyādivat te 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||
CAV5ab tadutpattāvasadbhāvāt svarge tṛptisukhādivat
CAV5cd vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukham ardane ||
CAV6ab ānantaryam ayuktaṃ cet, na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt
CAV6cd śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tat pratipāditam ||
CAV7ab kālāntarānupādānāt karmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca
CAV7cd codyamānasya citrāder ānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
CAV8ab atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaś cottarasya tu
CAV8cd svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||
CAV9ab yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ
CAV9cd sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||
CAV10ab śarīrād yadi cānyaḥ syān nāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet
CAV10cd na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||
CAV11ab yadi syād vidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet
CAV11cd viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syād idaṃ tataḥ ||
CAV12ab vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi
CAV12cd virodhaparihāraḥ syād vartamāne 'pi nāsty asau ||
CAV13ab phalaṃ ca na bhaved evaṃ bhasmībhāvād vidhāv api
CAV13cd tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||
CAV14ab prāyaś caivamprakāratvam arthavādeṣu dṛśyate
CAV14cd mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnaḥ ||
CAV15ab evaṃ saty agnihotrādivākyeṣv api mṛṣārthatā
CAV15cd vedavākyaikadeśatvāc citrādivacaneṣv api ||

* autpattikasūtra sambandhākṣepavāda (SAV)

SAV1ab svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ
SAV1cd svārthe vaktranapekṣatvāt padārthapadabuddhivat ||
SAV2ab tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ
SAV2cd vākyabuddhivad eva atra pūrvoktāś cāpi hetavaḥ ||
SAV3ab nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā
SAV3cd svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyartham aprāmāṇye nirkṛte ||
SAV4ab asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvam abravīt
SAV4cd sambandho 'sti ca nityaś cety uktam autpattikādinā ||
SAV5ab mithyā tv asya nirāsārthaṃ tatparair neṣyate dvayam
SAV5cd naiva cāsty atra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||
SAV6ab asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate
SAV6cd asminn eva ca sambandhe pratītir laukiko dhruvā ||
SAV7ab tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ
SAV7cd taddeśānantarādṛṣṭer vindhyo himavatā yathā ||
SAV8ab evam artho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyam asaṅgatam
SAV8cd kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetor uktam athāparaḥ ||
SAV9ab śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate
SAV9cd sambandhasiddhasādhyatvam atha sambandhamātrakam ||
SAV10ab pitāputrādisambandhair anekāntaḥ prasajyate
SAV10cd ekabhūmyādisambandhād dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
SAV11ab vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam
SAV11cd virodhaś ca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||
SAV12ab pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ
SAV12cd abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||
SAV13ab śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam
SAV13cd pratipattāv upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite || 
SAV14ab niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ
SAV14cd tatra yady apy asambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||
SAV15ab tathāpi yatkriyā tasyām upakāryopakāritā
SAV15cd sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||
SAV16ab na cātrāpy avinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam
SAV16cd saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cen na tadaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
SAV17ab gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ
SAV17cd na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||
SAV18ab tasmād gamakatā paścād dhūmāder iva jāyate
SAV18cd sānaṅgaṃ tadvad eva syād neyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||
SAV19ab nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hy asau
SAV19cd gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||
SAV20ab iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ
SAV20cd yad eva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||
SAV21ab tadaiva gamako 'syāyam iti nānyasvarūpataḥ
SAV21cd kathayanti kva cit tāvad boddhavyo 'smād ayaṃ tv iti ||
SAV22ab kva cid vācaka ity evaṃ vācyo 'yam iti cocyate
SAV22cd kva cid uccaritācchabdād dṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||
SAV23ab keṣāñ cit tatra boddhṛtvam anumānāt pratīyate
SAV23cd etenāsmād yataḥ śabdād artho 'yam avadhāritaḥ ||
SAV24ab tena nūnam imau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau
SAV24cd itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||
SAV25ab anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate
SAV25cd bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||
SAV26ab pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt
SAV26cd na lokaḥ kāranābhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati ||
SAV27ab balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate
SAV27cd kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||
SAV28ab sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābālāt
SAV28cd tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||
SAV29ab kiyad vā nityasambandhād abhidheyena lakṣyate
SAV29cd tatra prayogabāhulyāt tadviśeṣeṣv asatsv api ||
SAV30ab prayogāt parasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ
SAV30cd sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||
SAV31ab gośabda iti vijñānam anvayavyatirekajam
SAV31cd tasmād gamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||
SAV32ab tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ
SAV32cd sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||
SAV33ab sambandhagrahaṇāt pūrva yasmān na gamayaty ataḥ
SAV33cd gavāder nābhidhāśaktir devadattapade yathā ||
SAV34ab yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārāt pratīyate
SAV34cd tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||
SAV35ab svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale
SAV35cd tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktis tatkṛtā bhavet ||
SAV36ab yatsādhakatamatvena kasya cit kiñ cid ucyate
SAV36cd tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||
SAV37ab na hi tat kāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñ cid īdṛśam
SAV37cd itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||
SAV38ab pratyātmaniyatatvāc ca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet
SAV38cd bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva cit syād vā vivakṣayā ||
SAV39ab udvigno hy andhakāreṇa kaś cid evaṃ bravīty api
SAV39cd kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||
SAV40ab nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭir dīpaśatair api
SAV40cd rūpādidarśane yasmāt tasmāc cakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||
SAV41ab śarīrātmamanoyogād asādhāraṇātābalāt
SAV41cd vijñānāsattibhāvāc ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate ||
SAV42ab tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānam aṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ
SAV42cd gauravāt karaṇatvena mataṃ cet kena vāryate || 
SAV43ab yathā cakṣur itīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvam ucyate
SAV43cd devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ ||
SAV44ab prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate
SAV44cd phalānantaryataś cāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||
SAV45ab puruṣādhīnavijñānas tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ
SAV45cd yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaś ced dhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||
SAV46ab bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānād yathā rajjughaṭādiṣu
SAV46cd samaṃ nāsty anayoḥ kiñ cit tenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

* autpattikasūtra sphoṭavāda (SPH)

SPH1ab ādhārātmani vijñāte sukham ādheyabodhanam
SPH1cd tasyaiva tāvat prastāvād atha gaur ity ato 'bravīt ||
SPH2ab pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayam uttaram
SPH2cd tebhyo dadyād iti jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matam abravīt ||
SPH3ab tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam
SPH3cd yair āsatāṃ tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||
SPH4ab pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite
SPH4cd na hetur balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tataḥ ||
SPH5ab tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yady arthaṃ gamayen na vā
SPH5cd sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||
SPH6ab yadi tv arthagatau śaktir na syād asya tataḥ punaḥ
SPH6cd vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||
SPH7ab agnyādīn gamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi
SPH7cd na vā 'pratyāyakatvāt syād ekavarṇeṣv aśabdatā ||
SPH8ab na ca prāgarthavijñānāś chotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ
SPH8cd na cārthajñānataḥ paścād aśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||
SPH9ab parasparānapekṣāś ca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ
SPH9cd varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||
SPH10ab alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdam uccaritaṃ matiḥ
SPH10cd yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||
SPH11ab pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit
SPH11cd na ca varṇeṣv anusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvat paṭe ||
SPH12ab teṣām anupalabdheś ca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ
SPH12cd nāgamas tatparaś cāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||
SPH13ab na cāpy anupapattiḥ syād varṇasyāvayavair vinā
SPH13cd yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpy avayavāntaraiḥ ||
SPH14ab pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaś ca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ
SPH14cd kiṃ na syād, vyomavac cātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||
SPH15ab tadvac cāsyaikabuddhitvād deśabhede 'py abhinnatā
SPH15cd nanu bhedamatir na syāt, tavāpy ekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||
SPH16ab sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīs tadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ
SPH16cd na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syād ekatvadhīr yataḥ ||
SPH17ab vyaktes tāvan na sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate
SPH17cd varṇeṣv anyatra śabdatvān nānyac ced varṇa eva saḥ ||
SPH18ab sa eveti matir nāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tat kva cit
SPH18cd vināvayavasāmānyād varṇeṣv avayavā na ca ||
SPH19ab pratyakṣaviṣayatvāc ca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate
SPH19cd vācakaś cātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||
SPH20ab gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā
SPH20cd gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitat kiṃ na kalpyate ||
SPH21ab śābaleyagakāradīn niṣpannān vyaktirūpataḥ
SPH21cd sāmānyadhīr na gṛhṇātīty ato jātir apīṣyate ||
SPH22ab na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate
SPH22cd gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktir aparā sphuṭā ||
SPH23ab tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhir ekopajāyate
SPH23cd viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhaved vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
SPH24ab yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ 
SPH24cd viśeṣair api nānekam evaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||
SPH25ab tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedād bhedo 'bhyupeyate
SPH25cd mamāpi vyañjakair nādair bhedabuddhir bhaviṣyati ||
SPH26ab tena yat prārthyate jāte tad varṇād eva labhyate
SPH26cd vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīr yathā ||
SPH27ab kalpayitvāpi tatpaścād vibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ
SPH27cd pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyur mahataḥ śramāt ||
SPH28ab dvayasiddhas tu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca
SPH28cd kalpitasyeṣyate tadvat siddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||
SPH29ab pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati
SPH29cd vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛk pratīyate ||
SPH30ab dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ
SPH30cd vivedo 'sty eva na hy eṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||
SPH31ab akṣv apy evaṃ paropādhir drutādipratyayo yathā
SPH31cd varṇā ''śritatvād varṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||
SPH32ab gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate
SPH32cd gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvāt paraiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||
SPH33ab avastutvena sādhyatvān niṣedhād dhetusādhyayoḥ
SPH33cd sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhir na doṣāyātra jāyate ||
SPH34ab varṇatvāc cāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivad eva ca
SPH34cd vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer nātra dṛṣṭaṃ nirvartakam ||
SPH35ab gotvādivāraṇe tv eva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet
SPH35cd nānyathā hi matis tatra syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
SPH36ab na cāpy atraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ
SPH36cd na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvanir yathā ||
SPH37ab piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādir jātir nityaṃ pratīyate
SPH37cd tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātir ekā pratīyate ||
SPH38ab nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet
SPH38cd bhavato 'tīndriyatvāt tu kathaṃ nādair viśeṣadhīḥ ||
SPH39ab nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrād yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate
SPH39cd tadupaśleṣas tat asya bodhaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
SPH40ab naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhis tu tadvaśāt
SPH40cd saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||
SPH41ab madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā
SPH41cd gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||
SPH42ab tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāś ca gacchataḥ
SPH42cd parvatādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataś ca tān ||
SPH43ab maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ
SPH43cd vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||
SPH44ab gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇād vinā
SPH44cd vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntir bhaviṣyati ||
SPH45ab varṇāntaratvam evāhuḥ ke cid dīrghapluptādiṣu
SPH45cd na hi drutādivat tatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
SPH46ab tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate
SPH46cd sāmānyakalpanā tv anyair na yuktety abhidhīyate ||
SPH47ab atvam ity ucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayor bhavet
SPH47cd ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayos traimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||
SPH48ab sarvasādhāraṇatvena tad vijñātuṃ na śakyate
SPH48cd pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||
SPH49ab avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyād vanādivat
SPH49cd samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||
SPH50ab svato hrasvādibhedas tu nityavāde virudhyate
SPH50cd sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||
SPH51ab tasmād uccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate
SPH51cd dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ ā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svaym ||
SPH52ab dīrghāder nanv anaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet
SPH52cd itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||
SPH53ab yādṛśāt pūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāv artho gamyate tādṛśāt 
SPH53cd bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiś cet, nāsāv artham iti prati ||
SPH54ab yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet
SPH54cd paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmās tathaiva naḥ ||
SPH55ab nanu dīrghādyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet
SPH55cd ānupūrvīvad evāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||
SPH56ab tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ
SPH56cd teṣāṃ dīrghādivad bhedo na kadā cit pratīyate ||
SPH57ab tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syād drutādivat
SPH57cd nātra varṇāntaravyaktir iva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||
SPH58ab ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ
SPH58cd abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||
SPH59ab ke cit svarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cid bodhānuvartinaḥ
SPH59cd yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||
SPH60ab tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā
SPH60cd varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||
SPH61ab yugapatpracitais taiś ca syād udāttādikalpanā
SPH61cd pracaye tv itareṣāṃ syād vatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||
SPH62ab varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpām eva te matim
SPH62cd śanair utpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||
SPH63ab vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yady apy ekāntato bhavet
SPH63cd varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣas tathāpi na virudhyate ||
SPH64ab nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati
SPH64cd gakārādivacaś caitat teṣv eva na virotsyate ||
SPH65ab vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiś ca nityaiḥ sarvagatair api
SPH65cd vyatiriktapadārambho varṇair nātropapadyate ||
SPH66ab anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
SPH66cd varṇasāmānyavac cāpi na tatkalpanam arhati ||
SPH67ab varṇātmanām abhedāc ca siddhā sāmānyadhīr api
SPH67cd samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||
SPH68ab abhedasamudāyas tu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati
SPH68cd teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam arthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||
SPH69ab yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane
SPH69cd varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathivāvabodhakāḥ ||
SPH70ab teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānām arthapratyāyanaṃ prati
SPH70cd sāhityam ekakartrādikramaś cāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||
SPH71ab kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam
SPH71cd prayuñjānasya yat pūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||
SPH72ab yaugapdyaṃ tv aśakyatvān naiva teṣām ihāśritam
SPH72cd kartṛbhedaś ca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||
SPH73ab yugapad dṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā
SPH73cd bhāvās tathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||
SPH74ab dṛṣṭaś ca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ
SPH74cd abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||
SPH75ab sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā
SPH75cd sarvatrāstīti neha syād upālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||
SPH76ab niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi
SPH76cd sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedās tu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||
SPH77ab ekasādhanasāṃsthāś ca vyāpārāvayavā yadā
SPH77cd svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā ||
SPH78ab kiṃ punar bahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ
SPH78cd bhaveyur yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||
SPH79ab yadā tv ādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ
SPH79cd kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||
SPH80ab tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt
SPH80cd sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syād vyāpāre varttamānatā ||
SPH81ab pratyekaṃ ye punas tatra vyāpārās tannirūpaṇam
SPH81cd phalāniṣpattito na syān nāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||
SPH82ab phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati 
SPH82cd kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||
SPH83ab avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiś ca kasya cit
SPH83cd na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣām anaṅgatā ||
SPH84ab dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayor dhruvam
SPH84cd arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktis tatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||
SPH85ab yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā
SPH85cd tathaivetarayoḥ śaktir ānantarye na vidyate ||
SPH86ab na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktis tatra sarveṣv aśaktatā
SPH86cd tathā hy aṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||
SPH87ab śaktis tatrāsti kā cid dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate
SPH87cd saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||
SPH88ab na hy arthāvayavaḥ kaś cit pratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate
SPH88cd samastasyātha vā kaś cid bodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||
SPH89ab rathasyāpi tu yat kāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat
SPH89cd pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñ cin manāg api yathehitam ||
SPH90ab ath a yatkiñcid ucyeta vahane tad ihāpi naḥ
SPH90cd svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣv arthe 'pi vā kva cit ||
SPH91ab yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ
SPH91cd so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||
SPH92ab tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate
SPH92cd na cāvayavaśo vyaktis tadabhāvān na cātra śrīḥ ||
SPH93ab pratyekaṃ cāpy aśaktānāṃ samudāye 'py aśaktayā
SPH93cd tatra yaḥ parihāras te sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
SPH94ab sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam
SPH94cd tavādhikaṃ bhavet tasmād yatno 'sāv arthabuddhiṣu ||
SPH95ab nānyathānupapattiś ca bhaved arthamatiṃ prati
SPH95cd tad evāsyā nimittaṃ syāj jāyate yadanantaram ||
SPH96ab sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā
SPH96cd bhavatītīdṛg evāsyā nimittam avakalpate ||
SPH97ab vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ
SPH97cd kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
SPH98ab eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke cit pracakṣate
SPH98cd adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvan mātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||
SPH99ab atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi
SPH99cd dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||
SPH100ab tasyārthabuddhihetutve visāṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye
SPH100cd tadbhāvabhāvitāhetur anyatreva pratīyate ||
SPH101ab saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam
SPH101cd niṣpramāṇakam eveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||
SPH102ab yady api smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam
SPH102cd kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||
SPH103ab tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate
SPH103cd tasyārthabuddhihetutvam adṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||
SPH104ab śabdapakṣe 'pi tac caitad adṛṣṭatvān na mucyate
SPH104cd kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||
SPH105ab kṣīṇārthāpattir evaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet
SPH105cd saṃskārakalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||
SPH106ab dhvanibhyo 'py aparas tāvan neṣyetārthamatiṃ prati
SPH106cd te vā yady upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||
SPH107ab varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyam arthitā
SPH107cd nityatvāt sarvadā tat syān na tu kāraṇatā tathā ||
SPH108ab itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapad yātha vā parā
SPH108cd sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syān nityam arthadhiyaṃ prati ||
SPH109ab yad vā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yat param
SPH109cd samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||
SPH110ab tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate
SPH110cd nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tad bhavet ||
SPH111ab citrarūpāṃ cā tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām 
SPH111cd ke cid āhur yathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||
SPH112ab antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam
SPH112cd smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣv anye pracakṣate ||
SPH113ab sarveṣu caivam artheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām
SPH113cd iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsv api ||
SPH114ab na cet tadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi
SPH114cd śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||
SPH115ab tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syāt kramād varṇeṣu yady api
SPH115cd pūrvajñānaṃ parastāt tu yugapat smaraṇaṃ bhavet ||
SPH116ab tadārūḍhās tato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt
SPH116cd śabdārthamatis tena laukikair abhidhīyate ||
SPH117ab citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ
SPH117cd paścād gaur iti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate ||
SPH118ab vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭam ekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam
SPH118cd varṇarūpāvabodhāt tu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||
SPH119ab yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syād ekaikasmād trayasya tat
SPH119cd varṇatrayaparityāge buddhir nānyatra jāyate ||
SPH120ab gaur ity ekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhir nivāryate
SPH120cd tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syād ekatāmatiḥ ||
SPH121ab śaidhyād alpāntaratvāc ca gośabde sābhaved api
SPH121cd devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||
SPH122ab na gauṇaḥ śabda ity evaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet
SPH122cd asy akṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||
SPH123ab śabdād iti ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate
SPH123cd bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntāj jñānena vyavadhir bhavet ||
SPH124ab gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi
SPH124cd na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya cit sampratīyate ||
SPH125ab svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminn eva kārake
SPH125cd dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛk tu śabdasyety avyavetatā ||
SPH126ab gakārāder yadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate
SPH126cd tadā tasmāt pratīte 'rthe śabdād iti kathaṃ bhavet ||
SPH127ab śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā
SPH127cd pratyaye śabdajanyatvam iti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||
SPH128ab saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam
SPH128cd arthapratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||
SPH129ab tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate
SPH129cd samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||
SPH130ab yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate
SPH130cd varṇo 'ntyo gamakas tasya śabdatvān mudhyatā bhavet ||
SPH131ab varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ
SPH131cd vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||
SPH132ab sattvād ghaṭādivac ceti sādhanāni yathāruci
SPH132cd laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||
SPH133ab nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ
SPH133cd ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||
SPH134ab pratiṣedhet tu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān
SPH134cd dṛṣṭabādho bhavet tasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||
SPH135ab varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā
SPH135cd yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāder iva bahnidhīḥ ||
SPH136ab dīpavad vā gakārādir gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ
SPH136cd dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||
SPH137ab varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalam ādadhāti
SPH137cd kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni katuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

* autpattikasūtra ākṛtivāda (AKV)

AKV1ab ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca
AKV1cd na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tadvācyatvam ihocyate || 
AKV2ab tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyartham atra tāvat prayatyate
AKV2cd vācyatve vakṣyate yuktir vyaktyā saha balābale ||
AKV3ab jātim evākṛtiṃ prāhur vyaktir ākriyate yayā
AKV3cd sāmānyaṃ tac ca piṇḍānām ekabuddhinibandhanam ||
AKV4ab tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcit sāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram
AKV4cd sarva evecchatīty evam avirodho 'tra vādinām ||
AKV5ab sarvavastuṣu buddhiś ca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā
AKV5cd jāyate dvyātmatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||
AKV6ab viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatir bhavet
AKV6cd sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||
AKV7ab na cāpy anyatarā bhrāntir upacāreṇa ceṣyate
AKV7cd dṛḍhatvāt sarvadā buddher bhrāntis tadbhrāntivādinām ||
AKV8ab mukhyayoś cāpy adṛṣṭatvān nopacāreṇa kalpanā
AKV8cd bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||
AKV9ab anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ
AKV9cd viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||
AKV10ab nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat
AKV10cd sāmānyarahitatvāc ca viśeṣās tadvad eva hi ||
AKV11ab tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ
AKV11cd tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
AKV12ab sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣv eva yo vadet
AKV12cd vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktis tu kīdṛśī ||
AKV13ab grāhyā kiṃ vāpy asambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca
AKV13cd gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātir evānyaśabdikā ||
AKV14ab bhaven nirviṣayā buddhir yadi śaktir na gṛhyate
AKV14cd na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaś cid iṣyate ||
AKV15ab parasparavibhinnatvād viśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ
AKV15cd gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiś caiṣāṃ na vidyate ||
AKV16ab bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnām ekabuddhir na labhyate
AKV16cd viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatir bhavet ||
AKV17ab bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca
AKV17cd pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmāj jātir apīṣyatām ||
AKV18ab tenātmadharmo bhedānām ekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ
AKV18cd sāmānyam ākṛtir jātiḥ śaktir vā so 'bhidhīyatām ||
AKV19ab nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyam iti jāyate
AKV19cd buddhir vināpi sāmānyād anyasmāt sā kathaṃ bhavet ||
AKV20ab vanopanyāsatulyo 'yam upanyāsaḥ kṛtas tvayā
AKV20cd bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntir gotvādidhīr api ||
AKV21ab śabdāt pūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāv iva naikadhīḥ
AKV21cd vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
AKV22ab evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām anantatā
AKV22cd punas tena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatir asti hi ||
AKV23ab viśeṣeṣv api vastutvāt sāmānyam iti dhīr bhavet
AKV23cd sattādiṣv iva, ttenaitat sāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||
AKV24ab tasmād ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttis tannibandhanaḥ
AKV24cd sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāv ekadhīkaraṇena vā ||
AKV25ab piṇḍeṣv eva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ
AKV25cd na hy ākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñ cana ||
AKV26ab yad vā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ
AKV26cd śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||
AKV27ab tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tad eva tu
AKV27cd tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣv etat pratīyate ||
AKV28ab bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñ cic chaktiḥ kāś cid aśaktikāḥ
AKV28cd na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||
AKV29ab vahnir dahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām
AKV29cd na cānyā mṛgyate yuktir yathā sandṛśyate tathā ||
AKV30ab na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstīty etaj jñānam anarthakam
AKV30cd dharmaś cāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe || 
AKV31ab nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim
AKV31cd svābhāvikaś ca sambandho jātivyaktyor na hetumān ||
AKV32ab tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyat sāmānyam iṣyate
AKV32cd śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||
AKV33ab yad vā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt
AKV33cd viśeṣeṣv eva labdheṣu keṣu cin nānyavāñchanam ||
AKV34ab na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatas teṣu na dṛśyate
AKV34cd tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
AKV35ab sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet tasya vṛtter niyāmakam
AKV35cd gotvenāpi vinā kasmād gobuddhir na niyamyate ||
AKV36ab yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cid vṛttyapekṣitā
AKV36cd gotvāder animitte 'pi tathā buddhir bhaviṣyati ||
AKV37ab viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattir iṣyate
AKV37cd viśeṣād anyad icchanti sāmānyaṃ tena tad dhruvam ||
AKV38ab tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syur viṣayād ṛte
AKV38cd na tv anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||
AKV39ab aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ
AKV39cd naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedair ānantyato bhavet ||
AKV40ab anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate
AKV40cd jātivyaktyos tu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||
AKV41ab siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāv indriyaiḥ punaḥ
AKV41cd arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktir ekā niyāmikā ||
AKV42ab na cātmahetum evāsau siddhaṃ bādhitum arhati
AKV42cd śaktiś ca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||
AKV43ab sāmānyāntarayogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate
AKV43cd tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||
AKV44ab sambandhas tasya hetur vā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam
AKV44cd svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścād etad vikalpyate ||
AKV45ab sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvam ity upalakṣaṇam
AKV45cd na ca svasamavāyy eva kevalaṃ cihnam iṣyate ||
AKV46ab sāsnādibhyas tu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā
AKV46cd sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyas tadā syād etad uttaram ||
AKV47ab kasmāt sāsnādimatsv eva gotvaṃ yasmāt tadātmakam
AKV47cd tādātmyam asya kasmāc cet svabhāvād iti gamyatām ||
AKV48ab upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhir īdṛśī
AKV48cd svato gotvādibhedas tu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
AKV49ab sā bhūd drutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ
AKV49cd bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataś cet, iha tatsamam ||
AKV50ab vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam
AKV50cd tasmāt svābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||
AKV51ab anekānanyavṛttittvān na sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ
AKV51cd ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||
AKV52ab bhinnebhyaś cāpy abhinnatvād bhedas tat svātmavad bhavet
AKV52cd ekasmād vāpy abhinnatvād vyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||
AKV53ab ekānekatvam ekasya tathānyānanyatā katham
AKV53cd tat sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś cety evamādi ca duṣkaram ||
AKV54ab virodhas tāvad ekāntād vaktum atra na yujyate
AKV54cd sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||
AKV55ab sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ
AKV55cd evañ ca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||
AKV56ab kena cid dhy ātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit
AKV56cd sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||
AKV57ab darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ
AKV57cd yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||
AKV58ab citratvād vastuno 'py evaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam
AKV58cd sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||
AKV59ab tasya hetor asiddhatvaṃ siddhaś cet siddhasādhanam
AKV59cd bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā || 
AKV60ab tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate
AKV60cd tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||
AKV61ab sad apy agrāhyarūpatvād asadvat pratibhāti naḥ
AKV61cd viśeṣān api sāmānyād yadā bhedena buddhyate ||
AKV62ab tadā sāmānyamātratvam evam eva pratīyate
AKV62cd yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapat pratipadyate ||
AKV63ab tadānyān anyabhedādi sarvam eva pralīyate
AKV63cd na ca tat tādṛśaṃ kaś cic chabdaḥ śknoti bhāṣitum ||
AKV64ab sāmānyāṃśān apoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate
AKV64cd samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ||
AKV65ab ke cid āhur asadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate
AKV65cd sārūpyam eva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||
AKV66ab tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate
AKV66cd samānarūpabhāvaś cej jātiḥ sāsmābhir iṣyate ||
AKV67ab sādṛśyam atha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām
AKV67cd na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||
AKV68ab viśeṣarūpataḥ ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ
AKV68cd śābaleya iveti syāt tatra buddhir na gaur iva ||
AKV69ab śābaleyo 'yam iti vā bhrāntyā gaur iti nāsti dhīḥ
AKV69cd śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaur ity avatiṣṭhate ||
AKV70ab tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhir na syāt susadṛśeṣv api
AKV70cd dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||
AKV71ab na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīr bhāvet
AKV71cd na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣv asti sarvadā ||
AKV72ab sarvapuṃsām ato bhrāntir naiṣā bādhakavarjanāt
AKV72cd sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||
AKV73ab viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvād eva gauḥ kaś ca kathyatām
AKV73cd babhūva yady asau pūrvam asmadādes tadagrahāt ||
AKV74ab sādṛśyāvadhṛtir nāstīty ato godhīr na labhyate
AKV74cd na cāvayavasāmānyair vinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||
AKV75ab sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate
AKV75cd vyaktitaś cātireko 'sya syān na veti vicārite ||
AKV76ab sāmānyam eva sādṛśyaṃ bhaved vā vyaktimātrakam
AKV76cd tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam ||
AKV76ef granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate

* autpattikasūtra apohavāda (APV)

APV1ab agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam
APV1cd gotvaṃ vastv eva tair uktam ago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||
APV2ab bhāvāntaram abhāvo hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ
APV2cd tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||
APV3ab neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇas tāvad viṣayo nirvikalpanāt
APV3cd tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||
APV4ab śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam
APV4cd na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||
APV5ab na ca sākṣād viśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat
APV5cd na śābaleyavijñānam agovyāvṛttibandhanam ||
APV6ab nivṛttyā bāhuleyādes tadvijñānaṃ pravartate
APV6cd kuryād agonivṛttiṃ cen nāpohetātmavad dhi tān ||
APV7ab tenāṃśenānapohaś ca svarūpeṇāpy apohanam
APV7cd kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samamākṣepavāraṇe ||
APV8ab tasmāt prātyātmikai rūpair ago 'poho na yujyate
APV8cd samudāye 'pi naiteṣām agovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||
APV9ab sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhir vyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate
APV9cd na pratyekaṃ bhaved eṣā na samasteṣv aśaktitaḥ ||
APV10ab tasmāt sarveṣu yad rūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam
APV10cd gobuddhis tannimittā syād gotvād anyac ca nāsti tat || 
APV11ab nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate
APV11cd sattaiva hy atra sāmānyam anutpattyādirūṣitā ||
APV12ab tām utpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate
APV12cd anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
APV13ab anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyam ucyate
APV13cd abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syād bhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||
APV14ab puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ
APV14cd sāmānyapratyayaś caiṣu pratyekam upajāyate ||
APV15ab tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syād avastu tat
APV15cd gotvādāv api tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||
APV16ab kaiś cit tv atraikaśabdatvam akṣādāv iva kalpitam
APV16cd jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||
APV17ab nātra hy anantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate
APV17cd tasmāt kriyāguṇāḥ ke cid dhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||
APV18ab puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitad brāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam
APV18cd cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sad gamyate 'rthādibhir yathā ||
APV19ab yady apy avāntarā nāsti triṣu jātir vyavasthitā
APV19cd nañsāmārthyān naratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||
APV20ab śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā
APV20cd puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||
APV21ab dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktir gṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ
