APV148cd palaśādīn apohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||
APV149ab sāmānyādyanapohaś ca nāvirodhena kalpyate
APV149cd na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syād viruddhāviruddhatā ||
APV150ab na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdair asaṅgateḥ
APV150cd prāk śabdavyāpṛter nāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||
APV151ab anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate
APV151cd sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||
APV152ab śabdānurūpataś cet syād anyāpohanirūpaṇam
APV152cd bhinnatvād vṛkṣatarvāder apohaḥ kena vāryate ||
APV153ab śabdaspṛṣṭer vināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate
APV153cd na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgāc ca sidhyati ||
APV154ab adṛṣṭatvād vyudāsas tu purastād eva vāritaḥ
APV154cd sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||
APV155ab vyudāsas tatra durvāraḥ, kathañ cid dṛṣṭatā punaḥ
APV155cd brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate || 
APV156ab ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgas tulyo dravyakriyādiṣu
APV156cd vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhatyāder asaṃśayam ||
APV157ab puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā
APV157cd avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syān nīlotpalatulyatā ||
APV158ab vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate
APV158cd prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||
APV159ab tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate
APV159cd deśāvibhāgato vṛttir netrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||
APV160ab grāhakatvena vṛttis tu pratijāti vyavasthitā
APV160cd cakṣurādivad evātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||
APV161ab nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ
APV161cd sattvāder bodhakatvaṃ syād ekanyūnātirekataḥ ||
APV162ab tavaiva doṣaḥ syād eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate
APV162cd sāmānyaśabdaḥ vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpy asti vastutaḥ ||
APV163ab api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ
APV163cd nirupākhyeṣv apoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||
APV164ab tasmād yeṣv eva śabdeṣu nañyogas teṣu kevalam
APV164cd bhaved anyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||
APV165ab jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāt tvagādivat
APV165cd yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syād vyabhicāritā ||
APV166ab pakṣīkuryād yadā sarvāṃs tadāthāvītahetubhiḥ
APV166cd anaikānto virodhaś ca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
APV167ab nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena ced bhavet
APV167cd kevalāpohabuddher vā tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatā ||
APV168ab athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttir nāstīti sādhyate
APV168cd tataḥ prāk pakṣabādhaḥ syād gotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||
APV169ab sādhyahīnaś ca dṛṣṭāntaś cakṣurādy api tasya hi
APV169cd varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yady api na budhyate ||
APV170ab athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam
APV170cd apoharūpam apy etad vastv ity eva hi gamyate ||
APV171ab athāpohanimittāsya vṛttir arthe niṣidhyate
APV171cd vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvāt punaḥ prāk pakṣabādhanam ||
APV172ab anumāne tathā caitad ity anaikāntiko bhavet
APV172cd sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||
APV173ab viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivad yataḥ
APV173cd ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||
APV174ab vidhirūpapravṛtīr vā śabdo 'pohena varttate
APV174cd anumānāṅgabhūtatvād yathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||
APV175ab jātiṃ vā na bravīty eṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām
APV175cd pramāyām aṅgabhūtatvāt tvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||
APV176ab evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā
APV176cd nāvātiṣṭhata ity atra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

[vanavāda (VAV)]
[sambandhākṣepaparihāra (SAP)]
[citrākṣepaparihāra (CAP)]
[ātmavāda (ATV)]

* autpattikasūtra vanavāda (VAV)

VAV1ab sāsnādibhir viśiṣṭatvam ākṛter ucyate katham
VAV1cd yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||
VAV2ab ekāvayavisambandhas teṣāṃ gotvena vidyate
VAV2cd tenāsādhāraṇatvāt te syur gotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||
VAV3ab piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā
VAV3cd tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhir asaṃśayam ||
VAV4ab na caite vyañjakās tasya guṇavad vā viśeṣaṇam
VAV4cd tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syād gotvabodhanam ||
VAV5ab teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punargrahaṇakalpanā
VAV5cd tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syād gotvāvadhāraṇam ||
VAV6ab sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ
VAV6cd gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhisambhavaḥ ||
VAV7ab tasmāt sadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ
VAV7cd kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||
VAV8ab yady evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate
VAV8cd taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||
VAV9ab gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ
VAV9cd sāsnādeḥ kasya cid bodhas taddeśatvena jāyate ||
VAV10ab tadanatyantabhedād vā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate
VAV10cd bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||
VAV11ab pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hy atra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak
VAV11cd taddhīhānāv avijñānāt paṅktiyūthavanādivat ||
VAV12ab sarvatra lokasiddhatvān na vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam
VAV12cd niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||
VAV13ab visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ
VAV13cd pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kuto nv iyam ||
VAV14ab rūpādāv api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate
VAV14cd vivādaḥ, naiva lokas tu jātau vipratipadyate ||
VAV15ab vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ
VAV15cd dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||
VAV16ab ākṛtir jātir evātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate
VAV16cd na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate ||
VAV17ab anyadanyac ca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate
VAV17cd saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||
VAV18ab atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāv api tatsamam
VAV18cd na gotvena vinā hy etad vyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||
VAV19ab sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne saty apīdṛśe
VAV19cd na gotvādimatir dṛṣṭā tasmāj jātiḥ pṛthak tataḥ ||
VAV20ab rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvād yudāhṛtam
VAV20cd bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||
VAV21ab vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā
VAV21cd tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiś cāpy uttarārthinaḥ ||
VAV22ab hemārthinas tu mādhyasthaṃ tasmād vastu trayātmakam
VAV22cd notpādasthitibhaṅgānām abhāve syān matitrayam ||
VAV23ab na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham
VAV23cd sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||
VAV24ab mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate
VAV24cd tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātir indriyagocaraḥ ||
VAV25ab ārād dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu
VAV25cd na syād yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā || 
VAV26ab tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva cit kena cid iṣyate
VAV26cd rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādy apekṣayā ||
VAV27ab suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāt tāmratvāder asaṃśayam
VAV27cd tailād ghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||
VAV28ab bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate
VAV28cd aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||
VAV29ab saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ
VAV29cd kva cid ācārataś cāpi samyag rājānupālitāt ||
VAV30ab pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate
VAV30cd tathā saty api nānātvaṃ naikabuddher bhaviṣyati ||
VAV31ab na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam
VAV31cd vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||
VAV32ab yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ
VAV32cd kālabhede 'py abhinnaiva jātir bhinnāśrayā satī ||
VAV33ab kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate
VAV33cd na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||
VAV34ab tasmād vyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttir astīti gamyate
VAV34cd viśeṣāvasarābhāvāt tanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||
VAV35ab yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate
VAV35cd bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeś ca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||
VAV36ab tatrāvayavayogitvam avibhutvaṃca kāraṇam
VAV36cd ākṛtes tadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||
VAV37ab na ca dvaividhyam eveti vṛtter asti niyāmakam
VAV37cd trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvāt sambhaved dvividhā yathā ||
VAV38ab itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cet sragādiṣv api tatsamam
VAV38cd naiva hy anyonyatulyatvaṃ tayor nāpy anayā saha ||
VAV39ab na hy anyasminn adṛṣṭatvād vahner auṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati
VAV39cd na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñched yena nidarśanam ||
VAV40ab svarūpataś ca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtter na pararūpataḥ
VAV40cd nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣam apaśyatām ||
VAV41ab aṅgāṅgāsambhavāc cāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā
VAV41cd sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||
VAV42ab tasmād asambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam
VAV42cd yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavan bādham arhati ||
VAV43ab tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī
VAV43cd vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavat tatra gṛhyate ||
VAV44ab tasmāt piṇḍeṣu gobuddhir ekagotvanibandhanā
VAV44cd gavābhāsaikarūpyābhām ekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||
VAV45ab na śābaleyād gobuddhis tato 'nyālambanāpi vā
VAV45cd tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvād ghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||
VAV46ab pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ
VAV46cd pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvāt pratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||
VAV47ab pratyekasamavetāpi jātir ekaikabuddhitaḥ
VAV47cd nañyukteṣv api vākyeṣu brahmaṇādinivartanam ||
VAV48ab na ca sādṛśyaviṣayā godhīs tādrūpyajanmataḥ
VAV48cd prāmāṇye sati yadvad dhi pratyabhijñaikavastuni ||
VAV49ab naikarūpamatir gotve mithyā vaktuṃ ca śakyate
VAV49cd nātra kāraṇadoṣo 'sti bādhakapratyayo 'pi vā ||
VAV50ab yadā vyaktyatirekeṇa grāhyatvād anyatākṛteḥ
VAV50cd vanavannāsty anaikāntāt tatrāsambaddhatā katham ||
VAV51ab sādhanaṃ cen mayocyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā
VAV51cd dūṣaṇatvadhiyā tv etad asambaddhatvam ucyate ||
VAV52ab nāstitvahetor uktaiṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā
VAV52cd parasya sādhanaṃ hy atra yat tat pūrvam udāhṛtam ||
VAV53ab pratyakṣābhāsatā cātra naivāsti vanabuddhivat
VAV53cd kasya cin na hi mithyātvāt sarvaṃ mithyety asaṅgatiḥ ||
VAV54ab yathā vanādibuddhīnāṃ mithyātvān na rasādidhīḥ
VAV54cd mithyaivaṃ jātibuddhiḥ syād viśeṣo vābhidhīyatām || 
VAV55ab vṛkṣebhyo vyatirekeṇa vane yaikamatir bhavet
VAV55cd dūratvadoṣāt tatra syād ākṛtau tu na vidyate ||
VAV56ab sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhyekatvaṃ nivartate
VAV56cd kena cit tu prakāreṇa jātibuddhir na naśyati ||
VAV57ab yaikatvadhīr vinā śabdāt saivaṃ tāvan nirākṛtā
VAV57cd vanaśabdānuraktā tu madhyasthasyāpi jāyate ||
VAV58ab mithyātvakalpanā tv asyāḥ pratyakṣāder asambhavāt
VAV58cd jātiḥ sarvapramāṇais tu tadrūpaivāvagamyate ||
VAV59ab pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭe ca padam arthe prayujyate
VAV59cd tasmād dṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvaṃ syād vanādiṣu ||
VAV60ab ke cin nityaṃ vanaikatvaṃ śabdagamyaṃ samāśritāḥ
VAV60cd anyaiḥ saṅgatyabhāve 'pi satyaṃ tat syād rasādivat ||
VAV61ab mithyātvaṃ yadasaṅgatyā tadajñāne prasajyate
VAV61cd jñāyamānasya doṣas tu na tu kaś cid asaṅgateḥ ||
VAV62ab pramāṇāntaragamye 'rthe padaṃ nityaṃ prayujyate
VAV62cd dharmo 'yaṃ na ca sarveṣāṃ padānām abhyupeyate ||
VAV63ab asty eva saṅgatiś cātra vṛkṣā hi bahavo vanam
VAV63cd te pramāṇāntāj jñātāḥ saṃshyā caiṣānyavastuni ||
VAV64ab nānekasyaikaśabdyaṃ ced, ekaśeṣavad iṣyatām
VAV64cd tatra saṃkhyāvivṛddhiś ced, astu tanmātravarjanam ||
VAV65ab tasmāt sāmānyadṛṣṭena siddhaikatvasya saṅgatiḥ
VAV65cd tenānyānavagamyāpi saṃkhyā syāt sūryayānavat ||
VAV66ab ke cid bahutvasāmānyam āhur vṛkṣasthitaṃ vanam
VAV66cd tatra caikatvam asty eva, vanatvaṃ vāpi vidyate ||
VAV67ab vināpy ekāśrayatvena yathaivāvayavo tathā
VAV67cd asaṃyuktair abhivyaktir dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate ||
VAV68ab anyatrāpi ca tadbuddheḥ sāmānyaṃ tad abhaviṣyati
VAV68cd yathā ca bhramaṇatvādibhaṅgiṣv avayaveṣv api ||
VAV69ab vyaktaṃ nānāśrayatve 'pi gṛhyate vanatā tathā
VAV69cd yadvaikakāryahetutvād ekagośabdavad vanam ||
VAV70ab nityaṃ ye vyastavijñātā vṛkṣā neṣṭā hi te vanam
VAV70cd yad vā lakṣaṇayaikatvaṃ deśakālakriyādibhiḥ ||
VAV71ab dravyaikatvād vināpīṣṭaṃ paṅktiyūthavanādiṣu
VAV71cd vṛkṣāṇāṃ samudāye ca vanadhīr jāyate yathā ||
VAV72ab naivaṃ gosamudāye 'pi gotvadhīr upajāyate
VAV72cd yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīs tatra gotvadhīr api tādṛśī ||
VAV73ab vanavan nāpṛthaksiddheḥ samudāyatvakalpanā
VAV73cd na ca sāsnādisaṅghātas tadbuddhyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
VAV74ab kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍabuddhyaiṣu tatsāmānye hi gotvadhīḥ
VAV74cd tenāvayavyabhāve 'pi sāmānyaṃ vyatiricyate ||
VAV75ab pūrvoktād eva tu nyāyāt sidhyed atrāvayavy api
VAV75cd tasyāpy atyantabhinnatvaṃ na syād avayavaiḥ saha ||
VAV76ab vyaktibhyo jātivac caiṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate
VAV76cd kaiś cid avyatiriktatvaṃ kaiś cic ca vyatiriktatā ||
VAV77ab dūṣitā sādhitā vāpi na ca tatra balābalam
VAV77cd kadā cin niścitaṃ kaiś cit tasmān madhyasthatā varam ||
VAV78ab tato 'nyānanyate nasya sto na staś ceti kīrttyate
VAV78cd tasmāc citravadevāsya mṛṣā syād ekarūpatā ||
VAV79ab vastvanekatvavādāc ca na sandindhāpramāṇatā
VAV79cd jñānaṃ sandihyate yatra tatra na syāt pramāṇatā ||
VAV80ab ihānaikāntikaṃ vastv ityevaṃ jñānaṃ suniścitam
VAV80cd niṣkṛṣyāvayavān buddhyā yāvayavyapratītatā ||
VAV81ab buddhisthatvād vināśasya saulūkyasyāpi yujyate
VAV81cd vṛttiś cāvayaveṣv asya vyāsajyaiva pratīyate ||
VAV82ab tataḥ kārtsnyādisampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyo 'tra jātivat
VAV82cd sāsnādiguṇahetuś cen nānyasmin gotvadhīr bhavet ||
VAV83ab bhinna eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍāt piṇḍāntareyataḥ
VAV83cd na cāvayavasāmānyaṃ pareṣām upapadyate || 
VAV84ab tasmāt sāsnādito 'nyena gotvadhīr upajanyate
VAV84cd vanāntareṣa yā buddhir vanam ity upajāyate ||
VAV85ab tasyās tad eva vṛkṣatvaṃ grāhyaṃ bahvāśrayaṃ viduḥ
VAV85cd ekatve 'py ākṛter yadvad bahutvaṃ vyaktyapekṣayā ||
VAV86ab bahutve hi tathā vyakter ekatvaṃ jātyapekṣayā
VAV86cd ekānekābhidhāne ca śabdā niyataśaktayaḥ ||
VAV87ab ke cid vyaktiṃ tv asaṃkhyākāṃ gamayanty ambarādiṣu
VAV87cd eko vrīhiḥ suniṣpannaḥ iti jātiṃ svasaṃkhyayā ||
VAV88ab patnīsannahanādau tu vyaktim ākṛtisaṃkhyayā
VAV88cd kapiñjalādijātes tu pratītir vyaktisaṃkhyayā ||
VAV89ab vyaktijātī vadanty anye dravyāvayavasaṃkhyayā
VAV89cd asmān iti yathaikasmin pāśānaditir ity api ||
VAV90ab tatra vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ saṃkhyāyogo yathāruci
VAV90cd vanadārādiśabdās tu pravartante vyavasthayā ||
VAV91ab jaṅgame sthāvare cārthe yathā yūthavanādayaḥ
VAV91cd tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dārādiś cet prayujyate ||
VAV92ab vyakter avayavānāṃ ca saṃkhyām ādāya vartate
VAV92cd vanaśabdaḥ punarvyaktīr jātisaṃkhyāviśeṣitāḥ ||
VAV93ab bahvīrāhātha vā jātiṃ bahuvyaktisamāśrayām
VAV93cd evaṃ paṅktyādiśabdānāṃ saṃyogādi viśeṣaṇam ||
VAV94ab sarveṣāṃ kiñ cid astīti na nirālambanaikadhīḥ
VAV94cd tulyaṃ pratyakṣayā ''kṛtyā vane yat tadasad yadi ||
VAV95ab vṛkṣās tatra tayā tulyā iti śūnyatvavāditā
VAV95cd pratyakṣābhāsagamyatvād vṛkṣebhyo 'nyat tu tadvanam ||
VAV96ab nā''kṛtyā saha tasyāsti sparddhā pratyakṣagamyayā
VAV96cd athā''kṛtyā vanaṃ tulyaṃ sadbhāvena prasajyate ||
VAV96ef jātipakṣavimokena vanasiddhāntadūṣaṇam
VAV97ab iti nigaditam etallokasiddhaiḥ padārthair vyavahṛtir iha śāstre na svatantrābhyupetaiḥ
VAV97cd bhavati ca janadṛṣṭyā jātipaṅktyādibhedo yadi tu na ghaṭate 'sau naiva bādho 'sti kaś cit ||

* autpattikasūtra sambandhākṣepaparihāra (SAP)

SAP1ab bhavetāṃ nāma śabdārthau yāvetāvuditau tvayā
SAP1cd yadarthas tu prayāso 'yaṃ sa sambandho nirūpyatām ||
SAP2ab pūrvam evopadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate
SAP2cd svarūpākathanāc caitad uttaraṃ nopapadyate ||
SAP3ab kim auṣadhaṃ jvarasyeti pṛṣṭo yadi vaded idam
SAP3cd yenāsau naśyatīty evaṃ kiṃ tena kathitaṃ bhavet ||
SAP4ab tatra ke cid vanty eva pūrvatrāparitoṣataḥ
SAP4cd praśnaḥ punarupakrāntaḥ sambandhāntaram icchatā ||
SAP5ab yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ pratītyuttaro yataḥ
SAP5cd sā cānyapūrvikā tasmān nāsya pratyāyanāṅgatā ||
SAP6ab ajānāno 'pi saṃjñātvaṃ sambandhāntaradarśanāt
SAP6cd buddhyate 'rthaṃ tataḥ paścāt kaś cit saṃjñeti manyate ||
SAP7ab tam evānyo 'vinābhāvam atra sambandham icchati
SAP7cd na hi tasmād vinā śabde jñāte syād arthabodhanam ||
SAP8ab tattvayuktam, na bhāṣye 'sti tādṛksambandhakīrtanam
SAP8cd yadi hy etāvatocyeta kiṃ nānuktaḥ pratīyate ||
SAP9ab prayuktaś cāvinābhāvasaṃjñā lokāt tu gamyate
SAP9cd saṃjñetyagamyamāne 'pi gamakatvaṃ pratīyate ||
SAP10ab tasmāt sa eva śabdārthacintāvyavahito 'dhunā
SAP10cd nityānityavicārārthaṃ sambandhaḥ smāryate punaḥ ||
SAP11ab yacchabde jñāta ity evaṃ śaktir evātra kīrtyate
SAP11cd kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā yat tasyārthābhidhāṃ prati ||
SAP12ab svato naivāsti śaktatvaṃ vācyāvācakayor mithaḥ
SAP12cd pratītiḥ samayāt puṃsāṃ bhaved akṣinikocavat ||
SAP13ab samayaḥ pratimartyaṃ yā pratyuccāraṇam eva vā
SAP13cd kriyate jagadādau vā sakṛdekena kena cit || 
SAP14ab pratyekaṃ vāpi sambandho bhidyetaiko 'tha vā bhavet
SAP14cd ekatve kṛtako na syād, bhinnaś ced bhedadhīr bhavet ||
SAP15ab bhinnatve pratisambandhaṃ śaktiḥ kalpyābhidhā prati
SAP15cd ekasmin jñātaśaktau vā nānyenārthamatir bhavet ||
SAP16ab atha yo yasya puṃsaḥ syāt sa tena pratipadyate
SAP16cd yasyānekena sambandhaḥ kṛtas tasya kathaṃ bhavet ||
SAP17ab ekārthānāṃ vikalpaś cet, netarātyantabādhanāt
SAP17cd samuccayo 'pi naiteṣāṃ vyavahāre 'vagamyate ||
SAP18ab kiñ cid evaikamādāya vyavahāro hi dṛśyate
SAP18cd bahubhiḥ kṛtasambandhe na caiko gamako bhavet ||
SAP19ab śabdārthayor abhede 'pi pumbahutve 'pi kartari
SAP19cd nāyaṃ veti matir dṛṣṭā vikalpo 'to na yujyate ||
SAP20ab gośabde sakṛdukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu
SAP20cd vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaś cid budhyeta netare ||
SAP21ab samuccayo nṛbhedāc cet, na, vaktraikyād asambhavāt
SAP21cd vaktṛśrotṛdhiyor bhedād vyavahāraś ca duṣyati ||
SAP22ab vaktur anyo hi sambandho buddhau śrotus tathāparaḥ
SAP22cd śrotuḥ kartuṃ ca sambandhaṃ vaktā kaṃ pratipadyatām ||
SAP23ab pūrvadṛṣṭo hi yas tena śrotur naiva karoti tam
SAP23cd yaṃ karoti navaṃ so 'pi na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
SAP24ab sarvathā śrotṛsiddhiś ced, asiddhaṃ netaro vadet
SAP24cd ghaṭādāv api tulyaṃ cet, na, sāmānyaprasiddhitaḥ ||
SAP25ab yady api jñātasāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate
SAP25cd kriyate yā na tasyāś ca śaktiḥ kārye 'vadhāritā ||
SAP26ab tathāpy ākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktir utpādanādiṣu
SAP26cd tasyā na cādimattāsti, sambandhas tvādimāṃs tava ||
SAP27ab yadi tatrāpi sāmānyaṃ nityam abhyupagamyate
SAP27cd tathāpy asmanmataṃ siddham, na tu dvyākārasambhavaḥ ||
SAP28ab śaktir eva hi sambandho bhedaś cāsyā na vidyate
SAP28cd sā hi kāryānumeyatvāt tadbhedam anuvartate ||
SAP29ab anyathānupapattyā ca śaktisadbhāvakalpanam
SAP29cd na caikayaiva siddhe 'rthe bahvīnāṃ kalpaneṣyate ||
SAP30ab sambandhākhyānakāle ca gośabdādāv udīrite
SAP30cd ke cit sambandhabuddhyārthaṃ buddhyante nāpare tathā ||
SAP31ab tatra sambandhanāstitve sarvo 'rthaṃ nāvadhārayet
SAP31cd astitve sarvabodhaś cet, na kaiś cid anupagrahāt ||
SAP32ab jñāpakatvād dhi sambandhaḥ svātmajñānam apekṣate
SAP32cd tenāsau vidyamāno 'pi nāgṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ ||
SAP33ab vidyamānasya cārthasya dṛṣṭam agrahaṇaṃ kva cit
SAP33cd na tv atyantāsato 'stitvaṃ kāṃś cit pratyupapadyate ||
SAP34ab viruddhau sadasadbhāvau na syātām ekavastuni
SAP34cd nanu tulyaṃ virodhitvaṃ jñātājñātatvayor api ||
SAP35ab jñānaṃ hi puruṣādhāraṃ tadbhedān na virotsyate
SAP35cd puruṣāntarasaṃsthaṃ ca nājñānaṃ tena bādhyate ||
SAP36ab sambandhādhāratāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ sadasattvayoḥ
SAP36cd pratyuktatvāc ca bhedasya tadvaśān nāvirodhitā ||
SAP37ab andhānandhasamīpasthaḥ śuklo 'ndhair nāvagamyate
SAP37cd gamyate cetarais tasya sadasattvena tāvatā ||
SAP38ab śaktyaśaktyor narāṇāṃ tu bhedāt tatrāvirodhitā
SAP38cd na hy anyo darśanasyāsti sambandhād dhetur atra hi ||
SAP39ab evam evendriyais tulyaṃ vyavahāropalambhanam
SAP39cd yeṣāṃ syāt te 'vabhotsyante tato 'rthaṃ netare 'ndhavat ||
SAP40ab ādhānavat sakṛś caitat tantreṇopakariṣyati
SAP40cd smaraṇaṃ bhetsyate cāsya vahnipraṇayanādivat ||
SAP41ab sarveṣām anabhijñānāṃ pūrvapūrvaprasiddhitaḥ
SAP41cd siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate ||
SAP42ab pratyuccāraṇanirvṛttir bhāṣya eva nirākṛtā
SAP42cd sargādau ca kriyā nāsti, tādṛkkālo hi neṣyate || 
SAP43ab yadi tv ādau jagat sṛṣṭvā dharmādharmau sasādhanau
SAP43cd yathā śabdārthasambandhān vedān kaś cit pravartayet ||
SAP44ab jagaddhitāya vedasya tathā kiñ cin na duṣyati
SAP44cd sarvajñavat tu dussādham ity atraitan na saṃśritam ||
SAP45ab yadā sarvam idaṃ nāsīt kvāvasthā tatra gamyatām
SAP45cd prajāpateḥ kva vā sthānaṃ kiṃ rūpaṃ ca pratīyatām ||
SAP46ab jñātā ca kas tadā tasya yo janān bodhayiṣyati
SAP46cd upalabdher vinā caitat katham adhyavasīyatām ||
SAP47ab pravṛttiḥ katham ādyā ca jagataḥ sampratīyate
SAP47cd śarīrāder vinā cāsya katham icchāpi sarjane ||
SAP48ab śarīrādy atha tasya syāt, tasyotpattir na tatkṛtā
SAP48cd tadvadanyaprasaṅgo 'pi, nityaṃ yadi tad iṣyate ||
SAP49ab pṛthivyādāv anutpanne kimmayaṃ tatpunarbhavet
SAP49cd prāṇināṃ prāyaduḥkhā ca sisṛkṣāsya na yujyate ||
SAP50ab sādhanaṃ cāsya dharmādi tadā kiñ canna vidyate
SAP50cd na ca nissādhanaḥ kartā kaś cit sṛjati kiñ cana ||
SAP51ab nādhāreṇa vinā sṛṣṭirūrṇanābher apīṣyate
SAP51cd prāṇināṃ bhakṣaṇāc cāpi tasya lālā pravarttate ||
SAP52ab abhāvāc cānukampyānāṃ nānukampāsya jāyate
SAP52cd sṛjec ca śubham evaikam anukampāprayojitaḥ ||
SAP53ab athāśubhād vinā sṛṣṭiḥ sthitir vā nopapadyate
SAP53cd ātmādhīnābhyupāye hi bhavet kiṃ nāma dṛṣkaram ||
SAP54ab tathā cāpekṣamāṇasya svātantryaṃ pratihanyate
SAP54cd jagac cāsṛjatas tasya kiṃ nāmeṣṭaṃ na sidhyati ||
SAP55ab prayojanam anuddiśya na mando 'pi pravartate
SAP55cd evam eva pravṛttiś cec caitanyenāsya kiṃ bhavet ||
SAP56ab krīḍārthāyāṃ pravṛttau ca vihanyeta kṛtārthatā
SAP56cd bahuvyāpāratāyāṃ ca kleśo bahutaro bhavet ||
SAP57ab saṃhārecchāpi caitasya bhaved apratyayāt punaḥ
SAP57cd na cakaiś cid asau jñātuṃ kādā cid api śakyate ||
SAP58ab svarūpeṇopalabdhe 'pi sraṣṭṛtvaṃ nāvagamyate
SAP58cd sṛṣṭyādyāḥ praṇino ye ca budhyantāṃ kiṃ nu te tadā ||
SAP59ab kuto vayam ihotpannāḥ iti tāvan na jānate
SAP59cd prāgavasthāṃ ca jagataḥ sraṣṭṛtvaṃ ca prajāpateḥ ||
SAP60ab na ca tadvacanenaiṣāṃ pratipattiḥ suniścitā
SAP60cd asṛṣṭvāpi hy asau brūyād ātmaiśvaryaprakāśanāt ||
SAP61ab evaṃ vedo 'pi tatpūrvastatsadbhāvādibodhane
SAP61cd sāśaṅko na pramāṇaṃ syāt, nityasya vyāpṛtiḥ kutaḥ ||
SAP62ab yadi prāg apy asau tasmād arthādāsīn na tena saḥ
SAP62cd sambaddha iti tasyānyas tadartho 'nyaprarocanā ||
SAP63ab stutivākyakṛtaś caiṣa janānāṃ mativibhramaḥ
SAP63cd paurvāparyāparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdo 'nyāṃ kurute matim ||
SAP64ab upākhyānādirūpeṇa vṛttir vedavad eva naḥ
SAP64cd dharmādau bhāratādīnāṃ bhrāntis tebhyo 'py ato bhavet ||
SAP65ab ākhyānānupayogitvāt teṣu sarveṣu vidyate
SAP65cd stutinindāśrayaḥ kaś cid vedas tac codito 'pi vā ||
SAP66ab vedasyādipravṛttau ca nākṛtatvamatir bhavet
SAP66cd pralayeṣu sthitiś cāsya sāśaṅkā syāt prajāpatau ||
SAP67ab kartṛsargavināśānām athānāditvakalpanā
SAP67cd saivaṃ yuktāyathedānīṃ bhūtānāṃ dṛśyate kramāt ||
SAP68ab pralaye 'pi pramāṇaṃ naḥ sarvocchedātmake na hi
SAP68cd na ca prayojanaṃ tena syāt prajāpatikarmaṇā ||
SAP69ab na ca karmavatāṃ yuktā sthitis tadbhogavarjitā
SAP69cd karmāntaraniruddhaṃ hi phalaṃ na syāt kriyāntarāt ||
SAP70ab sarveṣāṃ tu phalāpetaṃ na sthānam upapadyate
SAP70cd na cāpy anupabhogo 'sau kasya cit karmaṇaḥ phalam ||
SAP71ab aśeṣakarmanāśe vā punaḥ sṛṣṭir na yujyate
SAP71cd karmāṇāṃ vāpy abhivyaktau kiṃ nimittaṃ tadā bhavet || 
SAP72ab īśvarecchā yadīṣyeta, saiva syāl lokakāraṇam
SAP72cd īśvarecchāvaśitve hi niṣphalā karmakalpanā ||
SAP73ab na cānimittayā yuktam utpattuṃ hīśvarecchayā
SAP73cd yad vā tasyā nimittaṃ yat tad bhūtānāṃ bhaviṣyati ||
SAP74ab sanniveśaviśiṣṭānām utpattiṃ yo gṛhādivat
SAP74cd sādhayec cetanādhiṣṭhāṃ dehānāṃ tasya cottaram ||
SAP75ab kasya cid dhetumātratvaṃ yady adhiṣṭhātṛteṣyate
SAP75cd karmabhiḥ sarvajīvānāṃ tatsiddheḥ siddhasādhanam ||
SAP76ab icchāpūrvakapakṣe 'pi, tatpūrvatvena karmaṇām
SAP76cd icchānantarasiddhis tu dṛṣṭānte 'pi na vidyate ||
SAP77ab anekāntaś ca hetus te taccharīrādinā bhavet
SAP77cd utpattimāṃś ca taddeho dehatvād asmadādivat ||
SAP78ab atha tasyāpy adhiṣṭhānaṃ tenaivety avipakṣatā
SAP78cd aśarīro hy adhiṣṭhātā nātmā muktātmavad bhavet ||
SAP79ab kumbhakārādyadhiṣṭhānaṃ ghaṭādau yadi ceṣyate
SAP79cd neśvarādhiṣṭhitatvaṃ syād, asti cet sādhyahīnatā ||
SAP80ab yathāsiddhe ca dṛṣṭānte bhaved dhetor viruddhatā
SAP80cd anīśvaravināśyādikartṛmattvaṃ prasajyate ||
SAP81ab kulālavac ca naitasya vyāpāro yadi kalpate
SAP81cd acetanaḥ kathaṃ bhāvas tadicchām anurudhyate ||
SAP82ab tasmān na paramāṇvāder ārambhaḥ syāt tadicchayā
SAP82cd puruṣasya ca śuddhasya nāśuddhā vikṛtir bhavet ||
SAP83ab svādhīnatvāc ca dharmādes tena kleśo na yujyate
SAP83cd tadvaśena pravṛttau vā vyatirekaḥ prasajyate ||
SAP84ab svayaṃ ca śuddharūpatvād asattvāc cānyavastunaḥ
SAP84cd svapnādivadavidyāyāḥ pravṛttis tasya kiṃ kṛtā ||
SAP85ab anyenopaplave 'bhīṣṭe dvaitavādaḥ prasajyate
SAP85cd svābhāvikīm avidyāṃ tu nocchettuṃ kaś cid arhati ||
SAP86ab vilakṣaṇopapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikī kva cit
SAP86cd na tv ekātmābhyupāyānāṃ hetur asti vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
SAP87ab pumānakartā yeṣāṃ tu teṣām api guṇaiḥ kriyā
SAP87cd katham ādau bhavet, tatra karma tāvan na vidyate ||
SAP88ab mithyājñānaṃ na trāsti rāgadveṣādayo 'pi vā
SAP88cd manovṛttir hi sarveṣāṃ na cotpannaṃ tadā manaḥ ||
SAP89ab karmaṇāṃ śaktyavasthānāṃ yair uktā bandhahetutā
SAP89cd sā na yuktā na kāryaṃ hi śaktisthāt kāraṇād bhavet ||
SAP90ab dadhiśaktir na hi kṣīre dādhikārambham arhati
SAP90cd dadhyārambhasya sā hetus tato 'nyā dādhikasya tu ||
SAP91ab kāraṇāc chaktyavasthāc ca yadi kāryaṃ prajāyate
SAP91cd bandhaḥ punaḥ prasajyeta phale datte 'pi karmaṇā ||
SAP92ab śaktyavasthatvam eveṣṭaṃ vināśe 'pi hi karmaṇām
SAP92cd prāk cāpi śaktisadbhāvād anuṣṭhānaṃ vṛthā bhavet ||
SAP93ab śaktyavasthaṃ ca rāgādi kiṃ neṣṭaṃ bandhakāraṇam
SAP93cd karmādattaphalatvāc cet, nāvyaktim api tad vrajet ||
SAP94ab tacchaktyaprayogitvān na jñānaṃ mokṣakāraṇam
SAP94cd karmaśaktyā na hi jñānaṃ virodham upagacchati ||
SAP95ab yady apy ajñānajanyatvaṃ karmaṇām avagamyate
SAP95cd rāgādivat tathāpy eṣāṃ na jñānena nirākriyā ||
SAP96ab karmakṣayo hi vijñānād ity etac cāpramāṇavat
SAP96cd phalasyālpasya vā dānaṃ rājaputrāparādhavat ||
SAP97ab adyatve 'pi hi śaktisthaṃ yadi syāt karmakāraṇam
SAP97cd tataḥ pradhānakāle 'pi yujyate kāraṇābhidhā ||
SAP98ab manovṛttir idānīṃ tu hetur nāsti ca sā tadā
SAP98cd manasāṃ saṅkarāc cāpi tadā syāt karmasaṅkaraḥ ||
SAP99ab gasmān naiṣo 'dhikārākhyo bandhahetuḥ prakalpate
SAP99cd yogyatve 'py adhikārākhye viprayogo na yujyate ||
SAP100ab caitanyaṃ yogyatā puṃsaḥ prakṛtes tadanātmatā
SAP100cd bhoktṛbhogyatvayos te ca na tābhyām apagacchataḥ || 
SAP101ab utpattau karmaṇāṃ ceṣṭam ajñānaṃ kāraṇaṃ yadi
SAP101cd tannāśāt syād anutpattis teṣāṃ na phaloavarjanam ||
SAP102ab jñānaṃ mokṣanimittaṃ ca gamyate nendriyādinā
SAP102cd na ca sāṅkhyādivijñānān mokṣo vedena codyate ||
SAP103ab ātmā jñātavya ity etanmokṣārthaṃ na ca coditam
SAP103cd karmapravṛttihetutvam ātmajñānasya lakṣyate ||
SAP104ab vijñāte cāsya pārārthye yāpi nāma phalaśrutiḥ
SAP104cd sārthavādo bhaved eva na svargādeḥ phalāntaram ||
SAP105ab sukhopabhogarūpaś ca yadi mokṣaḥ prakalpyate
SAP105cd svarga eva bhaved eṣa paryāyeṇa, kṣayo ca saḥ ||
SAP106ab na hi kāraṇavat kiñ cid akṣayitvena gamyate
SAP106cd tasmāt karmakṣayād eva hetvabhāve na mucyate ||
SAP107ab na hy abhāvātmakaṃ muktvā mokṣanityatvakāraṇam
SAP107cd na ca kriyāyāḥ kasyāś cid abhāvaḥ phalam iṣyate ||
SAP108ab tatra jñātātmatattvānāṃ bhogāt pūrvakriyākṣaye
SAP108cd uttarapracayāsattvād deho notpadyate punaḥ ||
SAP109ab karmajanyopabhogārthaṃ śarīraṃ na pravartate
SAP109cd tadabhāve na kaś cid dhi hetus tatrāvatiṣṭhate ||
SAP110ab mokṣārthī na pravarteta tatra kāmyaniṣiddhyoḥ
SAP110cd nityanaimittike kuryāt pratyavāyajihāsayā ||
SAP111ab prārthyamānaṃ phalaṃ jñātaṃ na cānicchor bhaviṣyati
SAP111cd ātmajñe caitad astīti tajjñānam upayujyate ||
SAP112ab sargapralayavijñānaṃ samastajagadāśrayam
SAP112cd svaśarīravidāṃ puṃsāṃ nādhikyenopayujyate ||
SAP113ab tasmād adyavad evātra sargapralayakalpanā
SAP113cd samastakṣayajanmabhyāṃ na sidhyatyapramāṇikā ||
SAP114ab sarvajñavanniṣedhyā ca sraṣṭuḥ sadbhāvakalpanā
SAP114cd na ca dharmādṛte tasya bhavel lokād viśiṣṭhatā ||
SAP115ab na cānanuṣṭhito dharmo nānuṣṭhānam ṛte mateḥ
SAP115cd na ca vedādṛte sā syād vedo na ca padādibhiḥ ||
SAP116ab tasmāt prāg api sarve 'mī sraṣṭurāsan padādayaḥ
SAP116cd syāt tatpūrvakatā cāsya caitanyād asmadādivat ||
SAP117ab evaṃ ye yuktibhiḥ prāhus teṣāṃ durlabham uttaram
SAP117cd aneṣyo vyavahāro 'yam anādir vedavādibhiḥ ||
SAP118ab pratyakṣādāv upakṣīṇe yo 'numānena ḍitthavat
SAP118cd sambandhitvān niyoktāraṃ gavādāv api kalpayet ||
SAP119ab gavādiśabdasambandhaṃ sarvo 'nyasmāt prapadyate
SAP119cd madvat tadvyavahāritvāt tasyaitat pratisādhanam ||
SAP120ab devadattādiśabde 'pi prasaktaivam anāditā
SAP120cd sambandhasya, balīyastvād dṛṣṭabādhān nivartate ||
SAP121ab tatrāpi śaktinityatvam, niyogasya tv anityatā
SAP121cd tadgatāc cāpy anityatvāc chaktau bhrāntiḥ pravartate ||
SAP122ab gavādiṣu tu na bhrāntir niyogānāditā yataḥ
SAP122cd yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt pūrvaṃ sambandhadarśanāt ||
SAP123ab siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate
SAP123cd yadā cāptapraṇītatvāc chabdo 'rthaṃ pratipādayet ||
SAP124ab na svaśaktyā tadāptatvaṃ mitau na smaryate katham
SAP124cd yathā bauddhādayo yāvad buddhādyuktaṃ na jānate ||
SAP125ab na tāvat pratipadyante bodhe vākyena saty api
SAP125cd samaye kathyamāne 'nyair asmaranto 'pi pāṇinim ||
SAP126ab ādaicaḥ pratipadyante vṛddhiṃ kartuṃ smṛtir vṛthā
SAP126cd sūtrasthaḥ pāṇinis tatra svasaṃjñāṃ pratipādayet ||
SAP127ab gauḥ sāsnādimatīty evaṃ vākyaṃ tv atra na vidyate
SAP127cd asambandhāc ca sarveṣām evaṃ kartum asambhavaḥ ||
SAP128ab tasmān na pratipattiḥ syāt kathañ cit kartṛvarjitā
SAP128cd dṛṣārthavyavahāratvād vṛddhyādau sambhaved api ||
SAP129ab dharmāya niyamo 'trāpi na vinā pāṇiner bhavet
SAP129cd ākārānugamo yo hi vṛddhyā syād āśvalāyane || 
SAP130ab nāsāv apāṇinīyatve sādhur ity avagamyate
SAP130cd dṛṣṭe bhavatu mā vā bhūt kartṛsampratipannatā ||
SAP131ab vaidido vyavahāras tu na kartṛsmaraṇād ṛte
SAP131cd burgeṣu gavi gośabdaprayogo gamyate katham ||
SAP132ab gatvā cet kena cid dṛṣṭaḥ sambanddhā kiṃ na gacchati
SAP132cd īśvaratvād agatiś cāsya na kva cit pratibadhyate ||
SAP133ab bahūnāṃ kāryataś cāpi saṅgānaṃ kena vāryate
SAP133cd ekatra kathitaṃ cāpi lokenānyatra nīyate ||
SAP134ab vṛddhyādiva, ato vyākhyā dvitīyaivātra śobhanā
SAP134cd kāṃś cit prasiddhasambandhān abhyupetya vaded yadi ||
SAP135ab sambandhakaraṇam, tatra ke siddhā iti durvadam
SAP135cd na tāvad anya evāsan śabdā iti hi yuktimat ||
SAP136ab viśeṣo 'dyatanānāṃ ca gavādīnāṃ na dṛśyate
SAP136cd śabdārthānāditāṃ muktvā sambandhānādikāraṇam ||
SAP137ab na syād anyad, ato vede sambandhādir na vidyate
SAP137cd upāyarahitatvena sambandhakaraṇānumā ||
SAP138ab anākhyānānumānaṃ tu dṛṣṭenaiva viruddhyate
SAP138cd buddhānāṃ dṛśyamānā ca pratipattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||
SAP139ab upāya iti taddhānirasiddhāvagatiṃ prati
SAP139cd hastasaṃjñādyupāyo hi siddho nādyakriyāsu naḥ ||
SAP140ab na hy asau jñātasāmarthyo vinānyair vyavahartṛbhiḥ
SAP140cd śabdavṛddhābhidheyāṃś ca pratyakṣeṇātra paśyati ||
SAP141ab śrotuś ca pratipannatvam anumānena ceṣṭayā
SAP141cd anyathā 'nupapattyā ca buddhyec chaktiṃ dvayāśritām ||
SAP141ef arthāpattyāvabuddhyante sambandhaṃ tripramāṇakam

* autpattikasūtra citrākṣepaparihāra (CAP)

CAP1ab citrādiniṣphalatve 'pi yaduktaṃ sādhanadvayam
CAP1cd tatra hetor asiddhatvam ānantaryaṃ hy acoditam ||
CAP2ab ānantaryaśrutiś cātra sāmārthyād api neṣyate
CAP2cd nāviśeṣā phalotpattiḥ karmaṇā nopapadyate ||
CAP3ab karmaṇāṃ cāpi vaicitryād deśakālādyapekṣaṇāt
CAP3cd kasya cic cārddhabhuktatvāt karmānyat pratibadhyate ||
CAP4ab tenānantaryaniṣpattiḥ phalasyehāpramāṇikā
CAP4cd pratyakṣādivisaṃvādo na śabde doṣamāsajet ||
CAP5ab ānantaryavisaṃvādo nāviśeṣapravartinīm
CAP5cd codanāṃ bādhituṃ śaktaḥ sphuṭād viṣayabhedataḥ ||
CAP6ab yā tu mardanasādharmyād ānantaryā 'numā kṛtā
CAP6cd bādhyate 'nupalabdhyāsau samānaviṣayā yataḥ ||
CAP7ab dṛṣṭārthasyāpi sevāder āyātam api satphalam
CAP7cd utpadyate cireṇaiva pratibandhena kena cit ||
CAP8ab uptamātre na hi vrīhau phalam utpadyate kva cit
CAP8cd athāṅkuro 'pi tatra syāt, svargo 'py astīti gamyatām ||
CAP9ab sthūlībhūtaś cireṇaiṣa bhogyatvaṃ pratipadyate
CAP9cd sarvasyotpadyamānasya kramaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sthitaḥ ||
CAP10ab anantaraphalatvaṃ tu citrāder yadi sādhyate
CAP10cd tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatvam anyadā na phalaṃ bhavet ||
CAP11ab vyabhicārāc ca sevādeḥ paśvādeḥ sādhanāntaram
CAP11cd kim apy adṛṣṭam asty eva tatrānyanniṣpramāṇakam ||
CAP12ab īśvarecchādhikārādiśabdaliṅgādivarjanāt
CAP12cd kṛtaṃ kadā cic citrādiśabdena tv avagamyate ||
CAP13ab nirnimittā na cotpattiḥ, na hi sarvāpramāṇatā
CAP13cd bodhayan na ca śabdo 'tra prāmāṇyād ativarttate ||
CAP14ab yeṣāṃ tv iha phalāny eva citrādīnīti kalpanā
CAP14cd nirnimittaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ syād ihākṛtakarmaṇām ||
CAP15ab citrādīnāṃ phalaṃ tāvat kṣīṇaṃ tatraiva janmani
CAP15cd na ca svargaphalasyeha kaś cid aṃśo 'nuvartate || 
CAP16ab naiva hy anyaphalaṃ karma sādhayen naḥ phalāntaram
CAP16cd gautamīye 'pi taccheṣas tasmāc citrādyapekṣayā ||
CAP17ab svābhāvikatve siddhe ca karmānantarabhāvy api
CAP17cd phalaṃ kriyānimittatvaṃ na kathañ cit prapadyate ||
CAP18ab tatra mlecchādivat sarve karmākṛtvāpi vaidikam
CAP18cd palaṃ labhanta ity evaṃ naṣṭā vedapramāṇatā ||
CAP19ab anantaraṃ niyogena paśvādi ca bhaved yadi
CAP19cd pratyakṣaphalataiva syāt trivṛtpānavirekavat ||
CAP20ab janmāntarānubhūtaṃ ca na smaryata itīdṛśam
CAP20cd na bhāṣyaṃ na ca sūtraṃ syād aprāpte śāstram arthavat ||
CAP21ab tasmāt kālāviśeṣeṇa codanārtho yathā sthitaḥ
CAP21cd sa tathaivānugantavyo nādhiko niṣpramāṇakaḥ ||
CAP22ab sarveṣāṃ karmavaiguṇyāt phalābhāvaṃ vadanti ye
CAP22cd ānantaryam upetyaiva te svābhāvikavādinaḥ ||
CAP23ab svargasyāmuṣmikatvaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhādye sthāpayiṣyate
CAP23cd paśvāder niyamābhāvo yogasiddhir itīha tu ||
CAP24ab yadā kadā cid bhavad etad iṣyate phalaṃ hi paśvādi na sāmparāyikam
CAP24cd tathā sthitasyaiva hi tasya sādhanaṃ vidhīyate yo 'pi bhṛśaṃ tvarānvitaḥ ||
CAP25ab sādhāraṇaṃ yat tu palaṃ bahūnāṃ svabhāvatas tādṛśaṃ eva ceṣṭam
CAP25cd sarvasya vā ''san na tayaiva kāmyaṃ vṛṣṭyādi tac caihikam eva yuktam ||
CAP26ab kamipadam aviśiṣṭaṃ yady api śrūyate vā bhavati phalaviśeṣī nānyathā kāmyate hi
CAP26cd phalati yadi ni sarva tat kadā cit tadaiva dhruvam aparam abhuktaṃ karma śāstrīyamās te ||

* autpattikasūtra ātmavāda (ATV)

ATV1ab sākṣād yady api sambandho nātmano yajñasādhanaiḥ
ATV1cd tathāpi lakṣaṇāvṛttyā śarīradvārako bhavet ||
ATV2ab pratyakṣatvaṃ ca dehasthaṃ bhāktam ātmani kalpitam
ATV2cd ātmanaḥ svargayānaṃ vā śarīrasyopacaryyate ||
ATV3ab nairātmyenātra cākṣiptāḥ sarvā eva hi codanāḥ
ATV3cd sādhyasādhanasambandhas tadukto na hi siddhyati ||
ATV4ab tā hi kartuḥ phalenāhuḥ sambandhaṃ kvāpi janmani
ATV4cd na ca vijñānamātratve bhoktṛkartṛtvasambhavaḥ ||
ATV5ab śarīravinipātāc ca paraṃ nānyad yadeṣyate
ATV5cd adattaphalaiṣṭyādau tadā tadvacanaṃ mṛṣā ||
ATV6ab tasmād vedapramāṇārtham ātmātra pratipādyate
ATV6cd yady api prakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyāyetārthavādataḥ ||
ATV7ab śarīrendriyabuddhibhyo vyatiriktatvm ātmanaḥ
ATV7cd nityatvaṃ ceṣyate, śeṣaṃ śarīrādi vinaśyate ||
ATV8ab nityaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtve pratipanno 'pi san yadā
ATV8cd na karmaphalasambandhaṃ bhogakāle 'vabudhyate ||
ATV9ab mayā yat tu kṛtaṃ karma tasyedaṃ bhujyate phalam
ATV9cd śubhāśubhaṃ mayaiveti tadā ko 'sya raso bhavet ||
ATV10ab aprāmṛśyamāne hi svakarmapratyaye phale
ATV10cd na viśeṣo bhavet kaś cit svaparātmopabhogayoḥ ||
ATV11ab kurvann apy aśubhaṃ karma tenaivaṃ cintayen naraḥ
ATV11cd na smariṣyāmi bhoge 'ham iti naitad vivarjayet ||
ATV12ab tatra nityatvapakṣe 'pi kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau
ATV12cd phalatas tulyarūpau ced vṛthā tatpratipādanam ||
ATV13ab naiṣa doṣaḥ, na bhoge hi smṛtir na upayujyate
ATV13cd na pravṛtir nivṛttir vā bhogakāle smṛter bhavet ||
ATV14ab tadaṅgaṃ yaḥ parāmarśas tadastitvaṃ ca mṛgyate
ATV14cd prāk pravṛttes tu so 'sty eva viduṣāṃ śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
ATV15ab paścād api ca śāstrajñā vimṛśanty eva ke cana
ATV15cd teṣām evādhikāraś ca mā bhūd aviduṣāṃ tu saḥ ||
ATV16ab parāmarśaś ca sarvatra nāsti sarvapramāṇakaḥ
ATV16cd na cānyenāparāmṛṣṭe syād anyasyāpramāṇatā ||
ATV17ab nāvabudhyeta yas tv evaṃ mamāsmāt karmaṇaḥ phalam 
ATV17cd bhaviṣyatīty avidvattvād daivād evātra na kriyā ||
ATV18ab aparāmṛśyamāne 'pi svāpakāle sukhāśraye
ATV18cd sambhoge mṛduśayyādau prākpravṛttiś ca dṛśyate ||
ATV19ab bhogakāle 'nusandadhyāt phalaṃ yadi tu kaś cana
ATV19cd rathādikarmavad yāge śāstraṃ syād aprakalpakam ||
ATV20ab tava nityavibhutvābhyām ātmāno niṣkriyā yadi
ATV20cd sukhaduḥkhāvikāryāś ca kīdṛśo kartṛbhoktṛtā ||
ATV21ab atha kartṛtvavelāyāṃ duḥkhādeś cāpi janmani
ATV21cd prāgrūpād anyathātvaṃ syān nityatāsya virudhyate ||
ATV22ab nānityaśabdavācyatvam ātmano vinivāryate
ATV22cd vikriyāmātravācitve na hy ucchedo 'sya tāvatā ||
ATV23ab syātām atyantanāśe 'sya kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau
ATV23cd na tv avasthāntaraprāptau loke bālayuvādivat ||
ATV24ab avasthāntarabhāvyetat phalaṃ mama śubhāśubham
ATV24cd iti jñātvānutiṣṭhaṃś ca vijahac ceṣṭate janaḥ ||
ATV25ab anavasthāntaraprāptir dṛśyate na ca kasya cit
ATV25cd anucchedāt tu nānyatvaṃ bhoktur loko 'vagacchati ||
ATV26ab sukhaduḥkhādyavasthāś ca gacchann api naro mama
ATV26cd caitanyadravyasattādirūpaṃ naiva vimuñcati ||
ATV27ab duḥkhinaḥ sukhyavasthāyāṃ naśyeyuḥ sarva eva te
ATV27cd duḥkhitvaṃ cānuvarteta vināśe vikriyātmake ||
ATV28ab tasmād ubhayahānena vyāvṛttyanugamātmakaḥ
ATV28cd puruṣo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ kuṇḍalādiṣu svarṇatvat ||
ATV29ab na ca kartṛtvabhoktṛtve puṃso 'vasthāsam āśrite
ATV29cd tenāvasthāvatas tattvāt karttaivāpnoti tatphalam ||
ATV30ab na cāvasthāntarotpāde pūrvātyantaṃ vinaśyati
ATV30cd uttarānuguṇatvāt tu sāmānyātmani līyate ||
ATV31ab svarūpeṇa hy avasthānām anyonyasya virodhitā
ATV31cd aviruddhas tu sarvāsu sāmānyātmā pravartate ||
ATV32ab nairātmyavādapakṣe tu pūrvam evāvabudhyate
ATV32cd madvināśāt phalaṃ nasyānmatto 'nyasyātha vā bhavet ||
ATV33ab iti naiva pravṛttiḥ syān na ca vedapramāṇatā
ATV33cd janmānare 'bhyupete 'pi jñānamātrātmavādinām ||
ATV34ab jñānānāṃ kṣaṇikatvād dhi kartṛbhoktranyatā bhavet
ATV34cd niṣkriyatvāvibhutvābhyāṃ na ca dehāntarāśritiḥ ||
ATV35ab kartā ya eva santāno nanu bhoktā sa eva naḥ
ATV35cd vijñānakṣaṇabhedas tu tvadavasthāntaraiḥ samaḥ ||
ATV36ab kartṛtvam eva duḥsādhaṃ dīrghakāleṣu karmasu
ATV36cd satsu jñānasahastreṣu kulakalpopamaṃ hi tat ||
ATV37ab vyatirikto hi santāno yadi nābhyupagamyate
ATV37cd santāninām anityatvāt kartā kaś cin na labhyate ||
ATV38ab bhoktur atyantabhedāc ca prasajyetākṛtāgamaḥ
ATV38cd kṛtanāśaṃ tu na brūmaḥ kṛtaṃ naiva hi kena cit ||
ATV39ab santānānanyatāyāṃ tu vācoyuktyantareṇa te
ATV39cd tatra coktam, na cāvastu santānaḥ kartṛtāṃ vrajet ||
ATV40ab santānakṣaṇikatve ca tad eva, akṣaṇikas tv atha
ATV40cd siddhāntahāniḥ, evaṃ ca so 'pi dravyāntaraṃ bhavet ||
ATV41ab ekā cāvyatiriktā ca santānibhyo 'tha santatiḥ
ATV41cd bhedābhedau prasaṅktavyau grāhyagrāhakayor yathā ||
ATV42ab tasmād atyantabhedo vā kathañ cid vāpi bhinnatā
ATV42cd santānasyety ayaṃ cātmā syād vaiśeṣikasāṃkhyayoḥ ||
ATV43ab santāno 'yaṃ sa eveti na tv abhedād vinā bhavet
ATV43cd vāyudopādisantāne vāyutvādir na bhidyate ||
ATV44ab jñānatvenāpy abhinnatvaṃ śūnyavāde nirākṛtam
ATV44cd tathaiva karmabhir veṣṭā phalārthaṃ cittavāsanā ||
ATV45ab na cātra vāsanākālaṃ kiñ cic cittam avasthitam
ATV45cd avastutvāc ca santānaḥ karmabhinaiva vāsyate ||
ATV46ab tatpāramparyajāte 'pi bhuñjāne karmaṇaḥ phalam 
ATV46cd tādātmyena vinā spaṣṭau kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau ||
ATV47ab santānāntarajebhyaś ca yo hetuphalabhāvataḥ
ATV47cd viśeṣaḥ so 'pi dussādhaḥ, parihāro na cānayoḥ ||
ATV48ab tasminn asaty api brūyāḥ parihāraṃ tvam anyathā
ATV48cd samānapṛthivīvāsajñānatvādyaviśeṣataḥ ||
ATV49ab samāna iti nāpy etadekatvānugamād vinā
ATV49cd tena yaccittajaṃ tasya santāna iti vo mṛṣā ||
ATV50ab na hi yacchabdatacchabdau vartete bhinnavastuni
ATV50cd tenaikātmakataiṣṭavyā tatsantānātmavādibhiḥ ||
ATV51ab nanv anyatvaṃ vidanto 'pi putrādiphalasiddhaye
ATV51cd pravartante yathā tadvajjñānasantānino 'pi nah ||
ATV52ab anyatve ca samāne 'pi yathā vaṃśāntarodbhavāḥ
ATV52cd na labhante phalaṃ tadvat santānāntarajāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ||
ATV53ab na tāvad buddhir atraivam, api cātmaphalecchayā
ATV53cd putrādibharaṇe vṛttiḥ syāt tad apy atra nāsti te ||
ATV54ab phalāntaram anuddiśya na ca putrādi bibhrati
ATV54cd vinaṣṭasya tu nātmīyasantānabharaṇāt phalam ||
ATV55ab yas tv anenaiva mārgeṇa phalāntaram apīcchati
ATV55cd svasantānyantarair bhogyaṃ tatsantānāny upakārakam ||
ATV56ab anavasthedṛśī tasya svopabhogād ṛte bhavet
ATV56cd naiva hy anyo 'pi santānī kaś cit tasyātmavanmataḥ ||
ATV57ab yāvad yāvac ca dūrasthe santānini phalaṃ bhavet
ATV57cd tāvat tāvac ca tannaśyet sutarāṃ viprakarṣataḥ ||
ATV58ab bharaṇaṃ yadapatyānāṃ tiryagādiṣu dṛśyate
ATV58cd ajñānaṃ śaraṇaṃ tatra prājñānāṃ tu na yujyate ||
ATV59ab dehāntare ca buddhīnāṃ sañcāro nopapadyate
ATV59cd pūrvadehād bahir bhāvo na ca tāsāṃ pratīyate ||
ATV60ab vāyunā preryamāṇaṃ hi jvālādyanyatra sañcaret
ATV60cd buddheḥ kāraṇadeśāt tu preraṇaṃ nāsti kena cit ||
ATV61ab amūrtatvāt svayaṃ nāsāvutplutyā 'nyatra gacchati
ATV61cd jīvaddehe 'pi tenāsyā gamanaṃ nopapadyate ||
ATV62ab antarābhavadehas tu niṣiddho vindhyavāsinā
ATV62cd tadastitve pramāṇaṃ hi na kiñ cid avagamyate ||
ATV63ab sahasā jāyate tac ca sahasaiva vinaśyati
ATV63cd sūkṣmarūpādiyuktaṃ cety utprekṣāmātram eva tat ||
ATV64ab saty api jñānasañcāras tatra syān niṣpramāṇakaḥ
ATV64cd tena cānyaśarīreṣu punarnikṣepakalpanā ||
ATV65ab kalalādiṣu vijñānam astīty etac ca sāhasam
ATV65cd asañjātendriyatvād dhi na tatrārtho 'vagamyate ||
ATV66ab na cārthāvagater anyad rūpaṃ jñānasya yujyate
ATV66cd mūrcchādāv api tenāsya sadbhāvo nopapadyate ||
ATV67ab na cāpi śaktirūpeṇa tadā dhīr avatiṣṭhate
ATV67cd nirāśrayatvāc chaktīnāṃ sthitir na hy avakalpate ||
ATV68ab yadi bhūtendriyādhārā jñānaśaktir bhavet tataḥ
ATV68cd tac caitanyaṃ prasajyeta na ca janmāntaraṃ bhavet ||
ATV69ab pariṇāmavivekādyaiḥ śaktyabhivyaktyanugrahāt
ATV69cd tebhya eva bhaved buddhir na buddhyantarapūrvikā ||
ATV70ab tathaivottarakāle 'pi pūrvabuddher yad ucyate
ATV70cd buddhyantaraprasūtatvaṃ dṛṣṭānto 'tra na vidyate ||
ATV71ab athādhāravinirmuktā śaktiḥ syāt kalalādiṣu
ATV71cd paścād vijñānasiddhyartham ātmā śaktyabhidho bhavet ||
ATV72ab śaktyādhāraprak.lptau vā nātmano 'nyaḥ prakalpyate
ATV72cd jvālābudbudavad vṛttir na cādhārād dhiyām ||
ATV73ab jñānaśaktisvabhāvo 'to nityaḥ sarvagataḥ pumān
ATV73cd dehāntarakṣamaḥ kalpyaḥ so 'gacchann eva yokṣyate ||
ATV74ab yajamānatvam apy ātmā sakriyatvāt prapadyate
ATV74cd na parispanda evaikaḥ kriyā naḥ kaṇabhojivat ||
ATV75ab na ca svasamavetaiva kartṛbhiḥ kriyate kriyā 
ATV75cd kriyā dhātvarthamātraṃ syād anyādhāre 'pi kartṛtā ||
ATV76ab sattājñānādirūpāṇāṃ kartā tāvat svayaṃ pumān
ATV76cd yo 'pi bhūtaparispandas tatrādhiṣṭānato bhavet ||
ATV77ab taduddeśapravṛtteś ca yā yā dehendriyaiḥ kriyā
ATV77cd kriyate puruṣeṇaiva sā sā sarvā kṛtocyate ||
ATV78ab naiva hy eṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ syāt puruṣeṇāparigrahe
ATV78cd asvātantryād ato naiṣāṃ parispande 'pi kartṛtā ||
ATV79ab tatkarmopārjitaiś cetaiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu karmasu
ATV79cd kartṛtā yajamānānām ṛtvikparaśukarmavat ||
ATV80ab yathā parikrayāmnānād ṛtvigdvārā kriyeṣyate
ATV80cd gamanādividhes tadvad bhūtadvāratvam āśritam ||
ATV81ab krayo yathātmano nāsti gamanādi tathaiva hi
ATV81cd vidhīyate ca tenātra paradvārāsya kartṛtā ||
ATV82ab yathā vā devadattasya cchedane kāṣṭhasaṃśrite
ATV82cd kartṛtvam evaṃ puṃsaḥ syāc charīragamanādiṣu ||
ATV83ab vyāpārāntaratas tatra kartṛtvaṃ ced ihāpi naḥ
ATV83cd saṅkalpasattvavattvābhyāṃ pumāniṣṭaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
ATV84ab sādhāraṇyena kartṛtvaṃ sattvavattvena karmasu
ATV84cd saṅkalpanaiḥ punar bhedāt pratikarmāsya kartṛtā ||
ATV85ab na ca sarvatra tulyatvaṃ syāt prayojakakarmaṇām
ATV85cd calanena hy asiṃ yoddhā prayuṅkte cchedanaṃ prati ||
ATV86ab senāpatis tu vācaiva bhṛtyānāṃ viniyojakaḥ
ATV86cd rājā sannidhimātreṇa viniyuṅkte kadā cana ||
ATV87ab tasmād acalato 'pi syāc calane kartṛtātmanaḥ
ATV87cd yathaivābhidyamānasya devadattasya bhettṛtā ||
ATV88ab karmāntarair yadādānaṃ svavyāpāraḥ sa eva vā
ATV88cd bhūtakriyāsu puṃsaḥ syāt, tāni bhūtāntaraiḥ punaḥ ||
ATV89ab tāni bhūtāntarebhyaś cety evamādir na vidyate
ATV89cd karmakṣayāt tv anātmīyaiḥ kṛtaṃ karma na limpati ||
ATV90ab anvārambhaṇamānādāv audumbaryādivarttini
ATV90cd svarūpāsambhavād yaṣṭuḥ śarīreṇaiva kartṛtā ||
ATV91ab tasmād yathākṛtau śāstraṃ pravṛttaṃ vyaktim āśrayet
ATV91cd tathā puṃsi pravṛttasya bhūtendriyasamāśrayaḥ ||
ATV92ab parair abhigatān pūrvam ātmahetun nirasyati
ATV92cd nety etāvad avacchedyam, vidharmāṇa ime yataḥ ||
ATV93ab athāvasthāntaraṃ tatra tathā mṛtyur apīṣyatām
ATV94ab etāvan iha bhedaḥ syāc charīre dṛḍha eva yā
ATV94cd prāṇādyapagatis tatra nimittaṃ na pratīyate ||
ATV95ab guṇo dravyavināśād vā vināśam upagacchati
ATV95cd guṇāntaropapātād vā tasmād utkṛtya nāśyate ||
ATV96ab na tāvat tad dvayaṃ mṛtyau sarvasyaivopalabhyate
ATV96cd avinaṣṭaśarīrasya prāṇādiś cāpagacchati ||
ATV97ab tasmān na dehadharmatvaṃ prāṇāder iti gamyate
ATV97cd tasmin dṛṣṭe 'py asadbhāvāt sragvilepanagandhavat ||
ATV98ab bahirvṛttitvam apy asti prāṇāder iti gamyate
ATV98cd parendriyaiḥ, sukhādis tu nāntaratvāt pratīyate ||
ATV99ab prahṛṣṭavadanatvādiliṅgagamyaṃ sadaiva hi
ATV99cd antaḥsthiter na dṛṣṭiś cet, pāṭite 'py anupagrahāt ||
ATV100ab antaḥśarīre rūpādi pāṭitasyopalabhyate
ATV100cd na sukhādiḥ, ago 'syāsau na manobuddhivad guṇaḥ ||
ATV101ab guṇatvād āśritatvaṃ hi sukhādeḥ syād rasādivat
ATV101cd ya āśritaḥ sa ātmā, iti bruvāṇasyaitaduttaram ||
ATV102ab puṇānāṃ paratantratvāt guṇavān anumīyate
ATV102cd siddhe guṇatve tat tv asmān pratyasiddhaṃ sukhādiṣu ||
ATV103ab bhedena kim upanyastā tulyanyāyecchayā smṛtiḥ
ATV103cd ubhayaṃ na hy adṛṣṭe 'rthe vāsanātaś ca siddhyati ||
ATV104ab upalabdhimanāśritya smṛtyaivecchopajāyate
ATV104cd upalabdhisamāno 'syāḥ kartā naikāntato bhavet || 
ATV105ab upalabdhyanusāreṇa smṛtyātmā punar iṣyate
ATV105cd samānas tena kartāsti tadarthaṃ punar ucyate ||
ATV106ab tatrāpi tu samānāyāṃ santatau vāsanā yataḥ
ATV106cd tasmāt saty api bhinnatve smaraṇaṃ vyavatiṣṭate ||
ATV107ab hetuṣv evaṃ parokteṣu pratiṣiddheṣu samprati
ATV107cd ahampratyayavijñeyaḥ svayamātmopapādyate ||
ATV108ab ahaṃ yāmīty ahaṃśabdaḥ śarīrārthaḥ prayujyate
ATV108cd gantṛtvāt tasya, na hy ātmā gamanaṃ pratipadyate ||
ATV109ab smaraṇapratyabhijñāne bhavetāṃ vāsanāvaśāt
ATV109cd anyārthaviṣaye, jñātuḥ pratyabhijñā tu durlabhā ||
ATV110ab ahaṃ vedmīty ahaṃ buddhir jñātāram adhigacchati
ATV110cd tatra syād jñātṛvijñānaṃ tadādhāro 'tha vā pumān ||
ATV111ab kṛtaṃ bhūtendriyāṇāṃ ca caitanyapratiṣedhanam
ATV111cd samastavyastasaṅghātavivekapariṇāminām ||
ATV112ab sāṅkhyādibhiḥ aśuddhatvāt saṅghātāt sanniveśataḥ
ATV112cd mṛtavac ca śarīratvād bhūtatvād bāhyabhūtavat ||
ATV113ab cetanatve hi sarveṣāṃ na sambandhaḥ parasparam
ATV113cd samatvāt, ekacaitanye 'nyasyāṅgatvaṃ virudhyate ||
ATV114ab saṅghātasanniveśau ca na staḥ pārārthyavarjitau
ATV114cd bhoktā ca cetanaḥ kaś cid astīty atrāviruddhatā ||
ATV115ab yadi syād jñānamātraṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ jñātṛ tatra vaḥ
ATV115cd na bhavet pratyabhijñānaṃ pūrvajñātari samprati ||
ATV116ab jñātavān aham evedaṃ puredānīṃ ca vedmy aham
ATV116cd tasya jñānakṣaṇaḥ ko nu viṣayaḥ parikalpyatām ||
ATV117ab pūrvavṛtte hi viṣaye jñātavān iti sambhavet
ATV117cd jānāmīti na satyaṃ syān nedānīṃ vetty asau tataḥ ||
ATV118ab yadīdānīntano grāhyo jānāmīty upapadyate
ATV118cd jñātavān ity ado 'satyaṃ naivājñāsīdayaṃ yataḥ ||
ATV119ab ubhayagrāhyatāṃ tu dvayam apy anṛtaṃ bhavet
ATV119cd na hy etau jñātavantau vā jānīto vādhunā punaḥ ||
ATV120ab santāno na ca tadgrāhyo dvairūpyasyāsambhavāt
ATV120cd jñātavān na hy asau pūrvam avastutvān na vādhunā ||
ATV121ab sāmānyaṃ na ca kiñ cit te jñātṛ pūrvāparakṣaṇe
ATV121cd sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñā cen na syād asadṛśeṣu sā ||
ATV122ab gām ahaṃ jñātavān pūrvam aśvaṃ jānāmy ahaṃ punaḥ
ATV122cd atha jñātṛtvasāmānyaṃ tat syād dehāntareṣv api ||
ATV123ab tatra sarveṇa vijñāte bhaved aham iti smṛtiḥ
ATV123cd ekasantānaje cāpi sa iti syāt kṣaṇe matiḥ ||
ATV124ab yathā dehāntarajñāne ghaṭādau vā bahiḥ sthite
ATV124cd jñātari pratyabhijñāṃ ca vāsanā kartum arhati ||
ATV125ab nātasmin sa iti jñānaṃ na hy asau bhrāntikāraṇam
ATV125cd na cāhampratyayo bhrāntir iṣṭo bādhakavarjanāt ||
ATV126ab jñātur anyaś ca viṣayas tasya na syāt svabhāvataḥ
ATV126cd ahaṃ pratyayavijñeyo jñātā naḥ sarvadaiva hi ||
ATV127ab guruḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśo vāham iti dehe 'pi yā matiḥ
ATV127cd bhrāntiḥ sā bhedarūpaṃ hi guru me tad itīṣyate ||
ATV128ab idaṃ mamedṛśaṃ cakṣurmano me bhrāntam ity api
ATV128cd indriyeṣv api bhedena vyavahāraś ca dṛśyate ||
ATV129ab ajñātṛtvasya siddhatvād virodhād bhedavaty api
ATV129cd pratyāsattinimittas tu syād abhedamatir bhramaḥ ||
ATV130ab mamātmeti matibhedavyapadeśena yātmanaḥ
ATV130cd tatrāvasthātmanā bhedaṃ jñānasyāśritya kalpanā ||
ATV131ab mametyetasya mukhyārtho nātmano 'nyaḥ pratīyate
ATV131cd tenāsau bhedahetuḥ syād, bhedaś ca jñānahetukaḥ ||
ATV132ab ye cehājñātanānātvās teṣāṃ deheṣv ahaṃ matiḥ
ATV132cd tatrāpy ātmābhimānenety ahambuddhir dhruvātmani ||
ATV133ab ye tu vijñātanānātvās te deheṣv anahaṃkṛtāḥ
ATV133cd jānāmy aham itīdaṃ tu jñānaṃ naiva nivarttate || 
ATV134ab tannivṛttau na teṣāṃ syād dhyānaṃ śiṣyopadeśane
ATV134cd pravṛttir dṛśyate sā ca, tenātmā taiḥ pratīyate ||
ATV135ab śāstrādavardhavijñāte yady ahaṃ jñātavān iti
ATV135cd nāvagacchet tataḥ sarvaḥ pravartetāditaḥ punaḥ ||
ATV136ab tenāsmāt pratyabhijñānāt sarvalokāvadhāritāt
ATV136cd nairātmyavādabādhaḥ syāt, ete ca pratihetavaḥ ||
ATV137ab hyastanāhammatigrāhyo jñātādyāpy anuvarttate
ATV137cd ahaṃpratyayagamyatvād idānīntaboddhṛvat ||
ATV138ab eṣa vā hyo bhavej jñātā jñātṛtvāt tat eva vā
ATV138cd hyastanajñātṛvat, teṣāṃ pratyayānāṃ ca sādhyatā ||
ATV139ab ekasantānasambandhijñātrahampratyayatvataḥ
ATV139cd hyastanādyatanāḥ sarve tulyārthaś caikabuddhivat ||
ATV140ab vedādevātmanāstitvaṃ yo nāma pratipadyate
ATV140cd virodhaṃ vātmanā brūyāt taṃ prati brāhmaṇābhidhā ||
ATV141ab anyathānupapatteś ca vidhinātmanyapekṣite
ATV141cd astitvadyotanād etair arthākṣiptasamarthanam ||
ATV142ab śāntāyāṃ vācyaśaktāyām ātmā kena prakāśyate
ATV142cd ātmanaiva prakāśyo 'yam ātmā jyotir itīritam ||
ATV143ab agrāhya iti sāmānyāt sarveṇeti pratīyate
ATV143cd ātmajyotiṣṭvavacanāt parair ity avatiṣṭhate ||
ATV144ab arthād evārthabuddhir yā sā śuddhaivopamocyate
ATV144cd sādṛśyabodhanaṃ śabdair upamānāgamau punaḥ ||
ATV145ab ātmajñānāvinābhūtadṛṣṭaceṣṭānirūpaṇāt
ATV145cd pareṣām ātmavijñānam anumānād udāhṛtam ||
ATV146ab sadasannāśyanāśātmaparikīrtanam ūḍhayā
ATV146cd coditaḥ pūrvapakṣo 'yam iti siddhāntam abravīt ||
ATV147ab avināśī svarūpeṇa puruṣo yā tu nāśitā
ATV147cd mātrāṇāṃ sā 'dhikārāṇām, bhūtādīnām asaṃjñitā ||
ATV148ab ity āha nāsti kyanirākariṣṇur ātmāstitāṃ bhāṣyakṛdatra yuktyā
ATV148cd dṛḍhatvam etadviṣayaś ca bodhaḥ prayāti vedāntaniṣevaṇena ||

* śabdanityatādhikaraṇa (SNA)

SNA1ab yady anityatvapakṣe 'pi śabdād artho 'vagamyate
SNA1cd anādir vyavahāraś ca nityatvaṃ kiṃ nu sādhyate ||
SNA2ab satyam icchanti te 'py evaṃ nyāyas tatra parīkṣyate
SNA2cd na parābhyupagatyaiva prāmāṇyam avatiṣṭhate ||
SNA3ab yadā hi kṣaṇikaḥ śabdo na śakto 'rthāvadhāraṇe
SNA3cd yuktyāvadhāryate tatra nirmalā vedadhīr bhavet ||
SNA4ab nirmūlair api vijñānair dṛṣṭārtheṣu bhaved gatiḥ
SNA4cd śrutimātrāśrayatvāt tu dharmo dauḥsthityam āśritaḥ ||
SNA5ab anādivyavahāratvam ādimad vastusaṃśrayam
SNA5cd pratyākhyeyam, ghaṭatvādijātau vyaktibhramo hi saḥ ||
SNA6ab sthite kūṭasthanityatve vyavahārasya nityatā
SNA6cd kūṭasthena vinaitena na tasyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
SNA7ab prasiddhatvād ṛte sarvo vyavahāro hi neṣyate
SNA7cd tasmād vedapramāṇārthaṃ nityatvam iha sādhyate ||
SNA8ab parasparāvinābhāvād anityakṛtakatvayoḥ
SNA8cd kāraṇaṃ dvayasiddhyarthaṃ kiñ cit kasya cid ucyate ||
SNA9ab nānādeśāvagamyatvād yugapat tulyabuddhibhiḥ
SNA9cd asmābhiḥ, kṛtakaḥ śabdo bhaved akṣaralekhyavat ||
SNA10ab yaugapadyopalambhād vā bhedo bhedāc ca kāryatā
SNA10cd avibhutve hi yugapannaiko nānāvagamyate ||
SNA11ab kārtyena cāvagamyatvād ekadeśe ghaṭādivat
SNA11cd śabdasyāvibhūtā tasmād anyatāsya mukhāntare ||
SNA12ab ekaḥ sann ekadeśastho yadaikena prayujyate
SNA12cd tadā vaktrantare na syād ekavaktṛmukhādivat ||
SNA13ab kāryatve syāt kriyābhedāt phalabhedaḥ pratikriyam
SNA13cd tenaikabuddhiḥ sādṛśyāt sphuṭe 'nyatve 'vakalpate ||
SNA14ab nityatve tv ekabuddheḥ syān na kiñ cid bhrāntikāraṇam
SNA14cd kāmaṃ deśā iti nyāyāt tac caikatvaṃ viruddhyate ||
SNA15ab na ca vyañjakabhedena deśabhedopalambhanam
SNA15cd pradīpair bhinnadeśasthair na bhinno vyajyate ghaṭaḥ ||
SNA16ab vyomānavayavaṃ caiṣāṃ dhvanīnām āśrayo matam
SNA16cd savyaṅgyānām ataḥ sarvair vyaktir ekatra te bhavet ||
SNA17ab vastvantaravikāryatvāt smṛtisādṛśyasādhitāt
SNA17cd ikārāder anityatvaṃ dadhikṣīraguḍādivat ||
SNA18ab hetuvṛddhyanusāritvāt kāryatāsya ghaṭādivat
SNA18cd na hi dīpasahasre 'pi vyañjake varddhate ghaṭaḥ ||
SNA19ab anaikāntikatā tāvaddhetūnām iha kathyate
SNA19cd prayatnānantarā dṛṣṭir nitye 'pi na viruddhyate ||
SNA20ab tasmāt tatraiva dṛṣṭatvād anyatrādṛṣṭakalpanā
SNA20cd prāgūrdhvānupalabdho ced dhetutvena vivakṣite ||
SNA21ab jātyaulūkyasya, sāṃkhyasya caitanyenātmavartinā
SNA21cd śākyasyāpi tv anaikāntaḥ kṣaṇikavyatirekibhiḥ ||
SNA22ab pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyānirodhavyom abhistribhiḥ
SNA22cd buddhipūrvaṃ vināśe hi pratisaṃkhyānirodhadhīḥ ||
SNA23ab abuddhipūrvakas teṣāṃ nirodho 'pratisaṃkhyayā
SNA23cd tau ca dvāv apy anāśitvād iṣṭāvakṛtakāv api ||
SNA24ab āhuḥ svabhāvasiddhaṃ hi te vināśam ahetukam
SNA24cd hetur yasya vināśo 'pi tasya dṛṣṭo 'ṅkurādivat ||
SNA25ab vināśasya vināśas tu nāsti tasmād akṛtrimaḥ
SNA25cd bhavati hy agnisambandhāt kāṣṭād aṅgārasantatiḥ ||
SNA26ab mudgarādihatāc cāpi kapālaṃ jāyatte ghaṭāt
SNA26cd svābhāviko vināśas tu jātamātrapratiṣṭitaḥ ||
SNA27ab sūkṣmaḥ sadṛśasantānadṛtter anupalakṣitaḥ
SNA27cd yadā vilakṣaṇo hetuḥ patet sadṛśasantatau ||
SNA28ab vilakṣaṇena kāryeṇa sthūlo 'bhivyajyate tadā 
SNA28cd tenāsadṛśasantāno hetoḥ sañjāyate yataḥ ||
SNA29ab tenaivākriyamāṇo 'pi nāśo 'bhivyajyate sphūṭaḥ
SNA29cd sa mudgaraprahārādiprayatnānantarīyakaḥ ||
SNA30ab yasmād akṛtako dṛṣṭo, hetuḥ syād vyabhicāryataḥ
SNA30cd ākāśam api nityaṃ sad yadā bhūmijalāvṛtam ||
SNA31ab vyajyate tadapohena svananotsecanādibhiḥ
SNA31cd prayatnānantaraṃ jñānaṃ tadā tatrāpi dṛśyate ||
SNA32ab tenānaikāntiko hetur yaduktaṃ tatra darśanāt
SNA32cd atha sthagitam apy etad asty evety anumīyate ||
SNA33ab tirohitānabhivyakteḥ śabdabuddhiprabandhavat
SNA33cd śabdasyaivānavasthānād iti hetuṃ vaded yadi ||
SNA34ab asthānād ity ayaṃ hetus tadānaikāntiko bhavet
SNA34cd ākāśadhīprabandho hi tadā tasmin na tiṣṭati ||
SNA35ab tirohitānabhivyakteḥ śabdabuddhiprabandhavat
SNA35cd śabdasyaivānavasthanād iti hetuṃ vaded yadi ||
SNA36ab asiddha eva vaktavyas tato 'bhivyaktivādinā
SNA36cd tadvyāpārakṛtatve 'pi vyaṅgyair mūlodakādibhiḥ ||
SNA37ab kutakatve 'pī teṣāṃ hi notpattiḥ khananādinā
SNA37cd na cāccāraṇato 'nyāsti śabdasyotpādikā kriyā ||
SNA38ab nibandharyasatīty evaṃ viśiṣṭe 'pi, tathaiva naḥ
SNA38cd abandhāḥ syur yaditeṣām abodho hetvabhāvataḥ ||
SNA39ab vyañjakābhāvataḥ śabde 'py abodho badhirādivat
SNA39cd tasyaiva vā nibandhṛtve bhaved dhetor asiddhatā ||
SNA40ab atha pūrvāparāsattvaṃ hitus tatrāpy asiddhatā
SNA40cd sann eva sādhānābhāvāc chabdo naivopalabhyate ||
SNA41ab kṣaṇikaṃ sādhanaṃ cāsya buddhir apy anuvartate
SNA41cd meghāndhakāraśarvaryā vidyujjanitadṛṣṭivat ||
SNA42ab yathā ghaṭāder dīpādir abhivyañjaka iṣyate
SNA42cd cakṣuṣo'nugrahād evaṃ dhvaniḥ syāc chrītrasaṃskṛteḥ ||
SNA43ab na ca paryanuyogo 'tra kenākāreṇa saṃskṛtiḥ
SNA43cd utpattāv api tulyatvāc chaktis tatrāpy atīndriyā ||
SNA44ab nityaṃ kāryānumeyā ca śaktiḥ kim anuyujyate
SNA44cd tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ pramāṇaṃ tatra gamyate ||
SNA45ab ato 'tīndriyayaivete śaktyā śaktim atīndriyām
SNA45cd indriyasyādadhānāḥ syuḥ śabdābhivyaktihetavaḥ ||
SNA46ab vyñjako nānyajātiś cet, śrotraṃ śabdsya te katham
SNA46cd pārthivānāṃ ghaṭādīnāṃ pradopādiś ca taijasaḥ ||
SNA47ab ātmādisamprayoge ca kāryaiḥ syāt tulyajātitā
SNA47cd jātir yā kā cid iṣṭā cet sā no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
SNA48ab upalabdhinimittāc ca nānyad vyañjakam ucyate
SNA48cd tasmād yathopalabdhatvāt sa jātivyañjako bhavet ||
SNA49ab tathā tadavinābhāvād vijātīyo bhaviṣyati
SNA49cd vāyavīyānabhijñatvāt tālvādisthābhimānataḥ ||
SNA50ab anabhivyañjakatvārtham āhoparatayor api
SNA50cd vāyavīradhiyaivoktaṃ na nūnam iti cottaram ||
SNA51ab abhighātavacas taḥ prāgevaṃ gūḍhadhiyāvubhau
SNA51cd yadi śabdam itīhāpi tredhābhivyaktisambhavaḥ ||
SNA52ab sā hi syāc chabdasaṃskārādindriyasyobhayasya vā
SNA52cd tatra sarvaiḥ pratīyeta śabdaḥ saṃskriyate yadi ||
SNA53ab nirbhāgasya vibhor na syād ekadeśe hi saṃskriyā
SNA53cd na cāsyādhārabhedena saṃskāraniyamo bhavet ||
SNA54ab yataḥ śabdo nirādhāro vyomātmādivad eva ca
SNA54cd athāpy ākāśam ādhāras tatrānavayave 'sati ||
SNA55ab na syāt pradeśasaṃskāraḥ, kṛtsnaśabdamater api
SNA55cd na hi sāmastyarūpeṇa yāvad vyoma vyavasthitaḥ ||
SNA56ab śaktyate sakalo boddhum ekadeśena saṃskṛtaḥ
SNA56cd ākāśaśrotrapakṣe ca vibhutvāt prāptitulyatā ||
SNA57ab dūrabhāve 'pi śabdānām iti jñānaṃ prasajyate 
SNA57cd śrotrasya caivam ekatvaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ bhavet ||
SNA58ab tenaikaśrutivelāyāṃ śṛṇuyuḥ sarva eva te
SNA58cd tasyānavayavatvāc ca na dharmādharmasaṃskṛtaḥ ||
SNA59ab nabhodeśo bhavec chrotraṃ vyavasthādvayasiddhayate
SNA59cd vaiśeṣikādisiddhānteṣv evaṃ tāvat prasajyate ||
SNA60ab kāpile 'pi vibhutvena śrotrāder iyam eva dik
SNA60cd sakṛc ca saṃskṛtaṃ śrotraṃ sarvaśabdān prabodhayet ||
SNA61ab ghaṭāyonmīlitaṃ cakṣuḥ paṭaṃ na hi na budhyate
SNA61cd etad eva prasaṅktavyaṃ viṣayasyāpi saṃskṛtau ||
SNA62ab samānadeśavartitvāt saṃskāro 'py aviśeṣataḥ
SNA62cd sthiravāyvapanītyā ca saṃskāro 'sya bhavan bhavet ||
SNA63ab dṛṣṭaṃ vāvaraṇāpāye taddeśānyopalambhanam
SNA63cd saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtatve ca śabdaikatve na siddhyataḥ ||
SNA64ab ekāvasthābhyupeto vā sarvair jñāyeta vā na vā
SNA64cd pratyekābhihitā doṣāḥ syur dvayor api saṃskṛtau ||
SNA65ab tena prādeśikaṃ jñānaṃ na kṛtatvād vinā bhaved
SNA65cd uttaraṃ śrotrasaṃskārād bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam ||
SNA66ab tadbhedāt śrutibhedaś ca pratiśrotṛ vyavasthitaḥ
SNA66cd nāvaśyaṃ śrotram ākāśam asmābhiś cābhyupeyate ||
SNA67ab na cānavayavaṃ vyoma jainasāṃkhyaniṣedhataḥ
SNA67cd tenākāśaikadeśo vā yad vā vastvantaraṃ bhavet ||
SNA68ab kāryārthāpattigamyaṃ na ḥ śrotraṃ pratinaraṃ sthiram
SNA68cd yady api vyāpi caikaṃ ca tathāpi dhvanisaṃskṛtiḥ ||
SNA69ab adhiṣṭhāneṣu sā yasya tacchabdaṃ pratipatsyate
SNA69cd athāpīndriyasaṃskāraḥ so 'py adhiṣṭhānadeśataḥ ||
SNA70ab śabdaṃ na śroṣyati śrotraṃ tenāsaṃskṛtaśaṣkuli
SNA70cd aprāptakarṇadeśatvād dhvaner na śrotrasaṃskriyā ||
SNA71ab ato 'dhiṣṭhānabhedena saṃskāraniyamasthitiḥ
SNA71cd nanv ekasminn adhiṣṭhāne labdhasaṃskāram indriyam ||
SNA72ab bodhakaṃ sarvadeheṣu syād ekendriyavādinaḥ
SNA72cd puṃsā dehapradeśeṣu vijñānotpattir iṣyate ||
SNA73ab tena pradhānavaideśyād viguṇā sā tu saṃskṛtiḥ
SNA73cd niṣpradeśo 'pi cātmā naḥ kārtsnyena ca vidann api ||
SNA74ab śarīra eva gṛhṇātīty evam ukte na dṛṣyati
SNA74cd ekatve 'pi yathākāśaṃ dravyaiḥ sāvayavaiḥ pṛthak ||
SNA75ab saṃsargabhedaṃ labhate saṃskārāsaṃskṛto tathā
SNA75cd vyomno 'navayavavyāptisadbhāve 'pi bhuviṣṭhitān ||
SNA76ab dvyāśrayatvaṃ na saṃsargo ghaṭādīnanurudhyate
SNA76cd bādhiryādivyavasthānam anenaiva ca hetunā ||
SNA77ab tadevābhogyam anyasya dharmādharmavaśīkṛtam
SNA77cd yathā tatra vasann eva svāmitvād avaropitaḥ ||
SNA78ab na bhogaṃ labhate tadvadbadhiro 'nyatra śṛṇvati
SNA78cd śrotraśabdāśrayāṇāṃ ca na nāmāvayavāḥ svayam ||
SNA79ab na caikadeśavṛttitvaṃ tathāpy etan na duṣyati
SNA79cd vyañjakānāṃ hi vāyūnāṃ bhinnāvayavadeśatā ||
SNA80ab jātibhedaś ca tenaiva saṃskāro vyavatiṣṭhate
SNA80cd anyārthaṃ prerito vāyur yathā'nyaṃ na karotivaḥ ||
SNA81ab tathānyavarṇaṃ saṃskāraśakto nānyaṃ kariṣyati
SNA81cd anyais tālvādisaṃyogair varṇo nānyo yathaiva te ||
SNA82ab tathā dhvanyantarākṣepo na dhvanyantarasāribhiḥ
SNA82cd tasmād utpattyabhivyaktyoḥ kāryārthāpattitaḥ samaḥ ||
SNA83ab sāmarthyabhedaḥ sarvatra, syāt prayatnavivakṣayoḥ
SNA83cd viṣayasyāpi saṃskāre tenaikasyaiva saṃskṛtiḥ ||
SNA84ab naraiḥ sāmarthyabhedāc ca na sarvair avagamyate
SNA84cd yathaivotpadyamāno 'yaṃ na sarvair avagamyate ||
SNA85ab digdeśādivibhāgena sarvān prati bhavann api
SNA85cd tathaiva yatsamīpasthair nādaiḥ syād yasya saṃskṛtiḥ ||
SNA86ab tair eva śrūyate śabdo na dūrasthaiḥ kathañ cana 
SNA86cd dvayasaṃskārapakṣe tu mṛṣā doṣadvaye vacaḥ ||
SNA87ab yenānyataravaikalyāt sarvaiḥ sarvo na gṛhyate
SNA87cd sarvalokaprasiddhāṃ ca vivakṣānusṛtāṃ śrutim ||
SNA88ab anugacchadibhir ekāntāt kāryo mārgaḥ parokṣakaiḥ
SNA88cd tatra ye tāvad icchanti prāksaṃyogavibhāgataḥ ||
SNA89ab śabda utpadyate tasmād anyas tatsadṛśaḥ punaḥ
SNA89cd tadanantaradeśe 'nyas tādṛganyas tataḥ paraḥ ||
SNA90ab vīcītaraṅgavṛttyaivam antyaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate
SNA90cd adṛṣṭakalpanā tasmin pakṣe bahvī prasajyate ||
SNA91ab śabdabhede na tāvan naḥ prajñābhedaḥ pravarttate
SNA91cd ārambhakatvaṃ śabdasya niṣkriyasyāpramāṇakam ||
SNA92ab deśāntaragataṃ kārya nāmūrtasyābhighnataḥ
SNA92cd deśeyattānimittaṃ ca nārambhaniyamaṃ prati ||
SNA93ab na ca diṅniyame hetur anuvātagates tathā
SNA93cd sadṛśaṃ vā sajātiṃ vā karotīti ca duṣkaram ||
SNA94ab ārambhasarvadikkatve na ca hetuḥ pratīyate
SNA94cd niranvayair vinaśyadbhir na cātyantāsatāṃ kriyā ||
SNA95ab jñānasantānavaccaiṣāṃ santāno nāvakalpate
SNA95cd vegavatsakriyatvābhyāṃ taraṅgāṇāṃ tu yujyate ||
SNA96ab kāryadeśāntarārambho yāvadvegaṃ ca tatkriyā
SNA96cd ārambhapratibandho 'sya na ca kuḍyādibhibhaṃvet ||
SNA97ab na hy asūrttasya sadbhāvo sūrtamadhye vihanyate
SNA97cd na ca kuḍyādibhir vyoma nāśyate sāryate 'pi vā ||
SNA98ab na tirodhīyate tasmāt kuḍyamadhye 'pi tad dhruvam
SNA98cd ākāśaṃ tatra na syāc cet kuḍyasthānaṃ virudhyate ||
SNA99ab tan madhyāvayavānāṃ ca, na hi tiṣṭhati te ghane
SNA99cd athāvṛtyātmakadravyasaṃyogarahitaṃ nabhaḥ ||
SNA100ab śabdotpādaṃ bibhartīti tatra nyāyo na kaś cana
SNA100cd anyathāpy upapannatvāt nārthāpattyaitad iṣyate ||
SNA101ab na pramāṇāntaraṃ ceyaṃ pramāṇadvayavādinām
SNA101cd sambandhānupalabdheś ca nānumānena kalpanā ||
SNA102ab brṛyāt sāmānyadṛṣṭaṃ ced, bhaved dhetor viruddhatā
SNA102cd sajātīyakaraḥ śabdo guṇatvāc cendriyādivat ||
SNA103ab aśabdārambhakas tadvat syād adeśāntare tathā
SNA103cd yatra hy avayavā deśe paṭādīnāṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
SNA104ab tatraiva tadguṇāḥ sarve tadārabdho 'vayavy api
SNA104cd tadguṇāś cāpi taddeśās tenaiṣām ekadeśatā ||
SNA105ab tadvadādyā pṛthagdeśāḥ śabdāḥ sarve bhavanti hi
SNA105cd śabdaṃ nārabhate śabdaḥ śabdatvād antyaśabdavat ||
SNA106ab evaṃ vibhāgasaṃyogau tadbhāvād antyayogavat
SNA106cd jainakāpilanirdiṣṭaṃ śabdaśrotrādisarpaṇam ||
SNA107ab sādhīyo 'smāt, tad apy atra yuktyā naivāvatiṣṭhate
SNA107cd śabdasyāgamanaṃ tāvad adṛṣṭaṃ parikalpitam ||
SNA108ab mūrtisparśādimattvaṃ ca teṣām abhibhavaḥ satām
SNA108cd tvagagrāhyatvam anye ca bhāgāḥ sūkṣmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||
SNA109ab teṣām adṛśyamānānāṃ kathaṃ ca racanākramaḥ
SNA109cd kīdṛśād racanābhedād varṇabhedaś ca jāyate ||
SNA110ab dravatvena vinā caiṣāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ kathyate katham
SNA110cd āgacchatāṃ ca viśleṣo na bhaved vāyunā katham ||
SNA111ab laghavo 'vayavā hy ete nibaddhā na ca kena cit
SNA111cd vṛkṣādyabhihatānāṃ ca viśleṣo loṣṭavad bhavet ||
SNA112ab ekaśrotrapraveśe ca nānyeṣāṃ syāt punaḥ śrutiḥ
SNA112cd na cāvāntaravarṇānāṃ nānātvasyāsti kāraṇam ||
SNA113ab na caikasyaiva sarvāsu gamanaṃ dikṣu yujyate
SNA113cd śrotrāgamanapakṣe ca, tan na, vṛttiś ca gacchati ||
SNA114ab tadadṛṣṭadvayaṃ tasya, dūrasthena ca vikriyā
SNA114cd prāptiḥ sarvagatatvāc cet, tulyā dūragateṣv api ||
SNA115ab vikriyāvikriye tatra sarvaiḥ syātāṃ na bhedataḥ 
SNA115cd asambaddhavikāritvam apīṣṭaṃ tatra pūrvavat ||
SNA116ab asambandhasamānatve nāsanno hi viśiṣyate
SNA116cd amūrtā śrotravṛttiś ca na mūrtena vihanyate ||
SNA117ab tatra vyavahitaḥ śabdaḥ kimarthaṃ nopalabhyate
SNA117cd śrtotrasya vikriyāyāṃ ca neyattāyā niyāmakam ||
SNA118ab nānuvātādibhis tasya vṛtteś ca preraṇaṃ bhavet
SNA118cd anuvātaṃ vihanyeta, prativātaṃ ca sā vrajet ||
SNA119ab tadgataṃ hy anuvātatvaṃ syān na śabdagataṃ tadā
SNA119cd yeṣāṃ tv aprāpta evāyaṃ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate ||
SNA120ab teṣām aprāptitulyatvaṃ dūravyavahitādiṣu
SNA120cd tatra dūrasamīpasthagrahaṇāgrahaṇe same ||
SNA121ab syātāṃ na ca kramo nāpi tīvramandādisambhavaḥ
SNA121cd tasmāc chrotriyadṛṣṭāpi kalpaneyaṃ parīkṣyatām ||
SNA122ab prayatnābhihato vāyuḥ koṣṭhyo yātītyasaṃśayam
SNA122cd sa saṃyogavibhāgau ca tālvāder anurudhyate ||
SNA123ab vegavattvāc ca so 'vaśyaṃ yāvad vegaṃ pratiṣṭhate
SNA123cd tasyātmavayavānāṃ ca stimitena ca vāyunā ||
SNA124ab saṃyogā viprayogāś ca jāyante gamanād dhruvam
SNA124cd karṇavyomani sa prāptaḥ śaktiṃ śrotre niyacchati ||
SNA125ab tadbhāve śabdabodhāc ca saṃskāro 'dṛṣṭa iṣyate
SNA125cd utpattiśaktivat so 'pīty adhikaṃ no na kiñ cana ||
SNA126ab tathaiva tadviśeṣo 'pi viśiṣṭagrahaṇād bhavet
SNA126cd śabdotpatter niṣiddhatvād anyathānupapattitaḥ ||
SNA127ab viśiṣṭasaṃskṛter janma dhvanibhyo 'dhyavasīyate
SNA127cd tadbhāvabhāvitā cātra śaktyastitvā'vavodhinī ||
SNA128ab śrotraśaktivad eveṣṭā, buddhis tatra hi saṃhṛtā
SNA128cd kuḍyādipratibandho 'pi yujyate mātariśvanaḥ ||
SNA129ab śrotradeśābhighāte 'pi tena tīvrapravartinā
SNA129cd tasya ca kramavartitvāt kṣayi vegātmasaṃpadaḥ ||
SNA130ab saṃskārakramatīvratvamandatādinimittatā
SNA130cd imam eva ca saṃskāraṃ śabdagrahaṇakāraṇam ||
SNA131ab ke cit tu paṇḍitam manyāḥ śrotram ity abhimanvate
SNA131cd saṃjñāsañcāraṇāc caiṣāṃ bahumānaḥ svacetasi ||
SNA132ab mudhaiṣāṃ bahumāno 'yaṃ vastvanutpādya kiñ cana
SNA132cd dhvanijanyād dhi saṃskārāc chrotraṃ nānyat pradarśitam ||
SNA133ab taṃ muktvā śrotraśabdena kiṃ dṛṣṭam adhikaṃ ca taiḥ
SNA133cd evañ jātīyakān arthān phalena pratipāditān ||
SNA134ab lokaḥ saṃskāraśabdena sāmānyenaiva jalpati
SNA134cd śrotraśabdo viśeṣeṇa tatrāvijñātasaṅgatiḥ ||
SNA135ab siddhaṃ svārthaṃ parityajya nābhidhānena vartate
SNA135cd ādāvaparibhāṣyatvaṃ bhāṣyakāro yadabravīt ||
SNA136ab padārtheṣu bhavet teṣāṃ tadatikramaṇaṃ phalam
SNA136cd saṃskāravyatirikte ca sarvalokasya vastuni ||
SNA137ab śrotraśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ san svāc chandyenāpanīyate
SNA137cd indriyāṇām abhivyaktir garbhasthasyaiva dehinaḥ ||
SNA138ab prākkāryād āgamaiḥ siddhā tatpradveṣeṇa laṅghyate
SNA138cd na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ kartuṃ yogyaḥ kathañ cana ||
SNA139ab kṣaṇikaśrotrapakṣe ca so 'vaśyaṃ kṛtako bhavet
SNA139cd saṃskāre tulyam etac cet, na saṃskārāntarasthiteḥ ||
SNA140ab saṃskāraśabdavācyā hi ke cid varṣaśatāny api
SNA140cd dhriyante tena tacchabdasambandho na vinaśyati ||
SNA141ab śrotraśabdaḥ punaḥ pūrva saṃskārād uttaratra tu
SNA141cd ekadeśanibaddhe hi sarvadārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ ||
SNA142ab śakyaṃ ca ghriyamāṇatvam indriyatvāt tvagāditvat
SNA142cd vaktuṃ śrotrasya tenātra kṣaṇikotpattyasambhavaḥ ||
SNA143ab yadi ca dhvanisasamparkāc chrotram evopajāyate
SNA143cd badhirasyāpi tajjanma kimarthaṃ nopalabhyate ||
SNA144ab yad yasya nāsti tat tasya sutarāṃ jananakṣamam 
SNA144cd tasmād apekṣitaṃ śrotraṃ badhirasyāpi jāyatām ||
SNA145ab saṃskāre 'py aviśiṣṭaṃ cet, nāsāv upahatendriye
SNA145cd śrotramācchāditaṃ doṣaiḥ saṃskartuṃ dhvanayo 'kṣamāḥ ||
SNA146ab utpadyamānapakṣe tu na kiñ cit pratibandhanam
SNA146cd śrotram ākāśadeśaṃ ca bhautikendriyavādinaḥ ||
SNA147ab yamāhus tasya sadbhāvaḥ prāgdhvaneḥ kena vāryate
SNA147cd siddhasya ca padārthasya yānyataḥ kāryaṃ yogyatā ||
SNA148ab saṃskāraśabdavācyatvāt sā yuktyā vāryate kayā
SNA148cd lokāgamaprasiddheṣu padārtheṣv anyathā vacaḥ ||
SNA149ab tanmudhākhedakāri syād goviṣāṇāśanopamam
SNA149cd yadi tv avaśyaṃ kartavyastārkikoktiviparyayaḥ ||
SNA150ab tato vedānusāreṇa kāryā dikśrotratāmatiḥ
SNA150cd diśaḥ śrotram iti hy etat pralayeṣv abhidhīyate ||
SNA151ab tac ca prakṛtigāmitvavacanaṃ cakṣurādivat
SNA151cd sūryam asya tathā cakṣuruktaṃ gamayatād iti ||
SNA152ab tejaḥ prakṛtivijñānaṃ tathā śrotraṃ digātmakam
SNA152cd dik ca sarvaṃgataukā ca yāvad vyoma vyavasthitā ||
SNA153ab karṇacchidraparicchannā śrtotram ākāśadeśavat
SNA153cd yāvāṃś ca kaṇabhugnyāyo nabhobhāgaprakalpane ||
SNA154ab digbhāge tu samasto 'sau, āgamāt tu viśiṣyate
SNA154cd tasmād digdravyabhāgo yaḥ puṇyāpuṇyavaśīkṛtaḥ ||
SNA155ab karṇacchidraparicchinnaḥ śrotraṃ saṃskriyate ca saḥ
SNA155cd tasmāt svato 'navasthānaṃ parastādity asiddhatā ||
SNA156ab pratyayasyānavasthānaṃ vyomny api sthagite 'sti naḥ
SNA156cd na ca tasmin vināśitvaṃ dravye 'dravyātmake sati ||
SNA157ab tatrānumānabuddhiś cet, śabde 'py astīti gamyatām
SNA157cd karoter yac ca karmatvāt kṛtakatvam udāhṛtam ||
SNA158ab arthas tāvadasiddho 'yam abhidhānam athocyate
SNA158cd tatrāpi vyabhicāritvaṃ tatkriyājanmavādinaḥ ||
SNA159ab gomayādāvatajjanye 'py eṣa śabdo hi dṛśyate
SNA159cd yathā kathañ cid iṣṭaṃ cet kāryatvaṃ gomayādiṣu ||
SNA160ab tathāpy ākāśamātratvaṃ kuruṣv ety atra dṛśyate
SNA160cd varaṇābhāvamātratvāt kāryam eveti cet, na tat ||
